        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
           
           
            viewSummary.PopupMenuShowing += ViewSummary_PopupMenuShowing;
            viewSummary.OptionsView.ShowFilterPanelMode = ShowFilterPanelMode.Never;


            

            if (null == _bbg)
                _bbg = new UtilsLib.BBGDDE();

            _bwicdetail = new GridHelper(gridDetail, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _summary = new GridHelper(grdSummary, server, false, _bat_signal);

            ctrlLegend.Init(_server);
            viewDetail.PopupMenuShowing += ViewDetail_PopupMenuShowing;
            ctrlBWICFilter1.SetFilterUpdate(_summary.UpdateFilter);
           
           bool hide = true;
           
           
           
           
           lblSuggestedAccounts.Visible = hide;
           listSuggestedAccounts.Visible = hide;
            
            default_bid_account = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingle<int>(_server, 3, true);
        }

        public void Divide1MM(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            AdjustOface(1 / 1000000.0);
        }

        public void DivideThousand(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            AdjustOface(1/1000.0);
        }

        public void Mult1MM(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            AdjustOface(1000000.0);
        }

        public void MultThousand(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            AdjustOface(1000.0);
        }

        private void AdjustOface(double mult)
        {
            int bwic_id = _summary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("bwic_id");
            BatCaveLib.BWICs.AdjustOface(_server, bwic_id, mult);
            RefreshCurrentBWICS(bwic_id);
           
        }



        private void ViewDetail_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem sub = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("BBG Blast Selected Bonds");
                sub.BeginGroup = true;
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem single = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("BWIC", this.BlastSingleBondsBWIC);
                sub.Items.Add(single);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem px_talk = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("PX Talk", this.BlastSingleBondsPxTalk);
                sub.Items.Add(px_talk);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem bids = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Bids", this.BlastSingleBondsBids);
                sub.Items.Add(bids);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem results = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Results", this.BlastSingleBondsResults);
                sub.Items.Add(results);

                menu.Items.Add(sub);
            }
        }

        private void ViewSummary_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {

            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                menu.Items.Clear();

                bool can_edit = false;
                if(viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount == 1)
                    can_edit = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("can_edit");


                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem menu_item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Create BWIC", this.CreateNewBWIC);
                menu.Items.Add(menu_item);


                if (can_edit)
                {
                    DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu manage = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem manage_item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Managed Selected BWIC", this.ManageBWIC);
                    int which = menu.Items.Add(manage_item);


                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem adjust_ofaces = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("Adjust OFACE");

                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem div1mm = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Divide 1MM",this.Divide1MM);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem div1m = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Divide 1M", this.DivideThousand);

                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem mult1mm = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Multiply 1MM", this.Mult1MM);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem mult1m= new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Multiply 1M", this.Mult1MM);
                    mult1mm.BeginGroup = true;
                    adjust_ofaces.Items.Add(div1mm);
                    adjust_ofaces.Items.Add(div1m);
                    adjust_ofaces.Items.Add(mult1mm);
                    adjust_ofaces.Items.Add(mult1m);
                    menu.Items.Add(adjust_ofaces);
                }

                
                
                
                
                
                


                
                
                
                
                
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem my_color = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Selected BWIC(s) - My Color Only", this.DisplayMyColor);
                my_color.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(my_color);




                string message = String.Format("Blast Selected BWIC{0}", viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount > 1 ? "s" : "");
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem bwic = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(message, this.BlastSelectedBWICs);
                bwic.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(bwic);

                string messaget = String.Format("Blast Selected BWIC{0} w/Talk", viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount > 1 ? "s" : "");
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem bwict = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(messaget, this.BlastSelectedBWICsTalk);
                menu.Items.Add(bwict);

                string messageb = String.Format("Blast Selected BWIC{0} w/Bids", viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount > 1 ? "s" : "");
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem bwicb = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(messageb, this.BlastSelectedBWICBids);
                menu.Items.Add(bwicb);

                string messager = String.Format("Blast Selected BWIC{0} w/Results", viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount > 1 ? "s" : "");
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem bwicr = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(messager, this.btnBlastResults_Click);
                menu.Items.Add(bwicr);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem tickers_only = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Selected BWIC(s) - Copy Tickers Only", this.CopyTickersOnly);
                tickers_only.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(tickers_only);
            }
        }

        public void CoveredHolders(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<int> ids = viewSummary.GetFilteredData<int>("bwic_id");
            CoveredHolders(ids);
        }

        public void DisplayMyColor(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<int> ids = viewSummary.GetActiveRowList<int>("bwic_id",true);
            DXHelper.LongForms.DisplayMyColorInternal(_server, ids, chkIncludeBDHolders.Checked,chkNAICTrades.Checked,_bat_signal);
        }
        public void CopyTickersOnly(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<int> ids = viewSummary.GetActiveRowList<int>("bwic_id", true);
            string msg = "";
            foreach (int i in ids)
            {
                List<string> tickers = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetUniqueBWICTickers(_server, i);
                
                string list = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, tickers);
                msg += list + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;
            }

            System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(msg);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Copied to clipboard!");
            
        }

        private void CoveredMatchers(List<int> bwic_ids)
        {
            Query q = new Query("UpcomingCoveredMatchers.sql", _server);
            q.AddParameter("@bwic_id", bwic_ids);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            SpawnInternalReport(tbl);
        }


        private void SpawnInternalReport(DataTable tbl)
        {
            DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView();
            f.Init(_server,_bat_signal);
            
            f.Populate(tbl, null);
            
            f.SetFormat("bid_time", "M/d h:mm tt");
            f.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);
            f.ShowDialog();
        }

        private void CoveredHolders(List<int> bwic_ids)
        {
            Query q = new Query("UpcomingCoveredHolders.sql", _server);
            q.AddParameter("@bwic_id", bwic_ids);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView();
            f.Init(_server,_bat_signal);
            
            f.Populate(tbl, null);
            
            f.SetFormat("bid_time", "M/d h:mm tt");
            f.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);
            f.ShowDialog();
        }

        public void BlastSelectedBWICs(object sender, EventArgs e)

            BWICBlastHelper.BlastSelectedBWICS(_server, ids,BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC,null,f,blast_indirects,all,_bbg,bt);
        }

        {

            List<string> tickers = viewDetail.GetActiveRowList<string>("ticker", true);

            DataTable all = ((DataView)viewSummary.DataSource).ToTable();
            BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt = BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.GetBlastTemplate(drpBlastFormat.EditValue.ToString());
            BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT f = GetBBGMSGFormat(chkCopyToClipboard.Checked, chkIB.Checked && chkIB.Visible);
            BWICBlastHelper.BlastSelectedBWICS(_server, ids, bf, tickers, f, blast_indirects,all, _bbg, bt);
        }

        public void CreateManageBWIC(Nullable<int> bwic_id)

            frm.Close();

        }


        public Nullable<int> GetNextBWIC(DataTable bwics)
        {
            bwics.AsDataView().Sort = "bid_time desc";
            foreach (DataRow row in bwics.DefaultView.AsDataTable().Rows)
            {
                DateTime bid_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["bid_time"]);
                if (bid_time > DateTime.Now)
                    return System.Convert.ToInt32(row["bwic_id"]);
            }
            return null;
        }

        


        private Nullable<int> _last_selected_bwic = null;
        private bool _loading_summary = false;
        public void RefreshCurrentBWICS(Nullable<int> bwic_id)
        {
            _bwicdetail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            _loading_summary = true;
            

            double days_back = .5;
            if (null != dtHistoricalBWICs.EditValue)
                days_back = (DateTime.Now - dtHistoricalBWICs.DateTime).TotalDays;

            
            DataTable summary = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetBWICSummary(_server,days_back);
            SortedDictionary<string,string> prods = BatCaveLib.Products.ProcessProducts(summary,"products");
            
            if(!_loaded_once)
            {
                List<string> prod_names = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(_server,true);
                ctrlBWICFilter1.SetPreferred(prod_names);
            }
            ctrlBWICFilter1.PopulateBoxes(prods);

            if (null == bwic_id)
                bwic_id = GetNextBWIC(summary);

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            string pre_filter_string = viewSummary.ActiveFilterString;
            
            _summary.SetGrid(summary, "#_bonds,bid_time,oface,cface,account,products,list_name,indirect,talk,results", null, null, false, null,false);
            

            
            viewSummary.SetColumnVisible(new string[] { "#_bonds", "bid_time", "oface", "cface", "account", "products", "list_name", "indirect", "talk", "results" }, true);
            

            grdSummary.SetFormat("bid_time", "M/d h:mm tt");
            grdSummary.SetFormat("oface", "0.000");
            grdSummary.SetFormat("cface", "0.000");
            viewSummary.BestFitColumns();
            
            grdSummary.SetWidth("indirect", 60);
            grdSummary.SetWidth("talk", 35);
            grdSummary.SetWidth("results", 50);
            



            
            btnAddColor.Checked = false;
            _loading_summary = false;
            int selected_bwic = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("bwic_id");
            viewSummary.SelectRowBasedOnID("bwic_id", bwic_id);

            if (null != bwic_id && selected_bwic == bwic_id)
            {
                PopulateActiveBWICFromSummary(bwic_id.Value);
            }
            

                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
        }


 



        List<string> filter_fields = new List<string>();
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            RefreshTab(true,null);
        }

        private bool _loaded_once = false;
        public void RefreshTab(bool force,Nullable<int> bwic_id)
        {
            if (_loaded_once && !force)
                return;
            if (null != bwic_id)
                _last_selected_bwic = bwic_id;

            PopulateBlastFormats();
            
            

            
            

            RefreshCurrentBWICS(_last_selected_bwic);


            _loaded_once = true;
            
        }

        private void frmBWICs_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            
            PopulateLegend();
        }

        private void PopulateBlastFormats()
        {
            DataTable formats = BWICBlastHelper.GetAllBlastFormats();
            drpBlastFormat.PopulateLookup(formats, "name", "name");
            string default_blast = "Default";
            string user_default_blast = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<string>(_server, 4,true);
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(user_default_blast))
                default_blast = user_default_blast;
            drpBlastFormat.EditValue = default_blast;

        }

        public void PopulateLegend()
        {
            ctrlLegend.Populate("type");
        }

        public void PopulateBWIC(int bwic_id, bool add_color, bool show_bids,string list_type)
        {
            if (_loading_summary)
                return;
            
            DataTable t = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetBWICDetailGrid(_server, bwic_id);
            string format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "bwic",t,"product_id");

            

            List<string> product_types = t.GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_1");

            
            if (!product_types.Contains("UNKNOWN") && product_types.Count == 1)
            {
                format = format.Replace("bond_label_1,", "");
            }
                


            _bwicdetail.SetGrid(t.DataSet, format);
            
            SetupDetailGrid(show_bids, list_type, format);

            if (add_color && t.Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                BWICRefreshHelper bwrh = new BWICRefreshHelper(show_bids, list_type, SetupDetailGrid,format);
                
                _bwicdetail.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, format, false, false, bwrh.Call,true, null, false,false, false, true, true,true);
            }
            
        }


        public class BWICRefreshHelper
        {
            public bool _show_bids = false;
            public string _list_type = null;
            public string _parent_format = null;
            public HelperDel _refresh;
            public delegate void HelperDel(bool show_bids, string list_type,string parent_format);
            public BWICRefreshHelper(bool show_bids, string list_type, HelperDel refresh, string parent_format)
            {
                _show_bids = show_bids;
                _list_type = list_type;
                _refresh = refresh;
                _parent_format = parent_format;
            }

            public void Call()
            {
                if (null != _refresh)
                    _refresh(_show_bids, _list_type, _parent_format);
            }

        }

        public class SuggestedAccountHelper
        {
            public string account_name;
            public double orig;
            public double pct;
            public int count;
        }

        private Dictionary<string, SuggestedAccountHelper> accounts = new Dictionary<string, SuggestedAccountHelper>();

        public void PopulateAccountSuggestions(DataTable accts)
        {
            
            accounts.Clear();
            
            this.Invoke((Action) (() => listSuggestedAccounts.Items.Clear()));
            if (null == accts)
                return;
            int total_count = 0;
            double total_orig = 0;
            foreach (DataRow row in accts.Rows)
            {
                string account = row["account"].ToString();
                bool cover = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["cover"]);
                if(!cover)
                    continue;
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(account))
                {
                    if (!accounts.ContainsKey(account))
                    {
                        var s = new SuggestedAccountHelper();
                        s.account_name = account;
                        
                        accounts.Add(account, s);
                    }

                    var a = accounts[account];

                    a.count++;
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    total_count++;
                }
                
            }

            foreach (var s in accounts.OrderByDescending(n => n.Value.count))
            
            {
                double dbl_pct = (double) s.Value.count / (double) total_count;
                if (dbl_pct < .05)
                {
                    continue;
                }
                string format = $"{dbl_pct:0%} - {s.Value.account_name}";
                
                this.Invoke((Action)(() => listSuggestedAccounts.Items.Add(format)));
            }
        }

        
        private void SetupDetailGrid(bool show_bids,string list_type,string parent_format)
        {
            gridDetail.BeginUpdateSafe();
            viewDetail.CleanColumns(null, parent_format, false);
            if (!show_bids)
            {
                _bwicdetail.HideColumn("bid");
                _bwicdetail.HideColumn("bid_acct");
            }
            else
            {
                DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
                RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
                li.PopulateGridLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id");
                viewDetail.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(gridDetail.MainView().Columns["bid_acct"], li);
                
                    li.Enter += Li_Enter;
            }



            if (null != _bwicdetail?._DataSet.Tables.Contains("Color"))
            {
                PopulateAccountSuggestions(_bwicdetail?._DataSet.Tables["Color"]);
            }
            
            viewDetail.BestFitColumnsSafe();
            viewDetail.SetWidth("ticker", 160);
            viewDetail.SetWidth("bid", 55);
            viewDetail.SetWidth("px_talk", 75);
            viewDetail.SetWidth("cpn_formula", 40);
            
            gridDetail.EndUpdateSafe();
        }

        private void Li_Enter(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            LookUpEdit li = sender as LookUpEdit;
            if(null != default_bid_account)
                li.EditValue = default_bid_account.Value;
            li.ShowPopup();
        }

        public string GetDefaultColorGroupName(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vColorGroups where default_colorgroup = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            string t = q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name");
            return t;
        }
        
        

        public List<double> GetOfaceFromClipboard()
        {
            List<double> bonds = new List<double>();
            foreach(string s in Clipboard.GetText().Split('\n'))
            {
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                    continue;
                Nullable<double> o = UtilsLib.Clean.ConvertOface(s);
                if(null != o)
                    bonds.Add(o.Value);
            }
            return bonds;
        }

        private void viewSummary_DoubleClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            bool cover = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("can_edit");
            bool legacy = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("legacy");

            
            
            
            
            

            if (cover)
            {
                if (legacy)
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Can't edit BWICs created in other system");
                }
                else
                {
                    GridView view = (GridView)sender;

                    Point pt = view.GridControl.PointToClient(Control.MousePosition);

                    DoRowDoubleClick(view, pt, ManageActiveBWIC);
                }
            }

        }

        private delegate void ManageBWICDelegate();
        private static void DoRowDoubleClick(GridView view, Point pt, ManageBWICDelegate mb)
        {
            
            {
                GridHitInfo info = view.CalcHitInfo(pt);

                if (info.InRow || info.InRowCell)
                {
                    DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You're about to edit the selected BWIC", "Just checking...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);

                    if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                    {
                        mb();
                    }

                }
            }
        }

        private void btnAddCusips_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
        }

        public void AddCusips(bool wait)
        {
            bool screen_showing = false;

            if (wait)
            {
                
                screen_showing = true;
            }
            int bwic_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("bwic_id");
            int bond_number = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("#_bonds");

            object oface = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<object>("oface");
            bool cover = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("cover");
            

            if(DBNull.Value == oface && bond_number != 0)
            {
                try
                {
                    List<double> bonds = GetOfaceFromClipboard();
                    if (bonds.Count != viewDetail.RowCount)
                    {
                        XtraMessageBox.Show("# of ofaces doesn't match # of bonds in bwic", "Hey!");
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        List<string> tickers = viewDetail.GetList<string>("ticker_bbg", false);
                        List<int> bwicdetail_id = viewDetail.GetList<int>("bwicdetail_id", false);
                        List<double> ofaces = GetOfaceFromClipboard();
                        
                        for (int i = 0; i != tickers.Count; i++)
                        {
                            BatCaveLib.BWICs.AddSingleBond(_server, bwic_id, tickers[i], ofaces[i], null,null,bwicdetail_id[i],null,null);
                        }

                        bool insert_events= Database.Common.GetGlobal<bool>(_server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.RECORD_EVENTS);
                        
                        if (insert_events)
                        {
                            string summary = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("list_name");
                            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(summary))
                            {
                                List<string> products = viewDetail.GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_1");
                                
                                
                                summary = String.Join(",", products);
                                
                            }
                            DateTime bid_time = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("bid_time");
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            
                            string caption = "New BWIC: {day} @ {time} - " + summary;
                            BatCaveLib.Alerts.InsertAlert(_server, 3, caption, null, null, 1, bwic_id,bid_time);
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    if (wait && screen_showing)
                    {
                        screen_showing = false;
                        
                        XtraMessageBox.Show("Whats in the clipboard:\n" + System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.GetText() + "\n\nERROR: " + n.Message, "oface did not parse correctly");
                    }
                }
            }

            else
            {
                string raw = Clipboard.GetText();
                var bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(_server, raw, '\n',false,true);
                if (bonds.notmatched.Count > 0)
                {
                    DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Load Halted...\n\nCouldn't match: \n\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.notmatched.ToArray()) + "\n\nERROR: " + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.errors.ToArray()), "Bond load halted...", MessageBoxButtons.OK);
                     return;
                }
                foreach (Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper s in bonds.matched_list)
                {
                    
                    BatCaveLib.BWICs.AddSingleBond(_server, bwic_id, s.ticker, null, null, null, null, null, null);
                }
            }
            if (wait && screen_showing)
            {
                screen_showing = false;
                
            }
            
            
            RefreshCurrentBWICS(bwic_id);
           

        }

        }

        
        
            
        



        private List<string> ProductOnFilter(DataTable table,List<int> ids)
        {
            List<string> products = new List<string>();
            foreach(DataRow row in table.Rows)
            {
                string list_type = row["list_type"].ToString();
                int bwic_id = Convert.ToInt32(row["bwic_id"]);

                if (!products.Contains(list_type) && ids.Contains(bwic_id))
                    products.Add(list_type);
            }
            return products;
        }
  
        public string ParseCriteria(string filter)
        {
            if (filter.Contains("[list_type] In"))
                return "MIXED";
            string clean = filter.Replace("[list_type] = ", "").Replace("'", "").Trim();
            clean = clean.Replace("[upcoming] = True", "");
            return clean;
        }

        public bool SaveBWICDetails(DataTable raw)
        {
            
            DataTable changes = raw.GetChanges();
            if(null == changes || changes.Rows.Count == 0)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Nothing changed - Nothing to save", "Oops...");
                return false;
            }
            List<DataColumn> changed = changes.GetChangedColumns();

            if (changes.Rows.Count == 0)
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Nothing to save!", "Oops...");
            int rows_changed = 0;
            foreach (DataRow row in changes.Rows)
            {
                int bwicdetail_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["bwicdetail_id"]);
                int bwic_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["bwic_id"]);
                string ticker = row["ticker"].ToString();



                Nullable<int> bid_id = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["bid_id"])
                    bid_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["bid_id"]);
                Nullable<int> privatecolor_id = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["privatecolor_id"])
                   privatecolor_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["privatecolor_id"]);
                bool write_px_talk = row.CellUpdated("px_talk", false);
                bool write_public_color = row.CellUpdated("public_color", false);
                bool write_results = row.CellUpdated("results", false);
                
                bool write_private = row.CellUpdated("private_color", false);
                bool write_oface = row.CellUpdated("oface", false);
                bool write_bid = row.CellUpdated("bid", false);
                bool write_bid_acct = row.CellUpdated("bid_acct", false);


                int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["product_id"]);

                string px_talk = null;
                string public_color = null;
                string results = null;
                string private_color = null;
                string bid = null;
                Nullable<double> oface = null;
                Nullable<int> bid_acct = null;
                int? privatecolorgroup_id = null;

                if (write_px_talk)
                    px_talk = row.RowDataHelper<string>("px_talk");
                if (write_public_color)
                    public_color = row.RowDataHelper<string>("public_color");
                if (write_results)
                    results = row.RowDataHelper<string>("results");
                if (write_private)
                {
                    private_color = row.RowDataHelper<string>("private_color");

                    privatecolorgroup_id = BatCaveLib.Color.DefautlColorGroupId(_server, product_id);
                }

                if (write_oface)
                {
                    object o = row.RowDataHelper<object>("oface");
                    if (DBNull.Value != o)
                        oface = System.Convert.ToDouble(o);
                    if (oface < 1000)
                        oface = oface * 1e6;
                }
                if (write_bid || write_bid_acct)
                    bid = row.RowDataHelper<string>("bid");
                if (write_bid || write_bid_acct)
                {
                    object o = row.RowDataHelper<object>("bid_acct");
                    if (DBNull.Value != o && null != o)
                        bid_acct = System.Convert.ToInt32(o);
                   
                }


                

                Nullable<int> results_kanerai = !write_results ? null : BatCaveLib.KaneraiHelper.SubmitKaneraiPricingIfNeeded(_server, row["cusip"].ToString(), product_id, row["results"].ToString());
                Nullable<int> px_talk_kanerai = !write_px_talk ? null : BatCaveLib.KaneraiHelper.SubmitKaneraiPricingIfNeeded(_server, row["cusip"].ToString(), product_id, row["px_talk"].ToString());

      
                
                
                
                
                
                
                

                
                
                    
                

                BWICDetails.SaveTalkAndResults(_server, bwicdetail_id, px_talk, results, public_color, write_px_talk, write_results, write_public_color, private_color, write_private, privatecolor_id, write_oface, oface, write_bid, bid, write_bid_acct, bid_acct, bid_id, px_talk_kanerai, results_kanerai,privatecolorgroup_id);



                rows_changed++;
            }

            string msg = String.Format("Saved {0} Changes!", rows_changed);
            XtraMessageBox.Show(msg,"Congrats");
            raw.AcceptChanges();
            return true;
        }

        private void CheckForChanges(bool force = false)
        {
            DataTable raw = ((DataView)viewDetail.DataSource).Table;
            DataTable changes = raw.GetChanges();
            if ((null != changes && changes.Rows.Count > 0) || force)
                btnSave.Visible = true;
        }


        private string[] _EditableFields;
        public void SetupEditButton(bool can_edit)
        {
            if(can_edit)
            {
                _EditableFields = new string[] { "oface", "px_talk", "results", "bid", "bid_acct", "public_color", "private_color" };
            }
            else
            {
                _EditableFields = new string[] {  "oface", "px_talk", "results", "private_color" };
                
            }
        }


        private void PopulateActiveBWICFromSummary(int bwic_id)
        {
            GridView gv = viewSummary;
            _bwicdetail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();

            bool can_edit = gv.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("can_edit");
            int bond_number = gv.GetActiveRowValue<int>("#_bonds");
            string list_type = gv.GetActiveRowValue<string>("list_type");
            object oface = gv.GetActiveRowValue<object>("oface");
            bool cover = gv.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("cover"); ;
            bool product_cover = gv.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("product_cover");
            
            btnAddColor.Checked = false;
            string coverage = gv.GetActiveRowValue<string>("coverage");
            DateTime due_time = gv.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("bid_time");
            string account = gv.GetActiveRowValue<string>("account");
            string list_name = gv.GetActiveRowValue<string>("list_name");
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(list_name))
                list_name += " - ";

            string format = "h:mm tt";

            var timeUtc = DateTime.UtcNow;
            TimeZoneInfo easternZone = TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById("Eastern Standard Time");
            DateTime nyc_time = TimeZoneInfo.ConvertTimeFromUtc(timeUtc, easternZone);

            if (due_time.Date > DateTime.Today)
                format = "M/d/yy h:mm tt";
            TimeSpan ts = due_time - nyc_time;
            string due_time_str = due_time.ToString(format);

            string remaining_string = "";

            if (ts.TotalDays > 1)
                remaining_string = String.Format("{0:0} day{1} till bid time", ts.TotalDays, ts.TotalDays >= 1 ? "s" : "\"");
            else if (ts.TotalHours > 1.5)
                remaining_string = String.Format("{0:0} hour{1} till bid time", ts.TotalHours, ts.TotalHours > 1 ? "s" : "\"");
            else if (ts.Minutes > 0)
                remaining_string = String.Format("{0:0} minutes till bid time", ts.TotalMinutes);

            else if (ts.TotalDays < -1)
                remaining_string = String.Format("BWIC OVER {0:0} day{1} ago", -ts.TotalDays, ts.TotalDays <= 1 ? "s" : "\"");
            else if (ts.TotalHours <= -1.5)
                remaining_string = String.Format("BWIC OVER {0:0} hour{1} ago", -ts.TotalHours, ts.TotalHours <= 1 ? "s" : "\"");
            else if (ts.TotalMinutes < 0)
                remaining_string = String.Format("BWIC OVER {0:0} minutes ago", -ts.TotalMinutes, ts.Days > 1 ? "s" : "\"");




            dockPanel1.Text = account + " - " + list_type + " - " + list_name + due_time.ToString(format) + " - (" + remaining_string + ")";
            
            
            if (product_cover && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(coverage))
                lblSalesCvg.Text = "Sales: " + coverage;
            else
                lblSalesCvg.Text = null;

            
            {

                



                PopulateBWIC(bwic_id, _add_color_automatically, product_cover, list_type);
                
                _last_selected_bwic = bwic_id;
            }

            SetupEditButton(can_edit);
            
            btnAddCusips.Visible = can_edit;
            if (bond_number == 0)
            {
                
                btnAddCusips.Text = "Add bonds from clipboard";
            }
            else if(DBNull.Value == oface)
            {
                btnAddCusips.Text = "Add oface from clipboard";
            }
            else if(bond_number > 0)
            {
                btnAddCusips.Text = "Append new bond(s) from clipboard";
            }

            


            
            
            
            
        }
        private void viewSummary_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            _bwicdetail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            GridView gv = (GridView)sender;
            if (gv.SelectedRowsCount > 1)
                return;
            if (gv.SelectedRowsCount == 0)
            {
                
                return;
            }

            int bwic_id = gv.GetActiveRowValue<int>("bwic_id");
            PopulateActiveBWICFromSummary(bwic_id);
        }

        private void ToggleBWICEdit()
        {
            if (!_bwicdetail.ActivelyEditing)
            {
                
                _bwicdetail.SetEditable(_EditableFields, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.EDIT_COLOR);
            }
            else
            {
                
                
                bool any_changes = _bwicdetail.DataSetHasChanges();
                if (any_changes)
                {
                    
                    var old = Localizer.Active;
                    Localizer.Active = new MyLocalizer();
                    DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("What do you want to do?", "You have unsaved changes...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                    Localizer.Active = old;
                    if (dr == DialogResult.No)
                    {
                        _bwicdetail.RejectDataSourceChanges();
                        
                    }
                    if(dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                    {
                        SaveBWICChanges();
                    }
                    else
                        return;
                }
                btnSave.Visible = false;
                btnAddColor.Checked = false;
                _bwicdetail.RemoveFromEdit(_EditableFields, System.Drawing.Color.White);
            }
        }

        private void btnBBGBlastWithBids_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)

            BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT f = GetBBGMSGFormat(chkCopyToClipboard.Checked, chkIB.Checked && chkIB.Visible);
            BWICBlastHelper.BlastSelectedBWICS(_server, ids, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID, null, f, blast_indirects,all, _bbg, bt);
        }

        private void btnBBGBlast_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT bbg = BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.NOT_SUPPORTED;
            if (chkBlastType.EditValue.ToString() == "summary")
                bbg = BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC;
            if (chkBlastType.EditValue.ToString() == "results")
                bbg = BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS;
            if (chkBlastType.EditValue.ToString() == "bids")
                bbg = BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID;
            if (chkBlastType.EditValue.ToString() == "px_talk")
                bbg = BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK;

            bool blast_indirects = false;

            List<int> ids = viewSummary.GetFilteredData<int>("bwic_id");
            if(chkOnlySelected.Checked)
                ids = viewSummary.GetUniqueList<int>("bwic_id", true);
            List<string> tickers = null;
            
            
            DataTable all = ((DataView)viewSummary.DataSource).ToTable();
            BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt = BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.GetBlastTemplate(drpBlastFormat.EditValue.ToString());
            BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT f = GetBBGMSGFormat(chkCopyToClipboard.Checked, chkIB.Checked && chkIB.Visible);
            BWICBlastHelper.BlastSelectedBWICS(_server, ids, bbg, tickers, f, blast_indirects,all, _bbg, bt);
        }

        public BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT GetBBGMSGFormat(bool clipboard_checked,bool ib_checked_and_visible)
        {
            if(clipboard_checked)
            {
                if (ib_checked_and_visible)
                    return BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT.IB;
                else
                    return BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT.CLIPBOARD;
            }
            return BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT.BLAST;
        }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlCalendar.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlCalendar : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlCalendar()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public string _server;
        public SchedulerStorage mainCalendarStorage = new SchedulerStorage();

        
        
        SchedulerHelper _scheduler_helper;
        GridHelper _grid_legend;
        GridHelper _myaccounts;
        bool loading = false;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        

        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            loading = true;
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            mainScheduler.DataStorage = mainCalendarStorage;
            mainCalendarStorage.BeginUpdate();
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.Start = "bid_time";
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.End = "end_time";
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.Subject = "subject";
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.AppointmentId = "id";
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.Status = "calendar_color";
            
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new DevExpress.XtraScheduler.AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("calendar_color", "calendar_color"));
            
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("list_type", "list_type"));
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("upcoming", "upcoming"));
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("products", "products"));
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("today", "today"));
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.CustomFieldMappings.Add(new AppointmentCustomFieldMapping("my_bwic", "my_bwic"));
            
            
            
            
            mainCalendarStorage.FetchAppointments += MainCalendarStorage_FetchAppointments;
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.Mappings.AppointmentId = "bwic_id";


           

            _scheduler_helper = new SchedulerHelper(mainScheduler, mainCalendarStorage);
            ctrlBWICFilter.SetFilterUpdate(_scheduler_helper.SetFilter);

            _grid_legend = new GridHelper(grdLegend, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _myaccounts = new GridHelper(grdMyAccounts, _server, true,_bat_signal);

            mainScheduler.Start = DateTime.Now;

            mainCalendarStorage.EndUpdate();
            
            lblVersion.Text = "s";
            
            
            

            var linkTimeLocal = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetBuildTime(TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById("Eastern Standard Time"));

            lblVersion.Text = $"BUILD: {linkTimeLocal.ToString()}\nRESTART: {DateTime.Now}";
            bool autostart_exists = AutoStartExists();
            chkStartBatcaveOnReboot.Checked = autostart_exists;
            PopulateCoverage();
            loading = false;

        }

        private void PopulateCoverage()
        {
            
            DataTable t = BatCaveLib.Coverage.MyCoverageSummary(_server, false);
            
            
            _myaccounts.SetGrid(t,"name,product");
        }

        private void MainCalendarStorage_FetchAppointments(object sender, FetchAppointmentsEventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        public partial class CalendarFilters
        {

        }
        bool _loaded_once = false;
        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            if (loading)
                return;
            
            TimeSpan ts = DateTime.Now - mainScheduler.Start;
            
            if (!_loaded_once)
            {
                List<string> prod_names = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(_server,true);
                ctrlBWICFilter.SetPreferred(prod_names);
            }

            DataTable table = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetBWICSummary(_server, ts.Days + 1);
            mainCalendarStorage.Appointments.DataSource = table;
            

            SortedDictionary<string, string> prods = BatCaveLib.Products.ProcessProducts(table,"products");
            ctrlBWICFilter.PopulateBoxes(prods);
            

            PopulateLegendIfNeeded();
            _loaded_once = true;
        }

        private bool legend_populated = false;
        public void PopulateLegendIfNeeded()
        {
            if (!legend_populated)
            {
                grdLegend.MainView().OptionsSelection.MultiSelect = true;
                DataTable colors = BatCaveLib.Color.GetColorLegendProducts(_server);
                _grid_legend.SetGrid(colors);
                
                grdLegend.MainView().FocusedRowHandle = -1;

                grdLegend.MainView().OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedRow = false;
                grdLegend.MainView().UnselectRow(0);
                grdLegend.MainView().OptionsSelection.MultiSelect = true;
                grdLegend.MainView().ClearSelection();
                grdLegend.MainView().Columns["name"].OptionsColumn.AllowFocus = false;
                legend_populated = true;
            }
        }

    private void mainScheduler_EditAppointmentFormShowing(object sender, AppointmentFormEventArgs e)
        {

            int bwic_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(e.Appointment.Id);
            DataTable tbl = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetBWICDetailGrid(_server, bwic_id);

            DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView();
            f.Init(_server, _bat_signal);
            string default_bwic = BatCaveLib.Utils.DefaultFormats(_server, "long_bwic",null);
            f.Populate(tbl, default_bwic);
            f.ShowDialog();


            e.Handled = true;
        }

        private void mainScheduler_AppointmentViewInfoCustomizing(object sender, AppointmentViewInfoCustomizingEventArgs e)
        {
            
            if (null != e.ViewInfo.Appointment.CustomFields["calendar_color"])
            {
                System.Drawing.Color c = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(e.ViewInfo.Appointment.CustomFields["calendar_color"].ToString());
                SolidBrush b = new SolidBrush(c);
                e.ViewInfo.Status.SetBrush(b);
            }

        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            
            
            
            Utils.RestartApp(_server);
        }

        private void btnMissingAnAccount_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string html = _myaccounts.ExportToHTMLSimple();
            BatCaveLib.Accounts.SpawnMissingAccountEmail(_server, html);
        }

        private void chkStartBatcaveOnReboot_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (loading)
                return;
            ToggleAutoStart(chkStartBatcaveOnReboot.Checked);
        }

        public bool AutoStartExists()
        {
            string shortcut = GetShortcutLocation;
            return File.Exists(shortcut);
        }

        public string GetShortcutLocation
        {
            get
            {
                return Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.Startup) + "\\BatCave.lnk";
            }
        }
        public void ToggleAutoStart(bool enable)
        {
            string location = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(_server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_LOCATION);
            string shortcut = GetShortcutLocation;
            if (enable)
            {
                if (!File.Exists(shortcut))
                {
                    File.Copy(location, shortcut);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                if(File.Exists(shortcut))
                {
                    File.Delete(shortcut);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

using Keys = System.Windows.Forms.Keys;

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlColor : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlColor()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        string _server;
        GridHelper _grid;
        private GridHelper _grid_legend;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            
            _grid = new GridHelper(gridDetail,_server, true, _bat_signal);
            ctrlLegend.Init(_server);
            
            
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            SearchActive();
        }

        private void txtSearch_KeyDown(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.Enter && Control.ModifierKeys != Keys.Shift)
            {
                SearchActive();
                e.Handled = true;
                
            }
        }

        private void SearchActive()
        {
            string raw_bonds = txtSearch.Text;

            bool show_wait = true;
            _grid.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();

            if(String.IsNullOrEmpty(raw_bonds))
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Can't be blank...");
                return;
            }
            bool orig_sort = true;
            DataSet tickers = BatCave.Color.SearchRaw(_server, raw_bonds, this.ParentForm, show_wait, null, true, true, true, true, true, true,false,true,false,true,chkDealSearch.Checked, orig_sort,true,true,true,true,true,null,false,false,true,true,true);
            if (null == tickers)
                return;

            string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "default", tickers.Tables[0],"product_id");
            
            _grid.SetColumnVisible(column_format );
            _grid.SetGrid(tickers.Tables[0],column_format);




            
            if (null != viewDetail.Columns["product_id"] && null != viewDetail.Columns["cusip"])
            {
                List<string> cusips = new List<string>();
                foreach (DataRow row in tickers.Tables[0].Rows)
                {
                    if(DBNull.Value == row["product_id"])
                        continue;
                    int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["product_id"]);
                    bool kanerai_enabled = BatCaveLib.Products.GetKaneraiProducts(_server).Contains(product_id);
                    if (kanerai_enabled)
                    {
                        string cusip = row["cusip"].ToString();
                        cusips.Add(cusip);
                    }

                    
                }

                if (cusips.Count != 0)
                    KaneraiLib.DB.RequestKaneraiLoad(_server, cusips, null);
            }

            if (tickers.Tables[0].Rows.Count > 0)
            {
                
                
               
                List<int> products = BatCaveLib.Products.ProductsRegColor(_server);
                _grid.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, column_format, true, false, ExtraActionForColor, true,null, false,false,false, true, true,true);
            }

        }

        public void ExtraActionForColor()
        {
            if (_grid._DataSet.Tables.Count > 0 && _grid._DataSet.Tables[0].Rows.Count == 1)
            
            {
                _grid.ExpandAllRows();
            }
        }
        




        private void ctrlColor_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("FOSTER"))
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                txtSearch.Text = "GNR 2016-H11 KI";
                
                
                simpleButton2.Visible = true;
                btnAllTranches.Visible = true;
            }

            txtSearch.SelectionStart = 0;
            txtSearch.SelectionLength = 0;

            PopulateLegend();
        }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlInventory.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlInventory : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlInventory()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        string _server;
        GridHelper _inventory;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _inventory = new GridHelper(grdInventory, server, true, _bat_signal);
            _inventory.AppendPopup(viewInventory, CustomInventoryPopup);
        }

        bool first_load = true;
        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            if (first_load)
            {
                
                
                UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime xd = new UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime(DateTime.Today);
                dtAsOf.EditValue = xd.PreviousBusinessDay();
                DataTable my_books = BatCaveLib.Inventory.GetMyBooksTable(_server);
                RepositoryItemLookUpEdit accts = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
                drpBooks.PopulateLookup(my_books, "book_id", "book_id");
                if(my_books.Rows.Count == 1)
                {
                    drpBooks.EditValue = System.Convert.ToInt32(my_books.Rows[0]["book_id"]);
                }
                
            }
            DateTime asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(dtAsOf.EditValue);
            List<int> books = new List<int>(new int[] { System.Convert.ToInt32(drpBooks.EditValue) } );
            DataTable inventory = BatCaveLib.Inventory.GetInventory(_server, asOf, books);
            _inventory.SetGrid(inventory);
            viewInventory.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewInventory.Columns["oface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "oface", "Total Notional: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewInventory.Columns["cface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "cface", "Total Current: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewInventory.Columns["sales_credit"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "sales_credit", "SC Paid Out: {0:0,.0}K");
            viewInventory.Columns["p/l pre-sc"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "p/l pre-sc", "P/L Pre SC: {0:0,.0}K");
            viewInventory.Columns["market_value"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "market_value", "Total MV: {0:0.000}MM");
            viewInventory.Columns["age"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Average, "age", "Average: {0:0.0} Days");
            viewInventory.Columns["age"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Max, "age", "Oldest: {0:0.0} Days");
            _inventory.BestFitVisible();
            first_load = false;
        }

        private void drpAccounts_Properties_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void ctrlInventory_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        public void CustomInventoryPopup(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu_tew = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item_tew = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Transfer to Order", this.TransferToOrder);
                item_tew.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(item_tew);
            }
        }


        private void TransferToOrder(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string ticker = viewInventory.GetActiveRowValue<string>("ticker");
            double oface = viewInventory.GetActiveRowValue<double>("oface");
            int? product_id = viewInventory.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("product_id", false);
            if(null == product_id)
                product_id = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<int>(_server, ticker, "product_id", false, false);
            int default_color_group = BatCaveLib.Color.GetDefaultColorGroup<int>(_server, "colorgroup_id", product_id);
            Nullable<int> account_id = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetStockAccount(_server);
            string bond_label_1 = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(_server, ticker, "bond_label_1", true, false);
            

            int order_id = BatCaveLib.Orders.InsertUpdateOrder(_server, null, ticker, oface, null, null, true, default_color_group, account_id, false, bond_label_1, null, null, null,product_id.Value,null,null, null,null,$"{oface:0.000}");
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
        }

        private void drpBooks_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void dtAsOf_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void btnAddColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _inventory.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, null, true, false, null, true, true, false,false, false, true, true,true);
        }
    }
}

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlLegend : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlLegend()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        public void Init(string server)
        {
            _server = server;
        }

        DataTable _colors;
        public void Populate(string column)
        {
            _colors = BatCaveLib.Color.GetColorLegend(_server);
            _val_col = "type";
            foreach (DataRow row in _colors.Rows)
            {
                listBox1.Items.Add(row[column]);
            }
        }

        public void MultiColumn(bool multi)
        {
            listBox1.MultiColumn = multi;
        }
        public void ToggleLabelVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            labelControl1.Visible = visible;
        }
        private string _val_col;


        public void SetBold()
        {
            this.listBox1.Appearance.Font = new System.Drawing.Font(listBox1.Font.Name, listBox1.Font.Size, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Bold);
        }
        public void PopulateEasy(string item,string color)
        {
            if(null == _colors)
            {
                _colors = new DataTable();
                _val_col = "value";
                _colors.Columns.Add("value");
                _colors.Columns.Add("row_color");
            }
            _colors.Rows.Add(new object[] { item, color });
            listBox1.Items.Add(item);
        }

        public void Resize(Nullable<int> width, Nullable<int> height)
        {
            int _width = listBox1.Width;
            int _height = listBox1.Height;
            if (null != width)
                _width = width.Value;
            if (null != height)
                _height = height.Value;

            listBox1.Size = new Size(_width, _height);
        }


            private void listBox1_DrawItem(object sender, ListBoxDrawItemEventArgs e)
        {
            string item = listBox1.Items[e.Index].ToString();
            string color = _colors.Select("["+_val_col+"] = '" + item + "'")[0]["row_color"].ToString();
            e.AllowDrawSkinBackground = false;
            e.Appearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromName(color);
        }
    }
}

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlMEmarks : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlMEmarks()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        private GridHelper _summary;
        private GridHelper _detail;

        private bool _editing = false;
        FilteringHelper _filter_helper;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;

        public void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _summary = new GridHelper(grdMarkRequests, _server, false,_bat_signal);
            _detail = new GridHelper(gridDetail, _server,true, _bat_signal);
            _summary.SetGridMultiSelect(false);
            viewSummary.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = true;
            viewSummary.OptionsBehavior.Editable = false;
            _summary.ShowAutoFilterPanel(false);
            _detail.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }
        bool first_load = true;
        public void RefreshTab()
        {

            Nullable<int> memark_id = null;
            if (viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount > 0 && viewSummary.IsShowFilterPanel == false && !viewSummary.IsFilterRow(viewSummary.FocusedRowHandle))
                memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");

            
            if (first_load)
            {
                DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Permissions.ProductPermissions(_server);
                if (products.Rows.Count == 0)
                    chkAutoFilterMe.Checked = false;
                LoadScreen(MODE.NEW, null, null, null, null, null, null);
                viewDetail.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
                
                
                


            }
            
            RefreshTab(memark_id);
            first_load = false;
        }

 

        public void RefreshTab(Nullable<int> memark_id)
        {
            _detail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            HandleFilter();

            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
            drpAccounts.PopulateLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id", false);

            
            DataTable summary = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetMEMarkRequests(_server, chkAutoFilterMe.Checked);
            string filter = null;
            if (first_load)
                filter = "[complete] = False";
            

            _summary.SetGrid(summary,null,"memark_id",memark_id,false, filter,false);
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

            
            if (first_load)
            {
                viewSummary.Columns["finished"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "finished", "{0:0}");
                viewSummary.Columns["total"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "total", "{0:0}");
                viewSummary.Columns["my_finished"].Summary
                    .Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "my_finished", "{0:0}");
                viewSummary.Columns["my_total"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "my_total", "{0:0}");
                viewSummary.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            }

            _summary.SetReadOnly(new string[] { "name", "due_date" });
            _summary.HideColumn("account_id");
            

            viewSummary.BestFitColumns();
            _summary.SetWidth("note", 250);
            _summary.SetWidth("name", 125);


            



        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpAccounts.EditValue);
            DateTime due_date = System.Convert.ToDateTime(dtDueTime.EditValue);
            string email_list = txtEmailList.Text;

            bool exists = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.MarkRequestsExists(_server, due_date, account_id);
            if(exists && _mode == MODE.NEW)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Mark request already exists for this account and date.  Proceed?", "Oops..", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo,MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                if(dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                {
                    return;
                }

            }
            if (_mode == MODE.UPDATE)
            {
                BatCaveLib.MEMarks.DeleteMarkRequest(_server, _loaded.memark_id.Value, true);
            }
            int memark_id = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.InsertUpdateMarkRequest(_server, account_id, due_date, txtNotes.Text, _loaded.memark_id,false,email_list);
            bool force_update = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().session_started;
            var bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(_server, txtBonds.Text, '\n', force_update, true);
            foreach (Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper bond in bonds.matched_list)
            {
                BatCaveLib.MEMarks.InsertMark(_server, memark_id, bond.ticker);
            }
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done","Woo-hoo...");
            LoadScreen(MODE.NEW, null, null, null, null, null, null);
            RefreshTab(memark_id);
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        private void ValidateSaveButton()
        {
            bool enable = false;

            if (null != drpAccounts.EditValue && null != dtDueTime.EditValue && null != txtBonds.EditValue)
                enable = true;
            btnSave.Enabled = enable;
            btnValidateBonds.Enabled = enable;
        }

        }

        {
            if (null != drpAccounts.EditValue)
            {
                int account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpAccounts.EditValue);
                string mails = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetLastSentEmails(_server, account_id, false);
                txtEmailList.EditValue = mails;
            }
            ValidateSaveButton();
        }

        private void dtDueTime_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
