        }

        private void btnValidateBonds_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            bool bbg_working = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().session_started;

            var bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(_server, txtBonds.Text, '\n', bbg_working, true);
            if (bonds.notmatched.Count == 0)
                XtraMessageBox.Show("All Bonds Validated", "Great Success!");
            else
                XtraMessageBox.Show(String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.notmatched), "Oops...");

        }

        private void gridView2_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            int[] selected_row = viewSummary.GetSelectedRows();
            _detail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            if (selected_row.Length == 1)
            {
                if (viewSummary.IsFilterRow(selected_row[0]))
                {
                    _detail.ClearUnderlyingData();
                    return;
                }
            }
            if (viewSummary.RowCount == 0)
            {
                _detail.ClearUnderlyingData();
                return;
            }
            int id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            string account = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("name");
            DateTime asOf = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("due_date");

            int? my_total = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("my_total");
            int? my_finished = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("my_finished");
            int togo = 0;
            if(null != my_total && null != my_finished)
                togo = my_total.Value - my_finished.Value;

            string label = String.Format("M/E Mark Details - {0} - Due: {1:M/d/yyyy}", account, asOf);
            if (togo > 0)
                label += String.Format(" - You have {0} cusips to go.", togo);
            dockPanel1.Text = label;
            PopulateId(id, true);
            LoadScreen(MODE.NEW, null, null, null, null, null, null);

        }

        private void gridView2_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {


        }

        private void PopulateSummaryBasedOnId(Nullable<int> memark_id)
        {
            int account_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            DateTime due_date = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("due_date");
            string notes = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("notes");
            string email_list = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("email_list");
            List<string> tickers = viewDetail.GetUniqueList<string>("ticker");
        }


        private void PopulateId(int id,bool add_color)
        {
            PopulateGridOnRow(id);
            btnEditMarksNew.Checked = false;
            
            string visible_cols = _detail.GetVisibleCSVString();
            if (add_color)
                _detail.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, visible_cols, true, false, FormatGridAppropriately,true, true, false, false, false, true, true, false);
        }
        private void FormatGridAppropriately()
        {

            if (gridDetail.InvokeRequired)
            {
                gridDetail.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { FormatGridAppropriately(); }));
            }
            else
            {
                FormatGridAppropriatelyInternal();
            }
        }
        private void FormatGridAppropriatelyInternal()
        {
            foreach (DataRow row in _results.Tables[1].Rows)
            {
                DateTime d = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["due_date"]);
                if (_mark_format == MARK_FORMAT.DEC || _mark_format == MARK_FORMAT.RAW)
                {

                    
                    if (null != viewDetail.Columns[d.ToString(asOfFormat)])
                    {
                        viewDetail.Columns[d.ToString(asOfFormat)].DisplayFormat.FormatType = DevExpress.Utils.FormatType.Numeric;
                        viewDetail.Columns[d.ToString(asOfFormat)].DisplayFormat.FormatString = "0.000";
                        
                    }
                }
                else
                    _detail.SetFormat(d.ToString(asOfFormat), "");
            }
            viewDetail.OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = false;
            _results.Tables[0].AcceptChanges();
        }
        DataSet _results = null;
        private void PopulateGridOnRow(int id)
        {
            _results = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.MarkDataSetDetail(_server, id);
            Nullable<DateTime> latest = null;
            foreach (DataRow row in _results.Tables[1].Rows)
            {
                DateTime d = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["due_date"]);
                _results.Tables[0].Columns.Add(d.ToString(asOfFormat), typeof(object));
                if (null == latest || (null != latest && d > latest))
                {
                    latest = d;
                }
            }

            int index = _results.Tables[0].Columns.IndexOf("bond_label_1");
            DataColumn col = _results.Tables[0].Columns.Add("marked_by", typeof(string));
            
            col.SetOrdinal(index + 1);

            foreach (DataRow row in _results.Tables[2].Rows)
            {
                string ticker = row["ticker"].ToString();
                DateTime asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["asOf"]);
                string mark = row["mark_raw"].ToString();

                foreach (DataRow m in _results.Tables[0].Rows)
                {
                    if (m["ticker"].ToString() == ticker)
                    {
                        object o = ConvertMark(_mark_format,mark);
                        m[asOf.ToString(asOfFormat)] = o;
                        if (asOf == latest)
                            m["marked_by"] = row["marked_by"].ToString();
                    }
                }
            }

            IEnumerable<string> marked_by = _results.Tables[0].UniqueValues<string>("marked_by");

            _detail.SetGrid(_results);
            if (marked_by.Count() == 1)
                _detail.HideColumnIfSameValue("marked_by");
            FormatGridAppropriately();



            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        string asOfFormat = "M/d/yyyy";



        private void btnEditSelected_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }




        private void SaveMarks()
        {
            DataTable changes = _detail.GetChangedRows();
            List<DataColumn> cols = changes.GetChangedColumns();
            List<string> errors = new List<string>();
            int actually_updated = 0;

            foreach (DataColumn asOf in cols)
            {
                DateTime mark_as_of = System.Convert.ToDateTime(asOf.Caption);
                string error = "";


                foreach (DataRow row in changes.Rows)
                {
                    string ticker = row["ticker"].ToString();
                    string mark_raw = null;
                    Nullable<double> mark_dbl = null;
                    if (DBNull.Value != row[mark_as_of.ToString(asOfFormat)])
                    {
                        mark_raw = row[mark_as_of.ToString(asOfFormat)].ToString();
                        if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(mark_raw))
                            mark_dbl = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.TicDec(mark_raw);
                        else
                            mark_raw = null;
                        Nullable<double> last_mark = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetLastMark(_server, ticker, mark_as_of,false);
                        if (null != last_mark && null != mark_dbl)
                        {
                            double delta = Math.Abs(last_mark.Value - mark_dbl.Value);
                            if (delta > 5.0)
                            {
                                error = ticker + " - " + last_mark.Value + " / " + mark_dbl;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    DialogResult dr = DialogResult.Yes;
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(error))
                    {
                        dr = XtraMessageBox.Show(error, "Large Change Warning - Update this bond?", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                    }
                    if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                    {
                        List<string> changed_and_completed = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetAssociatedMEMarks<string>(_server, ticker, mark_as_of, true,"name");

                        if(changed_and_completed.Count > 0)
                        {
                            Nullable<double> old_mark = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetLastMark(_server, ticker, mark_as_of, true);
                            Nullable<int> user_id = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetLastMEMarkMarkedBy(_server, ticker,mark_as_of,true);
                            string email = BatCaveLib.Users.GetUserDetail<string>(_server, user_id, "email");

                            SendPriceChangeNotification(_server,changed_and_completed, ticker,mark_as_of,old_mark,email);
                        }

                        BatCaveLib.MEMarks.InsertUpdateMark(_server, ticker, mark_as_of, mark_raw,true);
                        actually_updated++;
                    }
                    if(dr == DialogResult.No)
                    {
                        _detail.RejectDataSourceChanges();
                    }
                }
            }
            string message = String.Format("Saved {0} Marks", actually_updated);
            
            _detail.AcceptChanges();
            
            CheckChanges();
            
        }

        public static void SendPriceChangeNotification(string server, IEnumerable<string> accounts, string ticker, DateTime asOF,Nullable<double> old_mark,string emails)
        {
            UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.PRICING_EMAIL, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, null, null);
            
            
            accounts = accounts.Distinct();
            {
                string body = "";
                string bond_label = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(server, ticker, "bond_label_1", false, false);
                if(null != bond_label)
                {
                    body += "BOND TYPE: " + bond_label + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;
                }
                if (null != old_mark)
                    body += "OLD MARK: " + old_mark.Value + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;
                body += "Accounts Affected:\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, accounts.ToArray());
                string subject = String.Format("[{0:MM/dd/yyyy}] Completed Mark Changed: {1}", asOF, ticker);
                
                m.SendSMTPMail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.PRICING_EMAIL, emails, null, subject, body, null, false, true, CommonInterfaces.Constants.PRICING_EMAIL);
            }
        }

        private void CheckChanges()
        {
            bool changes = _detail.AnyChanges();
            if (changes)
                SaveMarks();
            
        }

        }

        private void btnSendMarks_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            int memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            int account_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("account_id");
            string account_name = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("name");


            int before = System.Convert.ToInt32(grpViewMarksIn.SelectedIndex);
            if (before != 0)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You want to export the prices in non-decimal form?", "Please confirm...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
                    return;
                if (dr == DialogResult.No)
                    grpViewMarksIn.SelectedIndex = 0;
            }

            PopulateId(memark_id, false);

            
            if (null != _detail.GetChangedColumns())
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("You have unsaved changes...Please save before proceeding");
                
            }
            DateTime current = _summary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("due_date");

            
            string export_columns = "ticker,cusip,bond_label_1," + current.ToString(asOfFormat);

            List<string> all_cols = new List<string>(export_columns.Split(','));
            List<string> cols2remove = new List<string>();
            foreach (DataColumn col in _detail._DataTable.Columns)
            {
                if (!all_cols.Contains(col.ColumnName))
                    cols2remove.Add(col.ColumnName);
            }

            foreach (string col in cols2remove)
            {
                _detail.HideColumn(col);
                
            }

            gridDetail.MainView().OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = true;
            
            
            
            
            string subject = "Baird Month End Pricing " + current.ToString(asOfFormat);
            string archive_folder = System.IO.Path.GetTempPath();
            string full_file = System.IO.Path.Combine(archive_folder, subject);


            DevExpress.XtraPrinting.XlsxExportOptionsEx heoe = new DevExpress.XtraPrinting.XlsxExportOptionsEx();
            heoe.ExportType = DevExpress.Export.ExportType.DataAware;

            string html_name = archive_folder + subject.Replace("/", "-") + ".html";
            string xls_name = archive_folder + subject.Replace("/", "-") + ".xlsx";

            gridDetail.MainView().BestFitColumns();
            
            gridDetail.ExportToHtml(html_name);
            gridDetail.ExportToXlsx(xls_name, heoe);
            
            gridDetail.MainView().OptionsView.ColumnAutoWidth = false;

            string header = "<center><img width=83 height=76 src=\"http:

            string disclaimer_file = System.IO.Path.Combine(System.IO.Path.GetDirectoryName(Application.ExecutablePath), "PricingDisclaimer.txt");
            string disclaimer = System.IO.File.ReadAllText(disclaimer_file);
            UtilsLib.Mail m = new Mail(null, null, null, null);
            string html = System.IO.File.ReadAllText(archive_folder + subject.Replace("/", "-") + ".html");
            List<string> warning = new List<string>();
            warning.Add("sold");
            foreach (string w in warning)
            {
                if (html.ContainsIns(w))
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show(w, "Suspicious Comment - Warning");
                }
            }
            
            string body = header + html + "<br><br><br>" + disclaimer + "<br><br><font face=\"Calibri\" size=2>Report Generated: " + DateTime.Now + "</font>";
            
            DataTable tbl = _detail._DataTable;
            List<int> products = tbl.GetUniqueList<int>("product_id");
            List<string> sales_coverage = new List<string>();
            var v = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetDetails(_server, memark_id);
            if(chkIncludeSales.Checked)
            {
                sales_coverage = BatCaveLib.Coverage.GetCoverageAttribute<string>(_server, account_id, products, "email");
                if (sales_coverage.Contains("dfoster@rwbaird.com"))
                    sales_coverage.Remove("dfoster@rwbaird.com");
            }
            string emails = v.email_list;
            sales_coverage.Add(CommonInterfaces.Constants.PRICING_EMAIL);
            string cvg_emails = String.Join(";", sales_coverage.ToArray());
            m.SendMail(emails, cvg_emails, null, subject, body, new string[] { xls_name }, true, false, CommonInterfaces.Constants.PRICING_EMAIL);


            grpViewMarksIn.SelectedIndex = before;
            PopulateGridOnRow(memark_id);
        }

         private void btnEditMarksNew_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ToggleEditing();
        }

        private void ToggleEditing()
        {
            DateTime current = _summary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("due_date");
            if (btnEditMarksNew.Checked)
            {
                _detail.SetEditable(new string[] { current.ToString(asOfFormat) }, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.EDIT_COLOR);
            }
            else
            
            {
                _detail._DataTable.RejectChanges();
                _detail.ResetEditable();
                
            }
            _editing = !_editing;
        }

        private void gridView2_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {


            if (e.MenuType == DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                menu.Items.Clear();

                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu manage = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem sent = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Mark Request As Sent", this.MarkRequestSent);
                menu.Items.Add(sent);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem manage_item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Delete M/E Mark Request", this.DeleteSelectedRequest);
                manage_item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(manage_item);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem edit_item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Edit Mark Request", this.EditMarkRequest);
                edit_item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(edit_item);

            }
        }

        public void MarkRequestSent(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int account_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("account_id");
            DateTime due_date = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<DateTime>("due_date");
            string txt = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("notes");
            int memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            string email_list = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("email_list");
            BatCaveLib.MEMarks.InsertUpdateMarkRequest(_server, account_id, due_date, txt, memark_id, true, "-1");
            RefreshTab();
        }
        public void DeleteSelectedRequest(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Are you sure you want to completely delete this M/E Mark Request?", "Just checking...",MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
            if(dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                BatCaveLib.MEMarks.DeleteMarkRequest(_server, memark_id,false);
                RefreshTab();
            }
        }

        public void EditMarkRequest(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            var v = BatCaveLib.MEMarks.GetDetails(_server, memark_id);
            LoadScreen(MODE.UPDATE, v.memark_id, v.account_id, v.due_time, v.note, v.email_list, v.bonds);
        }

        private enum MARK_FORMAT { TIC, DEC , RAW };
        private MARK_FORMAT _mark_format = MARK_FORMAT.DEC;
        private void grpViewMarksIn_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (grpViewMarksIn.EditValue.ToString() == "tics")
                _mark_format = MARK_FORMAT.TIC;
            if (grpViewMarksIn.EditValue.ToString() == "dec")
                _mark_format = MARK_FORMAT.DEC;
            if (grpViewMarksIn.EditValue.ToString() == "raw")
                _mark_format = MARK_FORMAT.RAW;

            int id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            if(null == _detail.GetChangedColumns() || _detail.GetChangedColumns().Count == 0)
                PopulateGridOnRow(id);
            else
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("You have unsaved changes.  The conversion will be active next time you select a new mark request","FYI");
            }
        }

        private object ConvertMark(MARK_FORMAT mf, object mark)
        {
            object o = null;
            if (mf == MARK_FORMAT.DEC && null != mark && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(mark.ToString()) && DBNull.Value != mark)
            {
                o = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.TicDec(mark.ToString());
                if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(mark.ToString()) && null == o)
                    o = mark.ToString();
            }
            if (mf == MARK_FORMAT.RAW)
                o = mark;
            if (mf == MARK_FORMAT.TIC)
            {
                if (null != mark && DBNull.Value != mark)
                {
                    double dbl;
                    if(Double.TryParse(mark.ToString(),out dbl))
                        o = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.DecTic(dbl);
                    if (mark.ToString().Contains("-") && mark.ToString().Split('-').Length == 2)
                        o = mark;
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(mark.ToString()) && null == o)
                        o = mark.ToString();
                }
            }
            return o;
        }

        private void ctrlMEMarks_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void chkAutoFilterMe_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilter();
            Nullable<int> memark_id = null;
            if (null == memark_id && viewSummary.SourceRowHandle >= 0)
                memark_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("memark_id");
            if(!first_load)
                RefreshTab(memark_id);
        }

        private void HandleFilter()
        {
            if (chkAutoFilterMe.Checked)
            {
                DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Permissions.ProductPermissions(_server);
                List<string> prod_list = products.Columns["name"].UniqueValues<string>();

                
                string filter = "[BOND_LABEL_1] in ('" + String.Join("','", prod_list) + "')";
                _detail.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);

                
                
            }
            else
            {
                _detail.ClearAutoFilter();
            }
        }



        private void btnRefreshSummary_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void btnRefreshSummary_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            LoadScreen(MODE.NEW, null, null, null, null, null, null);
        }

        public enum MODE { NEW, UPDATE }

        public MODE _mode = MODE.NEW;
        public BatCaveLib.MEMarks.MEMark _loaded;
        public void LoadScreen(MODE mode, Nullable<int> memark_id, Nullable<int> account_id, Nullable<DateTime> due_date, string notes, string email_list, List<string> bonds)
        {
            drpAccounts.EditValue = account_id;
            dtDueTime.EditValue = due_date;
            txtNotes.EditValue = notes;
            txtEmailList.EditValue = email_list;
            txtBonds.EditValue = null == bonds ? null : String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds);
            string header = "Update M/E Mark Request";
            string button = "Update";
           
            if (mode == MODE.NEW)
            {
                header = "Create New M/E Mark Request";
                btnSave.Enabled = false;
                UtilsLib.Dates.XDateTime d = new Dates.XDateTime(DateTime.Today.AddDays(-14));
                dtDueTime.EditValue = d.LastBizDayOfMonth();
                button = "Save";
            }
            btnSave.Text = button;
            grpCreateEditMark.Text = header;
            _mode = mode;
            _loaded = new BatCaveLib.MEMarks.MEMark(memark_id, due_date, account_id, notes, bonds, email_list);
           
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click_2(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            chkAutoFilterMe.Checked = false;
            _summary.ClearAutoFilter();
        }
    }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlNewBWIC.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlNewBWIC : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlNewBWIC()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public delegate void CloseForm(Nullable<int> bwic_id);

        string _server;
        CloseForm _cfd;
        public void Init(string server, CloseForm cfd)
        {
            _server = server;
            _cfd = cfd;
        }

        private void frmNewBWIC_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            
        }


        
        private BWIC _bwic;
        public void PopulateControl(Nullable<int> bwic_id)
        {
            _bwic = new BWIC(_server);
            if (null != bwic_id)
            {
                _bwic.PopulateFromDB(bwic_id.Value);
                btnDeleteBWIC.Visible = true;
                btnClearBonds.Visible = true;
            }

            if(null != _bwic.bid_time)
                dtBidTime.EditValue = _bwic.bid_time;
            else
                dtBidTime.EditValue = DateTime.Now.AddHours(2).RoundTime(30);

            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
            drpAccounts.PopulateLookup(accounts, "name", "account_id");

            DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductList(_server,false);
            drpProducts.PopulateLookup(products, "name", "id");

            

            if (null != _bwic.account_id)
                drpAccounts.EditValue = _bwic.account_id;

            


            chkIndirect.Checked = _bwic.indirect;

            txtListName.EditValue = _bwic.list_name;
            
            
        }


        private void PopulateBWIC()
        {
            _bwic.bid_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(dtBidTime.EditValue);
            _bwic.account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpAccounts.EditValue);
            _bwic.list_name = txtListName.Text;
            _bwic.indirect = chkIndirect.Checked;
            if (null != drpProducts.EditValue)
                _bwic.product_id_override = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpProducts.EditValue);
            else
                _bwic.product_id_override = null;
        }

        private void btnSave_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            PopulateBWIC();
            bool proceed = ValidateSuspiciousInput();
            if (proceed)
            {
                Nullable<int> bwic_id = _bwic.RecordUpdateBWIC();
                ShutDown(bwic_id);
            }
        }

        public bool ValidateSuspiciousInput()
        {
            if (_bwic.bid_time.Value.Hour > 18 || _bwic.bid_time.Value.Hour < 8)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Do you want to cancel save/update?" + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine  + _bwic.bid_time.ToString(), "BWIC Time Looks Suspcious",MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                    return false;
            }
            return true;
            
        }

        private void ShutDown(Nullable<int> bwic_id)
        {
            if (null != _cfd)
                _cfd(bwic_id);
        }



        private void drpAccounts_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ValidateButton();
        }

        private void dtBidTime_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ValidateButton();
        }

        private void txtListName_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ValidateButton();
        }
        private void ValidateButton()
        {
            btnSave.Enabled = (null != dtBidTime.EditValue) && (null != drpAccounts.EditValue);
            btnClearBonds.Enabled = btnSave.Enabled;
        }

        private void btnDeleteBWIC_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You're SURE you want to delete this BWIC?", "Just checking...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);

            if(dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                BatCaveLib.BWICs.DeleteBWIC(_server, _bwic.bwic_id.Value,true,true);
                ShutDown(null);
            }
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You're SURE you want to clear bonds only for this BWIC?", "Just checking...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);

            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                BatCaveLib.BWICs.DeleteBWIC(_server, _bwic.bwic_id.Value,true,false);
                ShutDown(null);
            }
        }

        private void ctrlNewBWIC_VisibleChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
           
        }
    }
}

using DataTable = System.Data.DataTable;

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlNewIssue : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {

        GridHelper _summary;
        GridHelper _detail;
        public ctrlNewIssue()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _summary = new GridHelper(grdSummary, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _detail = new GridHelper(gridDetail, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _summary.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
        }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            PopulateIssueSummary();
        }

        public void PopulateIssueSummary()
        {
            DataTable tbl = BatCaveLib.NewIssue.GetSummary(_server);
            _summary.SetGrid(tbl);
        }

        private void ctrlNewIssue_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void viewSummary_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            string deal_name = _summary.GetActiveRowValue<string>("deal_name");
            DataTable detail = BatCaveLib.NewIssue.GetDetail(_server, deal_name);
            _detail.SetGrid(detail);

        }

        private void BtnPopulateDeals_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<string> cusips = BatCaveLib.NewIssue.InsertRMBSNewIssue(_server, DateTime.Now.AddMonths(-12));
            DXETA eta = new DXETA(cusips.Count,null,this.ParentForm);
            foreach (string cusip in cusips)
            {
                MT.LoadHelper lh = Assets.MT.EnsureAllTranchesLoaded(_server,cusip);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
        }
    }
}

namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlOrders : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlOrders()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        string _server;
        GridHelper _orders;
        bool first_load = true;
        UtilsLib.BBGDDE _bbg;

        BatSignalLib.SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        private string _smtp_server;
       
        public void Init(string server,BatSignalLib.SignalRClient batSignal,string smtp_server)
        {
            

            _server = server;
            _smtp_server = smtp_server;
            
            

            

            
            _bat_signal = batSignal;
            _orders = new GridHelper(gridOrders, _server, true, _bat_signal);

            viewOrders.OptionsBehavior.EditingMode = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridEditingMode.EditFormInplace;
            viewOrders.OptionsView.RowAutoHeight = true;
            viewOrders.OptionsEditForm.CustomEditFormLayout = new ctrlAxe();
            viewOrders.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = false;
            viewOrders.OptionsBehavior.Editable = true;

            viewOrders.Appearance.GroupRow.Font = new System.Drawing.Font("Tahoma", 10.5F, System.Drawing.FontStyle.Bold);
            
            viewOrders.GroupFormat = "{1}";
            viewOrders.Appearance.GroupRow.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.Firebrick;

            

            viewOrders.ValidateRow += viewOrders_ValidateRow;
            viewOrders.PopupMenuShowing += viewOrders_PopupMenuShowing;
            viewOrders.RowUpdated += viewOrders_RowUpdated;
            viewOrders.EditFormShowing += viewCoverage_EditFormShowing;
            viewOrders.EditFormPrepared += viewOrders_EditFormPrepared;
            viewOrders.InitNewRow += viewOrders_InitNewRow;
            viewOrders.CustomDrawCell += ViewOrders_CustomDrawCell;
            viewOrders.EndGrouping += ViewOrders_EndGrouping;

            


            _orders.IgnoreDoubleClickToAddColor();
            _orders.AddDoubleClickToSendToBBGColumns("label");
            _orders.ExpandWhenFilterChanged(true);
            _orders.ShowGroupPanel(false);
            _orders.ToggleAutoFilter(true);

            ctrlLegend.Init(_server);
            ctrlLegend.PopulateEasy("NOT PUBLISHED", "Bisque");
            ctrlLegend.PopulateEasy("NOT PUBLIC", "Lavender");
            ctrlLegend.Resize(140, 28);
            
            ctrlLegend.SetBold();

            ctrlFilter.Resize(300, 50);
            ctrlFilter.MultiColumn(true);
            ctrlFilter.ToggleLabelVisibility(false);
            ctrlFilter.SetGridFilterField("product");
            ctrlFilter.SetBorder(DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.BorderStyles.NoBorder);
            ctrlFilter.SetPostFilterChangeOperation(SetPriorityColumns);


            _orders.AppendPopup(viewOrders, OfferBondBlast);
            _orders.AppendPopup(viewOrders, PublishAll);


        }

        private void ViewOrders_EndGrouping(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            viewOrders.ExpandAllGroups();
        }

        private void ViewOrders_CustomDrawCell(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.RowCellCustomDrawEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.Column.FieldName == "account")
            {
                GridView view = sender as GridView;
                object o = view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "account");
                object st = view.GetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle, "special_tag");
                
                bool special_tag = false;
                if (DBNull.Value != st && null != st)
                    special_tag = Convert.ToBoolean(st);
                if (null != o && DBNull.Value != o)
                {
                    
                    if(special_tag)
                    {
                        e.Appearance.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.Firebrick;
                        e.Appearance.Font = new Font(e.Appearance.Font, FontStyle.Bold);
                        e.Appearance.FontSizeDelta = 1;
                        e.Appearance.TextOptions.HAlignment = DevExpress.Utils.HorzAlignment.Center;
                        
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        private bool updating = false;
        public void RefreshTab(Nullable<int> respective_id,bool open_for_edit)
        {
            updating = true;
            RefreshOrderLazy(respective_id,open_for_edit);

            updating = false;
        }

        private void RefreshOrderLazy(int? respective_id, bool open_for_edit)
        {
            if(first_load)
            {
                List<int> acceptable = BatCaveLib.Permissions.GetInclusiveAxeccessProducts(_server);
                btnCreateAxe.Visible = (acceptable.Count > 0);
            }
            RefreshOrders(false, chkOnlyLive.Checked,respective_id,open_for_edit);
        }



        public void HandleSettingCustomFields()
        {
            List<int> prod = ctrlFilter.GetSelectedProducts(_server);
            int? product_id = null;
            if (prod.Count() == 1)
            {
                product_id = prod[0];
            }

            
            {
                var setting = ctrlAxe.GetSettingsBasedOnProduct(product_id);
                _orders.ShowGroupPanel(setting.ShowGroupByBox);
            }

            
            {
                string new_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.DefaultFormats(_server, "order_axe", product_id, null);
                string current_format = _orders.CurrentColumnVisible;
                if (new_format != current_format)
                {
                    _orders.SetVisibleColumns(new_format,false,false,false);
                    
                    SetPriorityColumns();
                }
            }
        }
        public void SetActiveFilterSafeCustom(CriteriaOperator filter)
        {

            int checked_items = ctrlFilter.CheckedItemCount;
            bool all_checked = ctrlFilter.AllCheckedItems;
            
            _orders.BeginViewUpdate();
            if (checked_items == 0 || all_checked)
            {
                _orders.ExpandWhenFilterChanged(true);
            }
            else
            {
                _orders.ExpandWhenFilterChanged(true);
            }
            bool was_grouped = viewOrders.GroupCount > 0;

            HandleSettingCustomFields();
   
            
            _orders.SetActiveFilterSafe(filter);

            

            {
                HandleRowFormats();
                
            }

            _orders.EndViewUpdate();

        }

        

        
        Delegates.TabSwitcher _tab_switcher;
        public void SetTabSwitcher(Delegates.TabSwitcher ts)
        {
            _tab_switcher = ts;
        }

        bool was_grouped = true;
        public void RefreshOrders(bool only_mine, bool only_live, int? respective_id, bool open_for_edit)
        {

            was_grouped = viewOrders.GroupCount > 0;
            if (null == respective_id && viewOrders.SelectedRowsCount > 0)
                respective_id = _orders.GetSelectedRowList<int>("order_id")[0];

            DataTable orders = BatCaveLib.Orders.GetOrders(_server, only_mine, only_live);
            
            
            
            
            string format =  BatCaveLib.Utils.DefaultFormats(_server, "order_axe", null);
            string filter = viewOrders.FilterPanelText;
            _orders.SetGrid(orders, format, "order_id", respective_id, false, null,false);
            SortedDictionary<string, string> prods = BatCaveLib.Products.ProcessProducts(orders, "product");
            if (first_load)
            {
                
                var v = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(_server,false);
                ctrlFilter.SetFilterUpdate(SetActiveFilterSafeCustom);

                ctrlFilter.SetPreferred(v);
                
                ctrlFilter.PopulateBoxes(prods);
                
                
                ctrlFilter.ToggleCheckVisibility(false);

            }

            if (prods.Count != ctrlFilter.AllItemsCount) 
            {
                ctrlFilter.PopulateBoxes(prods);
            }



            if (null != respective_id)
            {
                bool? row_visible = _orders.IsRowVisible("order_id", respective_id);

                if (null != row_visible && row_visible == false)
                {
                    DataRow[] rows = orders.Select($"order_id = {respective_id.Value}");
                    if (rows.Length == 1)
                    {
                        int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(rows[0]["product_id"]);
                        List<int> selected_prods = ctrlFilter.GetSelectedProducts(_server);
                        

                        if (!selected_prods.Contains(product_id) && selected_prods.Count != 0)
                        {
                            ctrlFilter.CheckBox(_server, product_id);
                        }
                    }
                }
               
            }

            
            
            
            HandleSettingCustomFields();

            if (first_load)
            {
                
                
                
            }




            
            
            

            


            

            viewOrders.OptionsView.RowAutoHeight = true;
            RepositoryItemMemoEdit me = new RepositoryItemMemoEdit();
            me.WordWrap = true;

            viewOrders.Columns["public"].ColumnEdit = me;
            RepositoryItemMemoEdit me2 = new RepositoryItemMemoEdit();
            me2.WordWrap = true;
            viewOrders.Columns["private"].ColumnEdit = me2;




            DataTable ratings = BatCaveLib.Products.RatingSimple(_server);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit li = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            li.PopulateGridLookup(ratings, "name", "rating_id");
            viewOrders.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewOrders.Columns["rating_id"], li);


            DataTable products = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductList(_server,false);
            RepositoryItemLookUpEdit pi = new RepositoryItemLookUpEdit();
            pi.PopulateGridLookup(products, "name", "id");
            viewOrders.SetRepositoryItemLookUpEdit(viewOrders.Columns["product_id"], pi);

            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            

            _orders.SetEditable(new string[] { "oface", "product", "ticker","buy_axe","rating_id", "tag", "level","account_id", "public", "private", "live", "publish", "colorgroup_id","publish_to","product_id","result_id", "sql_clause", "filter","axetype_id", "size"}, null);

            if(first_load || was_grouped)
            {
                HandleRowFormats();

            }
            
           
           
            
            first_load = false;
            SetPriorityColumns();
            if (null != respective_id)
            {
                viewOrders.SelectRowBasedOnID("order_id", respective_id);
            }

            if (null != respective_id && open_for_edit)
            {
                bool can_edit = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("can_edit");
                if (can_edit)
                {
                    viewOrders.ShowEditForm();
                }
            }
        }

        public void HandleRowFormats()
        {

            if(null == _orders._DataSet)
                return;



            _orders.HideColumn("colorgroup_id");
            _orders.HideColumn("live");
            _orders.HideColumn("publish");

            HandleHidePrivateNotes();

            viewOrders.Columns["product"].Group();
            viewOrders.Columns["order_type"].Group();
            viewOrders.ExpandAllGroups();
                
            

            
            
            
            SetPriorityColumns();

        }

        public void SetPriorityColumns()
        {
            
            {
                
                {
                    


                    int optimal_oface = viewOrders.CalcColumnBestWidth(viewOrders.Columns["oface"]);
                    _orders.SetWidth("oface", 75);

                    int optimal_size = viewOrders.CalcColumnBestWidth(viewOrders.Columns["size"]);
                    _orders.SetWidth("size", 100);

                    int optimal_size_label = viewOrders.CalcColumnBestWidth(viewOrders.Columns["size_label"]);
                    _orders.SetWidth("size_label", 100);


                    if (viewOrders.Columns["tag"].Visible)
                    {
                        int size = viewOrders.Columns["tag"].GetBestWidth();
                        _orders.SetWidth("tag", size);
                    }


                    
                    _orders.SetWidth("last_update", 70);
                    _orders.SetWidth("who", 25);


                    int optimal_public = viewOrders.CalcColumnBestWidth(viewOrders.Columns["public"]);

                    
                    

                    optimal_public = 500;
                    _orders.SetWidth("public", optimal_public);
                    

 

                   
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    

                    
                    
                    
                    
                }
            }

            
            
        }

        private void viewOrders_EditFormPrepared(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.EditFormPreparedEventArgs e)
        {

            object can_edit = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<object>("can_edit");
            ctrlAxe axe = (ctrlAxe)viewOrders.OptionsEditForm.CustomEditFormLayout;
            GridView view = sender as GridView;
            if (((DBNull.Value != can_edit && null != can_edit) && !System.Convert.ToBoolean(can_edit)))
            {
                
                {
                    foreach (object b in e.BindableControls)
                    {
                        BaseEdit be = b as BaseEdit;
                        if(null != be)
                            be.Properties.ReadOnly = true;
                        if(b.GetType() == typeof(FilterControl))
                        {
                            FilterControl fc = b as FilterControl;
                            
                        }
                    }
                }
                axe.LockForm();
            }
            object o = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<object>("product_id");
            if (null != o && DBNull.Value != o)
            {
                int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(o);
                bool supports_filter = BatCaveLib.Axe.SupportsFilter(product_id);

                axe.ToggleAddAxeVisible(supports_filter);
            }
            else
                axe.ToggleAddAxeVisible(false);

            string filter = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<string>("filter");
            axe.AddFilterString(filter);

            axe.Init(_server,_bat_signal);
            axe.Populate();

        }

        private void viewOrders_ValidateRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ValidateRowEventArgs e)
        {

            DataRow row = ((DataRowView)e.Row).Row;

            string public_note = row["public"].ToString();
            string private_note = row["private"].ToString();

            if(DBNull.Value == row["product_id"] || null == row["product_id"])
            {
                e.ErrorText = "You have to add a product";
                e.Valid = false;
                return;
            }

            if (DBNull.Value == row["axetype_id"])
            {
                e.ErrorText = "You have to add an axe type";
                e.Valid = false;
                return;
            }


            bool publish = false;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["publish"])
                publish = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["publish"]);


            Nullable<int> publish_to = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["publish_to"])
                publish_to = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["publish_to"]);


            if (publish && null == publish_to)
            {
                e.ErrorText = "If you're going to publish it it needs to be to a group";
                e.Valid = false;
                return;
            }


            string ticker_raw = row["ticker"].ToString();
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker_raw))
            {
                bool can_bbg_update = BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().session_started && BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().LIMIT_HIT == false;
                
                var ticker = Assets.MT.Ticker(_server, ticker_raw, can_bbg_update, true);

                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker) && can_bbg_update)
                {
                    e.ErrorText = "Ticker does not appear to be valid";
                    e.Valid = false;
                }
                else
                {
                    if(null != row["ticker"] && row["ticker"] != ticker)
                        row["ticker"] = ticker;
                }
            }
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
        

            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

        }


        public int UpdateRow(DataRow row)
        {
            string ticker = null;

            if (DBNull.Value != row["ticker"])
                ticker = row["ticker"].ToString();

            List<DataColumn> changed = row.GetChangedColumns();

            Nullable<double> oface = null;
            
            
            
            
            string size = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["size"])
                size = row["size"].ToString();

            
            {
                double d;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["size"])
                {
                    if (Double.TryParse(row["size"].ToString(), out d))
                    {
                        oface = d;
                    }
                }
            }


            string public_note = row["public"].ToString();
            string private_note = row["private"].ToString();
            Nullable<int> account_id = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["account_id"])
                account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]);
            bool publish = false;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["publish"])
                publish = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["publish"]);
            bool live = false;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["live"])
                live = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["live"]);
            int colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["colorgroup_id"]);

            Nullable<int> order_id = null;
            bool brand_new_order = (DBNull.Value == row["order_id"]);

            if (DBNull.Value != row["order_id"])
            {
                order_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["order_id"]);
            }


            int product_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["product_id"].ToString());

            string tag = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["tag"])
                tag = row["tag"].ToString();

            string level = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["level"])
                level = row["level"].ToString();

            Nullable<int> rating_id = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["rating_id"])
                rating_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["rating_id"]);

            Nullable<int> publish_to = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["publish_to"])
                publish_to = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["publish_to"]);

            Nullable<int> result_id = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["result_id"])
                result_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["result_id"]);

            string sql_clause = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["sql_clause"])
                sql_clause = row["sql_clause"].ToString();

            string filter = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["filter"])
                filter = row["filter"].ToString();


            bool can_publish_orders = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(_server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Permission.CAN_PUBLISH_ORDERS);

            if (!publish && can_publish_orders)
            {
                
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Your axe/order isn't published...\n\nPublish?", "Reminder...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
                {
                    publish = true;
                }
            }

            var prod = ctrlAxe.GetSettingsBasedOnProduct(product_id);
            if (prod.require_traders_on_unpublished && !can_publish_orders && publish)
            {
                publish = false;
                publish_to = null;
            }


            int? axetype_id = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["axetype_id"])
                axetype_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["axetype_id"]);
            order_id = BatCaveLib.Orders.InsertUpdateOrder(_server, order_id, ticker, oface, public_note, private_note, live, colorgroup_id, account_id, publish, tag, level, rating_id, publish_to, product_id, sql_clause, filter, result_id, axetype_id, size);
            row["order_id"] = order_id;
            if (null != account_id)
                row["account"] = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountNameUnsafeInternal(_server, account_id.Value, "name");
            string color = null;
            if (!publish)
                color = "Bisque";
            row["row_color"] = color;
            row["ticker"] = ticker;
            row["bid_ask"] = row["level"];

            string type = "New";
            if (changed.Count > 0)
                type = "Updated";
            string product = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductName(_server, product_id);
            string msg = $"{type} {product} Axe:  {ticker}  |  {tag}  |  SIZE: {size:0.00}";


            bool valid_ticker = UtilsLib.Validate.IsTicker(ticker);

            if (valid_ticker && null != row["level"])
            {
                string cusip = row["cusip"].ToString();
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cusip))
                {
                    cusip = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(_server, ticker, "cusip", false, false);
                }
                
                if (null != level)
                {
                    foreach (string l in level?.Split('/'))
                    {
                        BatCaveLib.KaneraiHelper.SubmitKaneraiPricingIfNeeded(_server, cusip, product_id, l.Trim());
                    }
                }
            }
            if (null != _bat_signal && publish && (null != publish_to && BatCaveLib.Color.GetPublicColorGroupId(_server) == publish_to.Value) && live)
            {
                
                
                {
                    if (product == "CORP")
                        tag = Assets.MT.GetAssetValueNullable<string>(_server, ticker, "sector", false, false);
                }
                AlertHelper ah = new AlertHelper(2, order_id, msg, public_note, public_note, new string[] { product }, Environment.UserName, false);
                
                

                
                
                

                _bat_signal.SendGeneric(ah);
                
            }
            if (!publish && prod.require_traders_on_unpublished && (brand_new_order || changed.Count > 0) && live)
            {
                string msg_vet = $"{type} AXE TO VET - {ticker}  |  {tag}  |  SIZE: {size:0.00} @ {level}";
                List<string> emails = BatCaveLib.Trades.WhoTrades<string>(_server, ticker, product_id, "email");
                List<string> usernames = BatCaveLib.Trades.WhoTrades<string>(_server, ticker, product_id, "username");
                UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail(null, _smtp_server, null, null);
                
                
                string to = String.Join(";", emails);
                string body = $"<<TO PUBLISH::   Open Cave - Hit 'Refresh' - Look for Orange/Pink Rows - Double Click - Make sure 'publish' is checked - hit 'Update'>> {Environment.NewLine}{Environment.NewLine}PUBLIC NOTE: {Environment.NewLine}{public_note} {Environment.NewLine} {Environment.NewLine}PRIVATE NOTE:{Environment.NewLine}{private_note}";
                string cc = UtilsLib.Mail.MyEmail;
                
                string bcc = BatCaveLib.Products.GetOrdersAxeBCC(_server, product_id);
                m.SendSMTPMail(to, cc, bcc, msg_vet, body, null, false, true, null, System.Net.Mail.MailPriority.Normal);


                if (null != _bat_signal)
                {
                    AlertHelper ah = new AlertHelper(2, order_id, msg_vet, msg, null, usernames, Environment.UserName, false);
                    _bat_signal.SendGeneric(ah);
                }
            }
            return order_id.Value;
        }

        private void viewOrders_RowUpdated(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.RowObjectEventArgs e)
        {
            
            DataRow row = ((DataRowView)e.Row).Row;
            

            int order_id = UpdateRow(row);

            RefreshTab(order_id,false);
        }

        private void viewOrders_InitNewRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.InitNewRowEventArgs e)
        {
            DataRow row = viewOrders.GetDataRow(e.RowHandle);
            row["live"] = true;
            row["publish"] = false;
            int? product_id = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValueNullable<int>("product_id", false);
            int default_colorgroup_id = BatCaveLib.Color.DefautlColorGroupId(_server, product_id);
            row["colorgroup_id"] = default_colorgroup_id;
            
            List<int> prods = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreference<int>(_server, 1);
            if (prods.Count > 0)
                row["product_id"] = prods[0];
            row["last_update"] = DateTime.Now;
            row["publish_to"] = CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.PUBLIC_COLOR_ID;
            
            
            
        }

        private void viewOrders_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {

            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row && !e.HitInfo.InGroupRow)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                
                if (viewOrders.SelectedRowsCount == 1)
                {
                    bool can_edit = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<bool>("can_edit");
                    if (can_edit)
                    {
                        DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem single = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Delete Order/Axe", this.DeleteOrderAxe);
                        single.BeginGroup = true;
                        menu.Items.Add(single);

                        DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem affirm = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Reaffirm Axe", this.ReaffirmAxe);
                        affirm.BeginGroup = true;
                        menu.Items.Add(affirm);
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        public void ReaffirmAxe(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int order_id = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<int>("order_id");
            BatCaveLib.Orders.ReAffirmOrder(_server, order_id);
            int[] handles = viewOrders.GetSelectedRows();
            foreach (int i in handles)
                viewOrders.SetRowCellValue(i,"last_update", DateTime.Now);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Updated: " + handles.Length + " orders/axes", "Done");
        }
        public void DeleteOrderAxe(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Are you sure you want to permanently delete this axe?  If the axe is no longer active you should uncheck 'Live' in the edit screen and it will still be in database for searching later.","Confirm",MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                int order_id = viewOrders.GetActiveRowValue<int>("order_id");
                BatCaveLib.Orders.DeleteOrder(_server, order_id);
                int[] handles = viewOrders.GetSelectedRows();
                foreach (int i in handles)
                    viewOrders.DeleteRow(i);
            }
        }

        private void viewOrders_GroupLevelStyle(object sender, GroupLevelStyleEventArgs e)
        {
            switch (e.Level)
            {
                case 0:
                    e.LevelAppearance.Options.UseBackColor = true;
                    e.LevelAppearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(31, 73, 125);
                    
                    break;
                case 1:
                    e.LevelAppearance.Options.UseBackColor = true;
                    e.LevelAppearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(141, 180, 226);
                    e.LevelAppearance.FontSizeDelta = -3;
                    
                    e.LevelAppearance.ForeColor = System.Drawing.Color.Navy;
                    
                    break;
                case 2:
                    e.LevelAppearance.Options.UseBackColor = true;
                    e.LevelAppearance.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.FromArgb(197, 217, 241);
                    break;
                default:
                    
                    break;

            }

        }

        public void PublishAll(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row && _orders.ContainsColumn("product_id"))
            {

                List<int> all_product_ids = _orders.GetSelectedRowList<int>("product_id");

                bool can_pub = CanPublishProducts(all_product_ids);
                if (can_pub)
                {
                    DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                    menu.BeginGroup = true;
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem single =
                        new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Publish ALL to PUBLIC", PublishAllNew);
                    menu.Items.Add(single);
                }

            }
        }

        public void PublishAllNew(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int total = viewOrders.GetSelectedRows().Count();
            DXETA eta = new DXETA(total, null, this.ParentForm);
            foreach (int i in viewOrders.GetSelectedRows())
            {
                DataRow row = ((DataRowView) viewOrders.GetRow(i)).Row;
                row["publish"] = 1;
                row["publish_to"] = BatCaveLib.Color.GetPublicColorGroupId(_server);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                UpdateRow(row);
                
            }
            XtraMessageBox.Show($"Updated {total} Bonds", "Done");
            List<int> selected_values = _orders.GetSelectedRowList<int>("order_id");
            int? row_to_refresh = null;
            if (selected_values.Count > 0)
                row_to_refresh = selected_values[0];
            RefreshTab(row_to_refresh, false);
        }

        public bool CanPublishProducts(List<int> product_ids)
        {
            bool can_publish = true;
            List<int> acceptable = BatCaveLib.Permissions.GetInclusiveAxeccessProducts(_server);
            foreach (int i in product_ids)
            {
                if (!acceptable.Contains(i))
                {
                    can_publish = false;
                    break;
                }
            }

            return can_publish;
        }

        }
        public void OfferBondBlast(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                

                DataTable formats = BWICBlastHelper.GetAllBlastFormats();
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem sub = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("Offer Blasts");
                sub.BeginGroup = true;
                
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem ib = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("IB");
                ib.BeginGroup = true;
                sub.Items.Add(ib);
                foreach(DataRow row in formats.Rows)
                {
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem single = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(row[0].ToString(), OfferBonds);
                    sub.Items.Add(single);

                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem single_ib = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem(row[0].ToString(), OfferBondsIB);
                    ib.Items.Add(single_ib);

                }
                
                menu.Items.Add(sub);
                
            }
        }


        private void OfferBonds(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            var v = sender as DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem;
            OfferBondsInternal(v.Caption, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT.BLAST);
        }
        private void OfferBondsIB(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            var v = sender as DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem;
            OfferBondsInternal(v.Caption, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT.IB);
        }

        private void OfferBondsInternal(string caption, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_MSG_FORMAT fmt)
        {
            
            BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt = BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.GetBlastTemplate(caption);
            DataTable tbl = _orders.GetUnderlyingTable(0);
            
            List<string> tickers = _orders.GetUniqueListInternal<string>("ticker", true, true, false, true, true, _orders.selected_row_order.ToArray());

            if (tickers.Contains(""))
                tickers.Remove("");
            if(tickers.Count == 0)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("You need to select the bonds you want to offer - hold control key down for multiple.");
                return;
            }
            string sql = String.Join("','", tickers);
            tbl = tbl.Select("ticker in ('" + sql + "')").CopyToDataTable();
            tbl = tbl.ReOrder<string>("ticker", tickers);



            AddAssetInfoDetails(_server, ref tbl, null);
            if (null == _bbg)
                _bbg = new UtilsLib.BBGDDE();

            BatCaveLib.BWICBlastHelper.BlastBBGInternal(_server, tbl, "OFFERS", null, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER, tickers, fmt, _bbg, bt, BWICBlastHelper.BLAST_BOND_SOURCE.ORDER);

        }



        public void AddAssetInfoDetails(string server, ref DataTable source_tbl,string csv_cols_to_add)
        {
            string t = source_tbl.UniqueValues<string>("ticker").Aggregate((current, next) => current + Environment.NewLine + next);
            DataSet tickers = BatCave.Color.SearchRaw(_server, t, this.ParentForm, false,null, false, false, false, false, false, false, false , false, false, false, false, false, false, false, false, false, false, null, false, false, false, false, false);
            if (null == csv_cols_to_add)
            {
                csv_cols_to_add = tickers.Tables[0].Columns.ToList().Select(n => n.ColumnName.ToLower()).Aggregate((current, next) => current + "," + next);
            }
            foreach(string col in csv_cols_to_add.Split(','))
            {
                if (!source_tbl.Columns.Contains(col))
                {
                    source_tbl.Columns.Add(col, tickers.Tables[0].Columns[0].DataType);
                    foreach (DataRow row in tickers.Tables[0].Rows)
                    {
                        DataRow[] bonds = source_tbl.Select("ticker = '" + row["ticker"] + "'");
                        foreach (DataRow b in bonds)
                        {
                            b[col] = row[col];
                        }
                    }
                }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlPnL.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlPnL : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlPnL()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        GridHelper _interest;
        GridHelper _trades;
        GridHelper _remits;
        GridHelper _summary;
        private SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _interest = new GridHelper(gridInterest, _server, true, _bat_signal );
            _trades = new GridHelper(gridTrades, _server, true, _bat_signal );
            _remits = new GridHelper(gridRemits, _server, true, _bat_signal );
            _summary = new GridHelper(gridSummary, _server, true, _bat_signal );
        }
        private void labelControl1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void labelControl2_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void labelControl4_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        bool first_load = true;
        private void ctrlPL_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            viewFunding.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewSummary.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewRemits.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;
            viewTrades.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;

            _remits.ShowGroupPanel(false);
            _summary.ShowGroupPanel(false);
            _interest.ShowGroupPanel(false);
            _trades.ShowGroupPanel(false);
        }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
    
        }

        private void btnGo_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            string cusip = txtCusip.Text;
            int book = System.Convert.ToInt32(txtBook.Text);
            DateTime start = dtStart.DateTime;
            DateTime end = dtEnd.DateTime;

            DataSet set = BatCaveLib.PnL.GetBreakdown(_server, cusip, book, start, end);
            _interest.SetGrid(set.Tables[0]);
            _trades.SetGrid(set.Tables[1]);
            _remits.SetGrid(set.Tables[2]);
            _summary.SetGrid(set.Tables[3]);


            if (first_load)
            {
                string format = "{0:###,##0}";
                viewFunding.Columns["cost_of_funds"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "cost_of_funds", format);
                viewTrades.Columns["oface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "oface", format);
                viewTrades.Columns["principal"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "principal", format);
                viewTrades.Columns["accrued_interest"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "accrued_interest", format);
                viewTrades.Columns["commission"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "commission", format);

                viewRemits.Columns["principal"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "principal", format);
                viewRemits.Columns["coupon"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "coupon", format);

                viewSummary.Columns["amount"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum,"amount", format);



                first_load = true;
            }

        }

        private void labelControl7_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }
    }
}

        public void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _summary = new GridHelper(grdMarkRequests, _server, false, _bat_signal);
            _detail = new GridHelper(gridDetail, _server,true, _bat_signal);
            _breakdown = new GridHelper(gridBreakdown, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _breakdown_two = new GridHelper(gridBreakdownTwo, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _breakdown_three = new GridHelper(gridBreakdownThree, _server, true, _bat_signal);
            _summary.SetGridMultiSelect(true);
            viewSummary.OptionsBehavior.ReadOnly = true;
            viewSummary.OptionsBehavior.Editable = false;
            
            
            _summary.AppendPopup(viewSummary, CustomPortfolioPopup);

            

            ctrlFilter.Resize(200,125);
            ctrlFilter.MultiColumn(true);
            
            ctrlFilter.SetGridFilterField("bond_label_1");
            ctrlFilter.SetBorder(DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.BorderStyles.NoBorder);
            ctrlFilter.SetPostFilterChangeOperation(SetProductColumns);

            viewBreakdownTwo.OptionsView.ShowFooter = true;


        }
