        public void ComparePortfoliosSameWindow(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ComparePortfoliosInternal(false);
        }

        public void ComparePortfoliosNewWindow(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ComparePortfoliosInternal(true);
        }

        public void SetProductColumns()
        {
            if (_detail.ContainsColumn("change_in_oface"))
            {
                string format = GetCompareFormats();
                _detail.SetVisibleColumns(format, true, false, false);
            }
        }

        public string GetCompareFormats()
        {
            int? product_id = _detail.GetProductIdFromGrid("product_id", .7, true);
            
            string format = BatCaveLib.Utils.DefaultFormats(_server, "default", product_id, null);
            var reorder_split = format.Split(',').ToList();
            reorder_split.ReOrderAfter("bond_label_2", "oface");
            reorder_split.ReOrderAfter("oface", "cface");
            reorder_split.ReOrderAfter("cface", "change_in_oface");
            string new_format = String.Join(",", reorder_split.ToArray());
            return new_format;
        }

        public void ComparePortfoliosInternal(bool new_window)
        {
            List<int> portfolios = _summary.GetSelectedRowList<int>("portfolio_id");
            DataSet delta = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.GetPortfolioCompare(_server, portfolios[0], portfolios[1]);
            DataSet detail = new DataSet();
            detail.Tables.Add(delta.Tables[1].Copy());
            DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView f = new DXHelper.Forms.frmQuickView();
            f.Init(_server,_bat_signal);
            string new_format = GetCompareFormats();
            

            _breakdown.SetGrid(delta.Tables[4]);
            _breakdown_two.SetGrid(delta.Tables[2]);
            _breakdown_three.SetGrid(delta.Tables[3]);
            viewBreakdownTwo.Columns["change_in_oface"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "change_in_oface", "TOTAL: {0:0.000}");
            viewBreakdownTwo.Columns["#_bonds"].Summary.Add(DevExpress.Data.SummaryItemType.Sum, "#_bonds", "# {0:0}");
            
            if (new_window)
            {
                f.Populate(detail.Tables[0], new_format);
                f.ToggleMinimizeButton(true);
                f.SetCustomSort("type", "sort_rank");
                f.ToggleAutoFilterRow(true);
                f.SetColumnColor("change_in_oface", System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow);
                f.SetColumnColor("oface", System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow);
                f.SetColumnColor("cface", System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow);
                f.BoldColumn("oface");
                f.BoldColumn("cface");
                f.BoldColumn("change_in_oface");

                f.SetSize(null, 800);
                f.ToggleGroupBy(true);
                f.GroupBySingle("type");
                f.ExpandAllGroupBy();
                f.Show();
            }
            else
            {
                _detail.SetGrid(detail, new_format);
                _detail.SetCustomSort("type", "sort_rank");
                _detail.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
                _detail.BoldColumn("oface");
                _detail.BoldColumn("cface");
                _detail.BoldColumn("change_in_oface");
                _detail.ToggleGroupBy(true);
                viewDetail.Columns["oface"].AppearanceCell.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow;
                viewDetail.Columns["cface"].AppearanceCell.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow;
                viewDetail.Columns["change_in_oface"].AppearanceCell.BackColor = System.Drawing.Color.LightYellow;
                viewDetail.Columns["type"].Group();
                viewDetail.ExpandAllGroups();
            }

        }


        bool first_load = true;
        public void RefreshTab(Nullable<int> portfolio_id)
        {
            _detail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            

            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);
            drpAccounts.PopulateLookup(accounts, new string[] { "name", "cover"}, "account_id", false,550,null,null,null,true);


            string csv = "account_id,NONAGENCY,CMBS,CDO/CLO,ABS,CORP,MUNI,AGENCY PT,GOVT,SBC,MBS CMO,OTHER,TOTAL_BONDS,portfolio_type,loaded_by,asOf";
            DataTable summary = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.GetPortfolioSummary(_server);
            _summary.SetGrid(summary,csv);
            
            _summary.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
            _summary.SetWidth("account_id", 350);
            if (viewSummary.SelectedRowsCount == 0 && viewSummary.RowCount > 0)
                viewSummary.SelectRow(0);
            
            if(null == portfolio_id && (viewSummary.SourceRowHandle >= 0 || viewSummary.FocusedRowHandle == 0))
                portfolio_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("portfolio_id");
            if (null != portfolio_id)
                viewSummary.SelectRowBasedOnID("portfolio_id", portfolio_id);


        }



        public void SetActiveFilterSafeCustom(CriteriaOperator filter)
        {

            int checked_items = ctrlFilter.CheckedItemCount;
            bool all_checked = ctrlFilter.AllCheckedItems;

            _detail.BeginViewUpdate();
            if (checked_items == 0 || all_checked)
            {
                _detail.ExpandWhenFilterChanged(true);
            }
            else
            {
                _detail.ExpandWhenFilterChanged(true);
            }
            bool was_grouped = viewDetail.GroupCount > 0;

            


            _detail.SetActiveFilterSafe(filter);

            

            {
                

            }

            _detail.EndViewUpdate();

        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpAccounts.EditValue);
            DateTime asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(dtDueTime.EditValue);

            bool exists = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.PortfolioExists(_server, asOf, account_id);
            if(exists)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Portfolio already exists for this account and date.  Proceed?", "Oops..", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo,MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                if(dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                {
                    return;
                }
            }

            int portfolio_id = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.InsertUpdatePortfolio(_server, account_id, asOf, txtNotes.Text, null,chkEnableAlerts.Checked,null,1);

            DXETA eta = new DXETA(-1, null,this.ParentForm);
            var bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(_server, txtBonds.Text, '\n',true,false,false,eta);
            eta = new DXETA(bonds.matched_count, null, this.ParentForm);
            foreach (Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper bond in bonds.matched_list)
            {
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                BatCaveLib.Portfolios.InsertPortfolioDetail(_server, portfolio_id, bond.ticker, bond.oface, null, null);
            }
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Portfolio ID: " + portfolio_id, "Done");
            CreateClearCreate();
            RefreshTab(portfolio_id);
        }




        private void CreateClearCreate()
        {
            txtNotes.EditValue = null;
            txtBonds.EditValue = null;
            drpAccounts.EditValue = null;
            
            chkEnableAlerts.EditValue = false;
            
        }

        private void ValidateSaveButton()
        {
            bool enable = false;

            if (null != drpAccounts.EditValue && null != dtDueTime.EditValue && null != txtBonds.EditValue)
                enable = true;
            btnSave.Enabled = enable;
            btnValidateBonds.Enabled = enable;
        }

        private void drpAccounts_Properties_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            ValidateSaveButton();
        }

        private void txtBonds_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

            PopulateFunds(account_id);
        }

        }

        private void btnValidateBonds_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            var bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(_server, txtBonds.Text, '\n',true,false,true);
            if (bonds.notmatched.Count == 0)
                XtraMessageBox.Show("All Bonds Validated", "Great Success!");
            else
                XtraMessageBox.Show(String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.notmatched), "Oops...");

        }

        DataSet _results = null;
        private string _format;
        private void PopulatePortfolioDetail(int id)
        {
            _results = BatCaveLib.Portfolios.GetPortfolioDetail(_server, id);

            _format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "default", _results.Tables[0], "product_id");
            
            _detail.SetGrid(_results, _format);
            _breakdown.SetGrid(null);
            _breakdown_two.SetGrid(null);
            _breakdown_three.SetGrid(null);




            
            {
                var v = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(_server, false);
                ctrlFilter.SetFilterUpdate(SetActiveFilterSafeCustom);

                ctrlFilter.SetPreferred(v);
                SortedDictionary<string, string> prods = BatCaveLib.Products.ProcessProducts(_results.Tables[0], "bond_label_1");
                ctrlFilter.PopulateBoxes(prods);
                
                
                ctrlFilter.ToggleCheckVisibility(false);
            }

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        string asOfFormat = "M/d/yyyy";

        private void gridView2_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {

            int[] selected_row = viewSummary.GetSelectedRows();

            if (selected_row.Length == 1)
            {
                if (viewSummary.IsFilterRow(selected_row[0]))
                    return;
            }
            else if (selected_row.Length == 0)
            {
                return;
            }
            _detail.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            if (selected_row.Length == 1)
            {
                int id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("portfolio_id");
                PopulatePortfolioDetail(id);
            }
        }

        public void DeletePortfolio(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int portfolio_id = viewSummary.GetActiveRowValue<int>("portfolio_id");
            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("Are you sure you want to completely delete this portfolio?", "Just checking...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo);
            if(dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                BatCaveLib.Portfolios.DeletePortfolio(_server, portfolio_id);
                RefreshTab();
            }
        }

        private void btnAddColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(this.ParentForm, false, false, null, null);

            
            _detail.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, _format, true, false,null,false,null,false,false,false, true, true, true);
            SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
        }

        private void viewSummary_PopupMenuShowing(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {


            if (e.MenuType == DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridMenuType.Row)
            {


                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                menu.Items.Clear();


                List<int> portfolios = _summary.GetSelectedRowList<int>("portfolio_id");
                if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row && portfolios.Count == 2)
                {

                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem twist =
                        new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXSubMenuItem("Compare Portfolios");


                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item_three =
                        new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("New Window", this.ComparePortfoliosNewWindow);
                    DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item_tew =
                        new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Current Window", this.ComparePortfoliosSameWindow);
                    twist.Items.Add(item_tew);
                    twist.Items.Add(item_three);
                    menu.Items.Add(twist);
                }

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem manage_item =  new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Delete Portfolio", this.DeletePortfolio);
                manage_item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(manage_item);
            }
        }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlReports.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlReports : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlReports()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }



        public string _server;
        public GridHelper _grid;
        FilteringUIContext _filter;
        FilteringUIContext _accountColorFilter;
        public GridHelper _gh_accounts;
        bool first_load = true;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server,BatSignalLib.SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid = new GridHelper(gridDetail, server, true, _bat_signal);
            _gh_accounts = new GridHelper(grdAccounts, server, true, _bat_signal);

            RefreshAccountColorFilterFilters();
            RefreshAssetFilterFilters();

            DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.AccordionContentContainer container = new AccordionContentContainer();
            container.MaximumSize = new System.Drawing.Size(0, 60);
            accordionControl1.Controls.Add(container);

            ctrlProductFilter.ToggleCheckVisibility(false);
            ctrlProductFilter.Resize(null, 525);
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            

        }


        private void RefreshAssetFilterFilters()
        {

            DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.AccordionContentContainer container = new AccordionContentContainer();
            
            _filter = new FilteringUIContext(this.components);
            _filter.ModelType = typeof(BondFilters);
            _filter.FilterCriteriaChanged += filteringUIContext1_FilterCriteriaChanged;
            _filter.QueryLookupData += filteringUIContext1_QueryLookupData;
            _filter.Control = accordionControl1;

            accordionControl1.ShowFilterControl = ShowFilterControl.Always;    
          }

        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            if (first_load)
            {
                var v = BatCaveLib.Products.GetAllProductList(_server,false,"name",true);
                ctrlProductFilter.PopulateBoxes(v);
                List<string> prefs = BatCaveLib.Products.GetPreferredProductNames(_server,false);
                ctrlProductFilter.SetPreferred(prefs);
                ctrlProductFilter.ToggleCheckVisibility(false);
                first_load = false;
            }
        }



        private void RefreshAccountColorFilterFilters()
        {
           
            _accountColorFilter = new FilteringUIContext(this.components);
            _accountColorFilter.ModelType = typeof(AccountColorFilters);
            _accountColorFilter.FilterCriteriaChanged += _accountColorFilter_FilterCriteriaChanged;
            _accountColorFilter.QueryLookupData += _accountColorFilter_QueryLookupData;
            _accountColorFilter.Control = accordionControl2;
        }

        private void _accountColorFilter_QueryLookupData(object sender, QueryLookupDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "account")
            {
                List<string> account = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("account");
                e.Result.DataSource = account;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "color_type")
            {
                List<string> color_types = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("color_type");
                e.Result.DataSource = color_types;
            }
        }

        private void _accountColorFilter_FilterCriteriaChanged(object sender, FilterCriteriaChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            gridDetail.MainView().ActiveFilterCriteria = _accountColorFilter.FilterCriteria;
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        private void btnCoverage_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        
        
        
  
        
        
        
        
        

        

        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
            
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
           

        
        
        

        

        public partial class AccountColorFilters
        {
            const string Main = "Account / Color Filters";
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "account", UseSelectAll =true, NullName = "No Account Associated")]
            public string account { get; set; }

            [Display(Name = "Color Types")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "color_type", UseSelectAll = true)]
            public string color_type { get; set; }


        }
            public partial class BondFilters
        {
            const string Main = "Bond Filters";


            [Display(Name = "Bond Type")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "bond_label_1")]
            public string bond_label_2 { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Asset Class")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "bond_label_1")]
            public string bond_label_1 { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Wrap")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "wrap")]
            public string wrap { get; set; }

            [Display(Name = "Rating")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "rating_ig",NullName = "Not Rated")]
            public string rating_ig { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Detatchment")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "detatch")]
            [FilterRange(0, 100, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double detatch { get; set; }

            [Display(Name = "Current Credit Enhancement")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "cce")]
            [FilterRange(0, 100, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double cce { get; set; }



            [Display(Name = "Coupon")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "cpn")]
            [FilterRange(0, 100, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double cpn { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "NAIC 1")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "naic_1")]
            [FilterRange(0, 120, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double naic_1 { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Has NAIC1")]
            [FilterBooleanChoice(false)]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "has_naic_1")]
            public bool has_naic_1 { get; set; }

            [Display(Name = "DLQ 60+")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "dlq_60p")]
            [FilterRange(0, 100, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double dlq_60p { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Loan Count")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "ln_cnt")]
            [DisplayFormat(DataFormatString = "{0:###,##0}")]
            [FilterRange(1, 15000, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public double ln_cnt { get; set; }

            [Display(Name = "Vintage")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "vintage")]
            [DisplayFormat(DataFormatString = "{0:0}")]
            [FilterRange(1985, 2017, EditorType = RangeUIEditorType.Spin)]
            public int vintage { get; set; }


            [Display(Name = "Shelf",AutoGenerateFilter =true)]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "shelf", SelectAllName = "All Shelves", MaxCountMember = "30")]
            public string shelf { get; set; }

            
            
            

        }

        private void filteringUIContext1_FilterCriteriaChanged(object sender, FilterCriteriaChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            gridDetail.MainView().ActiveFilterCriteria = _filter.FilterCriteria;
        }

        private void filteringUIContext1_QueryLookupData(object sender, QueryLookupDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "bond_label_1")
            {
                List<string> bond_label_1 = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_1");
                e.Result.DataSource = bond_label_1;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "bond_label_2")
            {
                List<string> bond_label_2 = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_2");
                e.Result.DataSource = bond_label_2;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "shelf")
            {
                List<string> shelf = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("shelf");
                e.Result.DataSource = shelf;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "wrap")
            {
                List<string> wrap = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("wrap");
                e.Result.DataSource = wrap;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "rating_ig")
            {
                List<string> rating_ig = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("rating_ig");
                e.Result.DataSource = rating_ig;
            }

        }

        private void hideContainerBottom_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void _filter_QueryRangeData(object sender, QueryRangeDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "ln_cnt")
            {
                List<int> list = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<int>("ln_cnt");
                int min = list.Min();
                int max = list.Max();
                e.Result.Minimum = min;
                e.Result.Maximum = max;
            }
        }

        {

        }

        private void btnResetFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            _filter.ClearFilterCriteria();
            _grid.ClearAutoFilter();
            rdGrpResults.Enabled = false;
            txtBondFilter.EditValue = null;
            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        private bool ExpandedTickerFilter = false;
        private bool ExpandedColorAccountFilter = false;

        private DataSet _filter_ds = null;

        
        private void btnBondFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            rdGrpResults.EditValue = "tickers";
            string raw_bonds = txtBondFilter.Text;
            _filter.ClearFilterCriteria();
            _grid.ClearAutoFilter();
            
            List<int> account_filters = _gh_accounts.GetSelectedRowList<int>("account_id");
           
            
            
            if (!chkUseAccountFilter.Checked)
                account_filters.Clear();

            bool include_bids = (chkColorTypes.Items["bids"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_bwics = (chkColorTypes.Items["bwics"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_portfolios = (chkColorTypes.Items["portfolios"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_color = (chkColorTypes.Items["color"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_trace = (chkColorTypes.Items["trace"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_matchers = (chkColorTypes.Items["matchers"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_trades = (chkColorTypes.Items["trades"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_scratchpad = (chkColorTypes.Items["scratchpad"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_memarks = (chkColorTypes.Items["memarks"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_orders = (chkColorTypes.Items["orders"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_news = (chkColorTypes.Items["news"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_malls = (chkColorTypes.Items["malls"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_new_issue_px = (chkColorTypes.Items["include_new_issue_px"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_offers = (chkColorTypes.Items["offer"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_ooc_bids = (chkColorTypes.Items["ooc_bids"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);

            List<int> products = ctrlProductFilter.GetSelectedProducts(_server);
            bool include_color_table = true;

            bool anything_selected = (products.Count > 0 || account_filters.Count > 0 || txtBondFilter.Text.Length > 0); 

            if (!anything_selected)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You don't have any accounts/product types/bonds as criteria\n\nYou sure you want to do this search? Will take ~5 min", "Just making sure....",MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                if (dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                    return;
            }


            DataSet tickers = BatCave.Color.SearchRaw(_server, raw_bonds, this.ParentForm, true, account_filters, include_bids, include_bwics, include_color, include_trace, include_portfolios, include_matchers,true,include_trades,true,true,false,false,include_scratchpad, include_memarks, include_orders, include_news, include_malls,products, include_color_table, true, include_new_issue_px, include_offers, include_ooc_bids);
            _filter_ds = tickers;
            string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "big_search", tickers.Tables[0], "product_id");
            _grid.SetGrid(_filter_ds, column_format);
            _grid.ApplyNewColor(tickers, false, null, column_format, false, true, false);
            

            
            rdGrpResults.Enabled = true;
            btnAddColor.Visible = tickers.Tables[0].Rows.Count > 0;
            
            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        
        
        
        
                
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        

        

        private void ctrlReports_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("FOSTER"))
            {
                txtBondFilter.Text = "04541GMR0\r\n004421GM9\r\n004421KL6\r\n";
                txtBondFilter.Text = Utils.SampleCusips20();
            }

            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(_server);
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            _gh_accounts.SetGrid(accounts,"name,type");

            

            
            viewAccounts.OptionsSelection.MultiSelectMode = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridMultiSelectMode.CheckBoxRowSelect;
            
            
            viewAccounts.ClearSelection();
            grdAccounts.MainView().Columns["name"].OptionsFilter.FilterPopupMode = DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.FilterPopupMode.CheckedList;
            
        }




        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
                 
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
                
        

        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
   

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
            
        
        

        private DialogResult ThrowOutFiltered(DataSet set)
        {

            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You have filtered rows - Throw those way and only show color on the filtered table?\n\n(Recommend: YES)", "Question...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                List<string> tickers = viewSearch.GetFilteredData<string>("ticker");

                DataSet s = _grid._DataSet.Copy();
                s.RemoveRowsNotIn<string>("ticker", tickers);
                string format = _grid.GetVisibleCSVString();
                _grid.SetGrid(s, format);


 
            }
            if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
            {
                return dr;
            }
            return dr;
        }

        {

        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)

            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        private void checkEdit1_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            grdAccounts.Enabled = chkUseAccountFilter.Checked;
            chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Enabled = chkUseAccountFilter.Checked;
            if (!chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Enabled)
            {
                chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Checked = false;
                grdAccounts.MainView().ClearSelection();
                grdAccounts.MainView().ClearColumnsFilter();
            }

        }


        private void dockManager1_StartDocking(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.Docking.DockPanelCancelEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Cancel = true;
        }

        private void rdGrpResults_EditValueChanging(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ChangingEventArgs e)
        {

            HandleToggle(e.NewValue.ToString());
            
            
        }

        public void HandleToggle(string val)
        {
            
            
            if (_grid.AnyRowsFiltered())
            {
                DialogResult dr = ThrowOutFiltered(_grid._DataSet);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
                    return;
            }
            if (null == val || (null != val && val == "tickers"))
            {
                _grid.TwistOrig(null, null);
            }
            else
            {
                _grid.TwistColor(null, null);
            }
        }

        private void btnClear_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            chkColorTypes.UnCheckAll();
        }

        private void btnClearBondFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            txtBondFilter.EditValue = null;
        }

        private void chkColorTypes_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void rdGrpResults_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void btnAddColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_grid.AnyRowsFiltered())
            {
                DialogResult dr = ThrowOutFiltered(_grid._DataSet);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
                    return;
            }
            string current_format = _grid.CurrentColumnVisible;
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(this.ParentForm, false, false, null, null);
            bool toggle = false;
            if (rdGrpResults.EditValue.ToString() != "tickers")
                toggle = true;
            if(toggle)
                _grid.TwistOrig(null, null);
            _grid.AddColorInternal(true, true, null, current_format, true, false, true, null, true, true, false, false, false, true, true, true);
            if (toggle)
                _grid.TwistColor(null, null);
            SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
        }


        
        
        
        
        

        
    }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Controls\ctrlScratchpad.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlScratchpad : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlScratchpad()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        string _server;
        GridHelper _grid;
        GridHelper _bottom;
        private Delegates.TabSwitcher _ts;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server, Delegates.TabSwitcher tab_switch, SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _ts = tab_switch;
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid = new GridHelper(mainControl, _server, true, bat_signal);
            _grid.AppendPopup(mainControl.MainView(), _view_ScratchPadAddColor);
            _bottom = new GridHelper(gridBottom, _server, true, bat_signal);
            _grid.SetGridMultiSelect(true);
            _grid.ToggleAutoFilter(true);
        }

        private void _view_ScratchPadAddColor(object sender, PopupMenuShowingEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.MenuType == GridMenuType.Row)
            {
                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu = e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Transfer Scratchpad Notes to Color Notes", this.TransferToColor);
                item.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(item);

                DevExpress.XtraGrid.Menu.GridViewMenu menu_tew= e.Menu as GridViewMenu;
                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem item_tew = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Transfer to Order", this.TransferToOrder);
                item_tew.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(item_tew);

                DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem inactive = new DevExpress.Utils.Menu.DXMenuItem("Mark Inactive", this.MarkInactive);
                inactive.BeginGroup = true;
                menu.Items.Add(inactive);
            }
        }

        private void MarkInactive(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<int> scratch_ids = _grid.GetSelectedRowList<int>("scratch_id");
            foreach (int i in scratch_ids)
            {
             
                BatCaveLib.ScratchPad.ToggleActive(_server, i, false);
            }

            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void TransferToColor(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int scratch_id = _grid.GetActiveRowValue<int>("scratch_id");
            BatCaveLib.ScratchPad.TransferScratchPad(_server, scratch_id);
            XtraMessageBox.Show("Done!");
        }

        private void TransferToOrder(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            int scratch_id = _grid.GetActiveRowValue<int>("scratch_id");
            int order_id = BatCaveLib.Orders.TransferToOrder(_server, scratch_id);
            if (null != _ts)
            {
                
                _ts(2, order_id);
            }

            
        }
        
        public void RefreshTab()
        {
            _grid.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            int colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpColorGroups.EditValue);
            bool include_all = chkIncludeAll.Checked;
            DataTable t = BatCaveLib.ScratchPad.GetTable(_server, colorgroup_id, include_all);
            
            IEnumerable<string> last_updated_by = t.UniqueValues<string>("last_update_by");
            
            
            

            string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "scratchpad",t, "product_id");

            _grid.SetGrid(t, column_format, null, null, false,null,false);
            if (last_updated_by.Count() == 1)
            {
                _grid.HideColumn("last_update_by");
             
            }
            _grid.SetEditable(new string[] { "ticker", "notes", "active", "oface", "scratchpriority_id","account_id", "tag", "level"}, null);

            DataTable accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(_server);

            DataTable scratch = BatCaveLib.ScratchPad.GetPriorities(_server);
            _grid.SetUpDropdown(scratch, "scratchpriority_id", "name", "id");
            
            _grid.SetUpDropdown(accounts, "account_id", "name", "account_id");
            
            


            
            _bottom.CancelAnyAsyncQueries();
            PopulateStandardGrid(t);
            
            ApplyCustomGridFormats();

        }


        public void PopulateStandardGrid(DataTable grid)
        {
            List<string> tickers = grid.GetUniqueList<string>("ticker");
            string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "default", grid, "product_id");
            
            DataSet t = BatCaveLib.Color.SearchBase(_server, tickers, null);
            _bottom.SetGrid(t, column_format);
            

            if (tickers.Count != 0)
                _bottom.AddColorInternal(tickers, true, true, null, column_format, true, false, true, ExpandActiveTicker, true, true, false,false, false, true, true, true);
        }

        private void ApplyCustomGridFormats()
        {
            RepositoryItemMemoExEdit me = new RepositoryItemMemoExEdit();
            me.WordWrap = true;
            
            me.ValidateOnEnterKey = true;
            me.ShowIcon = false;
            me.PopupFormMinSize = new Size(300, 0);
            me.AcceptsTab = true;
            me.ScrollBars = ScrollBars.Vertical;
            me.MaxLength = 1250;
            me.AutoHeight = true;
            mainView.SetRepositoryItemMemoExEdit(mainView.Columns["notes"], me);
            
            

            
            

            _grid.SetWidth("notes", 700);
            
            _grid.SetWidth("added", 75);
            _grid.SetWidth("rating_worst", 60);
            _grid.SetWidth("bond_label_2", 120);
            _grid.SetWidth("ticker", 120);
            _grid.SetWidth("account_id", 70);
            _grid.SetWidth("oface", 50);
            _grid.SetWidth("cface", 50);
            _grid.SetWidth("scratchpriority_id", 70);
            _grid.SetWidth("last_update", 50);
            _grid.SetWidth("last_update_by", 70);
            
            _grid.SetWidth("active", 60);
            
        }
        
        
        private void mainView_ValidateRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.ValidateRowEventArgs e)
        {
            
            
            {
                try
                {
                    DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView v = sender as DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView;
                    
                    string ticker_in_grid = v.GetRowValue<string>("ticker", e.RowHandle);

                    if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker_in_grid))
                    {
                        e.ErrorText = "Ticker is invalid...";
                        e.Valid = false;
                        return;
                    }

                    string ticker = Assets.MT.Ticker(_server, ticker_in_grid, true, false);
                    string note = v.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle,"notes");
                    string oface_str = v.GetRowValue<string>("oface", e.RowHandle);
                    Nullable<int> scratchpriority_id = v.GetRowValueNullable<int>(e.RowHandle,"scratchpriority_id");
                    bool active = v.GetRowValue<bool>("active", e.RowHandle);
                    Nullable<int> scratch_id = null;
                    Nullable<double> oface = null;
                    Nullable<int> account_id = v.GetRowValueNullable<int>(e.RowHandle, "account_id");
                    string level = v.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle,"level");

                    string s = v.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle,"scratch_id");
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(s))
                        scratch_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(s);
                    if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(oface_str))
                        oface = System.Convert.ToDouble(oface_str);
                    
                    
                  
                    int colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(drpColorGroups.EditValue);

                    string tag  = v.GetRowValue<string>(e.RowHandle,"tag");

                    int id = BatCaveLib.ScratchPad.InsertUpdateScratchPad(_server, ticker, note, active, scratch_id, oface, scratchpriority_id, colorgroup_id, account_id,tag,level);
                    v.SetRowCellValue(e.RowHandle,"scratch_id", id);

                    
                    e.Valid = true;
                    RefreshTab();
                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    XtraMessageBox.Show(n.Message,"Error with input...");
                }
            }
        }

        private void mainView_InitNewRow(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.InitNewRowEventArgs e)
        {
            DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView v = sender as DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Grid.GridView;
            v.SetFocusedRowCellValue("active", true);
            
        }

        private bool loading = false;
        private void ctrlScratchpad_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            loading = true;
            
            int? product_id = _grid.GetActiveRowValue<int>("product_id", false);
            int colorgroup_id = BatCaveLib.Color.GetDefaultColorGroup<int>(_server, "colorgroup_id",product_id);
            

            DataTable color_groups = BatCaveLib.Color.GetMyColorGroups(_server,false);
            drpColorGroups.PopulateLookup(color_groups, new string[] { "name", "who" }, "colorgroup_id",false, CommonInterfaces.Constants.BatCave.COLORGROUP_DROPDOWN_WIDTH);
            drpColorGroups.EditValue = colorgroup_id;
            loading = false;
        }

        private void btnAddColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _grid.AddColorAsync(true, true, null, null, true, false, ApplyCustomGridFormats,true,true, false,false, false, true, true,true);
        }

        private void ExpandActiveTicker()
        {
            string ticker = _grid.GetFocusedRowValue<string>("ticker");
            
            string filter = "[TICKER] = '" + ticker + "'";
            _bottom.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(filter);
            _bottom.FindAndExpand("ticker", ticker,true);
        }

        private void mainView_SelectionChanged(object sender, DevExpress.Data.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            
        }

        private void drpColorGroups_EditValueChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if(!loading)
                RefreshTab();
        }

        private void btnRefresh_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }

        private void mainView_FocusedRowChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.FocusedRowChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            ExpandActiveTicker();
        }

        private void chkIncludeAll_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshTab();
        }
    }
}

        private void btnScrape_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            List<string> clos = GetAllCLOs(_server);
            UtilsLib.ETA eta = new UtilsLib.ETA(clos.Count, Console.WriteLine);
    

            int max = 10;
            if (clos.Count > max)
                clos.RemoveRange(max, clos.Count - max);

            
           

            foreach (string t in clos)
            {
                System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine(t);
                Assets.MT.GetOCTerminalData(_server, t);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
  
        }

        private void gridView1_MouseDown(object sender, MouseEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView view = sender as GridView;
            downHitInfo = null;

            GridHitInfo hitInfo = view.CalcHitInfo(new Point(e.X, e.Y));
            if (Control.ModifierKeys != Keys.None)
                return;
            if (e.Button == MouseButtons.Left && hitInfo.InRow && hitInfo.RowHandle != GridControl.NewItemRowHandle)
                downHitInfo = hitInfo;
        }

        private void gridView1_MouseMove(object sender, MouseEventArgs e)
        {
            GridView view = sender as GridView;
            if (e.Button == MouseButtons.Left && downHitInfo != null)
            {
                Size dragSize = SystemInformation.DragSize;
                Rectangle dragRect = new Rectangle(new Point(downHitInfo.HitPoint.X - dragSize.Width / 2,
                    downHitInfo.HitPoint.Y - dragSize.Height / 2), dragSize);

                if (!dragRect.Contains(new Point(e.X, e.Y)))
                {
                    view.GridControl.DoDragDrop(downHitInfo, DragDropEffects.All);
                    downHitInfo = null;
                }
            }
        }

        private void gridView1_DragObjectOver(object sender, DevExpress.XtraGrid.Views.Base.DragObjectOverEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void gridControl1_DragOver(object sender, DragEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.Data.GetDataPresent(typeof(GridHitInfo)))
            {
                GridHitInfo downHitInfo = e.Data.GetData(typeof(GridHitInfo)) as GridHitInfo;
                if (downHitInfo == null)
                    return;

                GridControl grid = sender as GridControl;
                GridView view = grid.MainView as GridView;
                GridHitInfo hitInfo = view.CalcHitInfo(grid.PointToClient(new Point(e.X, e.Y)));
                if (hitInfo.InRow && hitInfo.RowHandle != downHitInfo.RowHandle && hitInfo.RowHandle != GridControl.NewItemRowHandle)
                    e.Effect = DragDropEffects.Move;
                else
                    e.Effect = DragDropEffects.None;
            }
        }

        private void gridControl1_DragDrop(object sender, DragEventArgs e)
        {
            GridControl grid = sender as GridControl;
            GridView view = grid.MainView as GridView;
            GridHitInfo srcHitInfo = e.Data.GetData(typeof(GridHitInfo)) as GridHitInfo;
            GridHitInfo hitInfo = view.CalcHitInfo(grid.PointToClient(new Point(e.X, e.Y)));
            int sourceRow = srcHitInfo.RowHandle;
            int targetRow = hitInfo.RowHandle;
            MoveRow(sourceRow, targetRow);
        }
        private void MoveRow(int sourceRow, int targetRow)
        {
            if (sourceRow == targetRow || sourceRow == targetRow + 1)
                return;

            GridView view = gridView1;
            DataRow row1 = view.GetDataRow(targetRow);
            DataRow row2 = view.GetDataRow(targetRow + 1);
            DataRow dragRow = view.GetDataRow(sourceRow);
            decimal val1 = (decimal)row1[OrderFieldName];
            if (row2 == null)
                dragRow[OrderFieldName] = val1 + 1;
            else
            {
                decimal val2 = (decimal)row2[OrderFieldName];
                dragRow[OrderFieldName] = (val1 + val2) / 2;
            }
        }

        }

            Clipboard.SetText(note);

           memoEdit1.Text = null;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        private void simpleButton7_ClickS(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            string[] txt = System.IO.File.ReadAllLines(@"C:\temp\txt.txt");
            List<string> lines = new List<string>();
            string from = "";
            string time = "";
            bool next = false;
            string body = "";
            foreach (string s in txt)
            {
                if (s.Contains("from"))
                {
                    if (s.Contains("704"))
                        from = "Dan:    ";
                    else
                        from = "Darren: ";
                }
                if (s.Contains("t be won without luck"))
                {

                }
                if (s.Contains("time"))
                {
                    time = s.Replace("<time>", "").Replace("</time>", "");
                    DateTime t;
                    if (DateTime.TryParse(time, out t))
                    {
                        time = t.ToString();
                    }
                }
                string line = s.Replace("<body>", "").Replace("</body>", "");
                if (s.Contains("<body>"))
                {
                    next = true;
                }
                if (next)
                    body += line;
                if (s.Contains("</body>"))
                {
                    next = false;
                }



                if ((next && !String.IsNullOrEmpty(body) || !String.IsNullOrEmpty(body)))
                {

                    lines.Add(from + body);
                    body = "";
                    next = false;
                }
            }
            lines.Reverse();
            File.WriteAllLines(@"C:\temp\output.txt", lines);

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            
            
            
        }

        }

        private void simpleButton8_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            string text = memoEdit1.Text;
            List<string> cusips = new List<string>();
            string last_cusip = "";

            bool next = false;
            string start = "********";
            bool has_accrued = false;
            List<string> formatted = new List<string>();
            string header = "CUSIP\tCOF\tCPN\tACCR\tEOM ACCRUED\tMTD P/L";
            formatted.Add(header);
            string COF = "";
            string CPN = "";
            string INT_ACCR = "";
            string EOM_ACCR = "";
            string MTD_PL = "";
            bool done = false;
            bool summary_page = false;
            foreach (string line in text.Split(Environment.NewLine))
            {
                
                if(line.Contains(start))
                {
                    has_accrued = false;
                }
                if(summary_page)
                {
                    if(!line.Contains("NET DIVIDEND/INTEREST INCOME(EXPENSE"))
                        continue;
                    else
                    {
                        summary_page = false;
                        continue;
                    }
                }
                if (line.Contains("ACCOUNT TOTALS - REG"))
                {
                    summary_page = true;
                }
                
                foreach (string s in line.Split('\t'))
                {
                    string local = s;
                    local = local.Trim();

                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    if (local.Contains("COST OF FUNDS")) 
                    {
                        string t = line.Replace("COST OF FUNDS", "|").Trim();
                        t = t.Split('|')[t.Split('|').Length - 1].Trim();
                        foreach(string q in t.Split("  "))
                        {
                            t = t.Replace("  ", " ");
                            t = t.Split(' ')[0];
            
                        }
                        if (t.Contains("-"))
                        {
                            t = t.Replace("-", "");
                            t = t.Insert(0, "-");
                        }
                        COF = t;
                       
                    }

                    if (local.Contains("CPN") && (local.Contains("COST OF FUNDS") || local.Contains("NET"))) 
                    {
                        next = true;
                        string t = line.Replace("CPN", "");
                        if (t.ToCharArray()[19] == (char)32)
                        {

                        }
                        else
                        {
                            t = t.Trim().Split(' ')[0];

                            if (t.Contains("-"))
                            {
                                t = t.Replace("-", "");
                                t = t.Insert(0, "-");
                            }
                            CPN = t;
                            cusips.Add(last_cusip + "\t" + t);
                        }
                    }
                    if (local.Contains("INT ACCRUAL")) 
                    {
                        next = true;
                        string t = line.Replace("INT ACCRUAL", "|").Trim();
                        t = t.Split('|')[1].Trim().Split(' ')[0];
                        if(t.Contains("-"))
                        {
                            t = t.Replace("-", "");
                            t = t.Insert(0, "-");

                        }
                        INT_ACCR = t.Split(' ')[0];
                        
                    }

                    if (local.Contains("ACCRUED")) 
                    {
                        has_accrued = true;
                    }
                    if (local.Contains("INT ACCRUAL") && has_accrued) 
                    {
                        next = true;
                        string t = line.Replace("INT ACCRUAL", "|").Trim();
                        
                        if (t.Split('|')[1].Split('.').Length != 4)
                            continue;
                        string[] hi = t.Split('|')[1].Trim().Split(' ');
                        t = hi[hi.Length - 1];

                        if (t.Contains("-"))
                        {
                            t = t.Replace("-", "");
                            t = t.Insert(0, "-");

                        }
                        EOM_ACCR = t;
                        
                    }
                    if (local.Contains("MTD TOTAL P/L")) 
                    {
                        next = true;
                        string t = line.Replace("MTD TOTAL P/L", "|").Trim();
                        t = t.Split('|')[1].Trim();
                        if (t.Contains("CR"))
                        {
                            t = t.Replace("CR", "");
                            t = t.Insert(0, "-");

                        }
                        MTD_PL = t.Split(' ')[0];



                        
                    }

                    foreach (string cusip in line.Split(' '))
                    {
                        if (UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(cusip))
                        {

                            string l = String.Format("{0}\t{1}\t{2}\t{3}\t{4}\t{5}", last_cusip, COF, CPN, INT_ACCR, EOM_ACCR, MTD_PL);
                            formatted.Add(l);

                            COF = "";
                            CPN = "";
                            INT_ACCR = "";
                            EOM_ACCR = "";
                            MTD_PL = "";

                            last_cusip = cusip;

                            
                            {

                            }
                            

                            
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            string format = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, formatted);
            string txt = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, cusips);
        }

        public class Customer
        {
            public int id { get; set; }
            public string message { get; set; }
        }

        private void simpleButton10_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            DXETA eta = new DXETA(10, null, this.ParentForm);
            _tab.BringToFront();
            for (int i = 0; i != 10; i++)
            {
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(1000);
            }
        }
        static void Changed(object sender, RecordChangedEventArgs<Customer> e)
        {
            var changedEntity = e.Entity;
            Console.WriteLine("DML operation: " + e.ChangeType);
            Console.WriteLine("ID: " + changedEntity.id);
            Console.WriteLine("Message: " + changedEntity.message);
        }

        private void simpleButton11_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            IPAddress[] IPs = Dns.GetHostAddresses(txtSQL.Text);

            Socket s = new Socket(AddressFamily.InterNetwork,
                SocketType.Stream,
                ProtocolType.Tcp);

            Console.WriteLine("Establishing Connection to {0}", txtSQL.Text);
            s.Connect(IPs[0], 8080);
            Console.WriteLine("Connection established");
        }

        private void mainAlertControl_AlertClick(object sender, AlertClickEventArgs e)
        {
            AlertHelper ah = e.Info.Tag as AlertHelper;
            if (null != ah)
            {
                Nullable<int> tab_id = ah.tab_id;
                Nullable<int> respective_id = ah.respective_id;
                if (null != tab_id)
                {
                    this._tab_switcher(tab_id.Value, respective_id);

                }
            }
        }

        {
            AlertControl a = sender as AlertControl;
            e.AlertForm.Size = new System.Drawing.Size(600, 60);
        }

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\FilteringHelper.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public class FilteringHelper
    {
        FilteringUIContext _filter;
        IContainer _components;
        IFilteringUIProvider _container;
        Type _type;
        public FilteringHelper(IContainer components,Type t, IFilteringUIProvider container)
        {
            _components = components;
            _type = t;
            _container = container;
            Reset();
        }
        public void Reset()
        {
            _filter = new FilteringUIContext(_components);
            _filter.ModelType = _type;
            _filter.Control = _container;
           
        }


        public partial class ProductFilter
        {
            const string Main = "Product Filter";

            [Display(Name = "Product")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "product")]
            public string product { get; set; }
        }

            public partial class BWICFilter
        {
            const string Main = "BWIC Filters";

            [Display(Name = "List Type")]
            [FilterLookup(ValueMember = "list_type")]
            public string list_type { get; set; }



            [FilterBooleanChoice(false, EditorType = BooleanUIEditorType.Check, DefaultName = "Show all")]
            [Display(Name = "Only Upcoming")]
            public bool upcoming { get; set; }

            [FilterBooleanChoice(false, EditorType = BooleanUIEditorType.Check)]
            [Display(Name = "Today Only")]
            public bool today { get; set; }
        }

        GridView _gv;
        GridHelper.UpdateFilterDelegate _co;
        public void AssociateWithBWICFilter(GridHelper.UpdateFilterDelegate co )
        {
           
            _co = co;
            _filter.FilterCriteriaChanged += _filter_FilterCriteriaChanged;
            _filter.QueryLookupData += _BWICfilteringUIContext1_QueryLookupData;
        }

  
        public void RetrieveFields()
        {
            _filter.RetrieveFields();
        }
       
        
        private void _filter_FilterCriteriaChanged(object sender, FilterCriteriaChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            _co(_filter.FilterCriteria);
        }

  
        public string FilterCriteria
        {
            get
            {
                if (ReferenceEquals(_filter.FilterCriteria,null))
                    return null;
                return _filter.FilterCriteria.ToString();
            }
        }

        
        
        
        

        public List<string> _filter_list_types = new List<string>();
        public List<string> _filter_accounts;
        private void _BWICfilteringUIContext1_QueryLookupData(object sender, QueryLookupDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "list_type")
            {
                if (null != _filter_list_types)
                    _filter_list_types = _data.GetUniqueList<string>("list_type");
                
                e.Result.DataSource = _filter_list_types;
                
                
                
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "account")
            {
                if (null != _filter_accounts)
                    _filter_accounts = _data.GetUniqueList<string>("account");

                
                {
                    e.Result.DataSource = _filter_accounts;
                }
            }
        }

        DataTable _data;
        public void RefreshBWICFiltersIfNeeded(DataTable data)
        {
            _data = data;
            List<string> filter_fields_local = data.GetUniqueList<string>("list_type");
            
            if (!filter_fields_local.ContainsSameValues<string>(_filter_list_types))
            {
                this._filter_list_types = filter_fields_local;
                
                
                _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
                _filter.RetrieveFields();

                
            }
        }


    }
}


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Forms\frmAddAxe.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Forms
{
    public partial class frmAddAxe : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public frmAddAxe()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        string _server;
        GridHelper _grid;
        BatSignalLib.SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        public void Init(string server,BatSignalLib.SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid = new GridHelper(gridAllTickers, _server, false, _bat_signal);
            mainFilterControl.SourceControl = gridAllTickers;
            
            _grid.ShowGroupPanel(false);
        }

        Query _q;
        public void SetFilter(string filter)
        {
            mainFilterControl.FilterString = filter;
        }
        public void SetPopulateSQL(Query q)
        {
            _q = q;
        }
        IAxeHelper axe_helper;
        public void SetHelper(int product_id)
        {
            if(product_id == 3)
            {
                BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.ctrlAxeCMBSHelper ch = new BatCave.Controls.Axe_Helper.ctrlAxeCMBSHelper();
                grpHelper.Controls.Add(ch);
                axe_helper = ch;
                ch.SetFilterDelegate(UpdateFilter);
                ch.SetFilterDelegateEx(UpdateFilterEx);
                ch.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
                IAxeHelper c = ch;
                if(String.IsNullOrEmpty(mainFilterControl.FilterString))
                    c.ApplyDefaultFilters();
            }
        }

        public void Populate()
        {
            DataTable d = _q.ExecuteTable();
            _grid.SetGrid(d);
        }

        public void UpdateFilter(string column, string filter)
        {
            viewAllTickers.Columns[column].FilterInfo = new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.ColumnFilterInfo(filter);
        }
        public void UpdateFilterEx(string column, CriteriaOperator co)
        {
            viewAllTickers.Columns[column].FilterInfo = new DevExpress.XtraGrid.Columns.ColumnFilterInfo(co);
        }
        private void mainFilterControl_FilterChanged(object sender, FilterChangedEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void mainFilterControl_FilterStringChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _grid.SetActiveFilterStringSafe(mainFilterControl.FilterString);
        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            _grid.ClearAutoFilter();
            if (null != axe_helper)
                axe_helper.StartOver();

        }

        public string FilterString { get { return mainFilterControl.FilterString; } }
        public string SQLString
        {
            get
            {
                return DevExpress.Data.Filtering.CriteriaToWhereClauseHelper.GetMsSqlWhere(mainFilterControl.FilterCriteria);
            }
        }
        public CriteriaOperator Criteria
        {
            get
            {
                return mainFilterControl.FilterCriteria;
            }
        }

        public bool SaveAndExitPressed = false;
        private void btnSave_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            this.SaveAndExitPressed = true;
            this.Close();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Forms\frmColorLegend.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Forms
{
    public partial class frmColorLegend : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public frmColorLegend()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private string _server;
        private GridHelper _grid;
        SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        private void Init(string server,SignalRClient bat_signal)
        {
            _server = server;
            _bat_signal = bat_signal;
            _grid = new GridHelper(grdLegend, _server, true,_bat_signal);
        }

        public void PopulateLegend()
        {
            DataTable colors = BatCaveLib.Color.GetColorLegend(_server);
            _grid.SetGrid(colors);
            grdLegend.MainView().FocusedRowHandle = -1;

            grdLegend.MainView().OptionsSelection.EnableAppearanceFocusedRow = false;
            grdLegend.MainView().UnselectRow(0);
            grdLegend.MainView().OptionsSelection.MultiSelect = true;
            grdLegend.MainView().ClearSelection();
            grdLegend.MainView().Columns["type"].OptionsColumn.AllowFocus = false;
        }

    }
}

    public partial class frmNewBwic : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public frmNewBwic()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }


        public delegate void CloseForm(Nullable<int> f, frmNewBwic frm);

        private CloseForm _closeFrmDele;
        public void Init(string server, CloseForm closeFrmDele)
        {
            _closeFrmDele = closeFrmDele;
            ctrlNewBWIC1.Init(server, CloseFormHere);
        }

        public void CloseFormHere(Nullable<int> ret)
        {
            _closeFrmDele(ret, this);
        }
        public void PopulateData(Nullable<int> bwic_id)
        {
            if (null != bwic_id)
                this.Text = "Managing Existing BWIC";
            ctrlNewBWIC1.PopulateControl(bwic_id);
        }
        private void frmNewBwic_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }
