--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Localizer.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public class MyLocalizer : Localizer
    {
        public override string GetLocalizedString(StringId id)
        {
            switch (id)
            {
                case StringId.XtraMessageBoxYesButtonText:
                    return "SAVE";

                case StringId.XtraMessageBoxOkButtonText:
                    return "My OK Button";

                case StringId.XtraMessageBoxNoButtonText:
                    return "THROW AWAY";

                case StringId.XtraMessageBoxCancelButtonText:
                    return "CANCEL/GO BACK";

                default:
                    return base.GetLocalizedString(id);

            }   
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\mainForm.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    public partial class mainForm : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        string server = CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.DATABASE_SERVER;
        public mainForm()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }


        private Image __img_cache;
        public Image _img_cache
        {
            get
            {
                if (null == __img_cache)
                    __img_cache = Image.FromFile("Images\\bat_small.png");
                return __img_cache;
            }

        } 
        private SignalRClient _bat_signal;
        private string smtp_server;

        
        
        
        

        public void RefreshTab()
        {

        }
        
        private void mainForm_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

            
            {

                
                
                
                    HandleSignalR(this.server);


                smtp_server = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.SMTP_SERVER);

                ctrlBWICs.Init(this.server,_bat_signal);
                ctrlAdvancedReports.Init(this.server);
                ctrlCalendar.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlColor.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                
                   
                ctrlTrash.Init(this.server, _bat_signal, mainTabControl);
                ctrlScratchPad.Init(this.server,this.TabSearcher, _bat_signal);
                ctrlMEMarks.Init(this.server,_bat_signal);
                ctrlAdmin.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlPortfolios.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlAccounts.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlInventory.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlOrders.Init(this.server, _bat_signal, this.smtp_server);
                ctrlEvents1.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlAxeStreamer.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlPnL.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                ctrlNewIssue.Init(this.server, _bat_signal);
                

                
                tabReports.PageVisible = true;
                
                

                

                bool view_trash_tab = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(this.server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Tabs.TRASH_TAB);

                bool view_month_end_marks = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(this.server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Tabs.MONTH_END_MARKS);
                bool view_admin = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(this.server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Tabs.ADMIN_TAB);
                bool view_inventory = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(this.server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Tabs.INVENTORY_TAB);
                bool view_portfolio = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(this.server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Tabs.PORTFOLIO_TAB);
                
                
                
                

         

                bool view_pnl = ((Environment.UserName.ToUpper() == "DFOSTER"));
                bool view_ni = ((Environment.UserName.ToUpper() == "DFOSTER") ||
                                (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("HOLOWATY")) ||
                                (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("KATZ")) ||
                                (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("GLAVIN")) ||
                                (Environment.UserName.ToUpper().Contains("BOLGER")));

   
                
                tabTrash.PageVisible = view_trash_tab;
                tabMEMarks.PageVisible = view_month_end_marks;
                tabAdmin.PageVisible = view_admin;
                tabInventory.PageVisible = view_inventory;
                
                tabPnL.PageVisible = view_pnl;
                tabNewIssue.PageVisible = view_ni;
                
                



                HandleTabOverrides(this.server);

                this.mainTabControl.SelectedPageChanged += new DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.SelectedPageChangedEventHandler(this.mainTabControl_SelectedPageChanged);

                RefreshActiveTab(true,null, null);
                
                ctrlEvents1.SetTabSwitcher(this.TabSearcher);
                ctrlTrash.SetTabSwitcher(this.TabSearcher);
                ctrlOrders.SetTabSwitcher(this.TabSearcher);

                
                

                
                SetRestart(this.server);
                StartBBGAsync();


                bool do_alerts = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<bool>(this.server, 6, false, true);

                if (do_alerts)
                    StartMessageMonitor();


                Database.DBUtils.RecordUsage(this.server, 1,null, null, null,null,true);
                

            }
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public void HandleTabOverrides(string server)
        {
            string tab_overrides = Preferences.GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<string>(server, 8,true);
            if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(tab_overrides))
            {
                foreach (TabNavigationPage t in mainTabControl.Pages)
                {
                    bool should_be_visible = false;
                    bool done_one = false;
                    foreach (string s in tab_overrides.Split(','))
                    {
                        if(s == t.Name)
                            should_be_visible = true;
                        t.PageVisible = should_be_visible;
                        if (!done_one && should_be_visible)
                        {
                            mainTabControl.SelectedPage = t;
                            done_one = true;
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                
                
                
            }
        }
 


        public void StartBBGAsync()
        {
            new Thread(() =>
            {
                Thread.CurrentThread.IsBackground = true;
                
                
                BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance();
            }).Start();
        }
        public void CheckandCreateShortCut()
        {
            try
            {
                bool created = UtilsLib.FileLib.CreateCommonStartMenuIfNotExists(@"\\mhn-fs-01\Shared\Applications\BatCave\BatCave.application", "BatCave", null);
                if (created)
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("You now have a shortcut on your desktop.", "FYI...");
            }catch(Exception n)
            {

            }
        }

        System.Windows.Forms.Timer restart_check = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
        System.Windows.Forms.Timer message_polling = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
        DateTime restart_time;

        public void SetRestart(string server)
        {
            int restart_hours = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_RESTART_HOUR);
            string people = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_NO_RESTART);
            if(people.ToUpper().Contains(System.Security.Principal.WindowsIdentity.GetCurrent().Name.ToUpper()))
                return;

            restart_time = DateTime.Today.AddHours(restart_hours);
            if(restart_time <= DateTime.Now)
                restart_time = DateTime.Today.AddDays(1).AddHours(restart_hours);
            

            restart_check.Tick += Restart_check_Tick;
            restart_check.Interval = 60 * 1000;
            restart_check.Start();
        }

        public void StartMessageMonitor()
        {
            last_event_processed = Database.Common.GetGlobal<DateTime>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.LAST_EVENT);
            int polling_seconds = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.LAST_EVENT_POLLING);
            message_polling.Tick += MessagePollingCheck;
            message_polling.Interval = 1000 * polling_seconds;
            message_polling.Start();
        }

        Nullable<DateTime> last_event_processed = null;
        private void MessagePollingCheck(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            try
            {
                DateTime current_last = Database.Common.GetGlobalNoCache<DateTime>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.LAST_EVENT);
                
                if (current_last > last_event_processed)
                {
                    DataTable latest_list = BatCaveLib.Alerts.GetLatest(this.server, last_event_processed.Value);
                    System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine("Processing Alerts");
                    
                    foreach (DataRow row in latest_list.Rows)
                    {
                        
                        
                        string message = row["alert_summary"].ToString();
                        string caption = row["caption"].ToString();
                        bool priority = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["priority"]);
                        if (!priority)
                            continue;
                        

                        Nullable<int> tab_id = null;
                        Nullable<int> respective_id = null;

                        if (null != row["tab_id"])
                            tab_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["tab_id"]);
                        if (null != row["respective_id"])
                            respective_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["respective_id"]);
                        Nullable<int> product_id = null;
                        string product = "";

                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        


                        
                        
                        
                        string hot_text = null;
                        if (null != tab_id)
                        {
                            string tab = BatCaveLib.Tabs.GetNiceTabName(this.server, tab_id.Value);
                            hot_text = String.Format("Go to {0}", tab);
                        }
                        AlertHelper ah = new AlertHelper(tab_id, respective_id, null, null, hot_text, null, Environment.UserName, false);
                        int seconds_delay = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.ALERT_DELAY);
                        mainAlertControl.AutoFormDelay = seconds_delay * 1000;
                        mainAlertControl.Show(this, caption, message, hot_text, _img_cache, ah);
                        
                    }
                    last_event_processed = current_last;
                }
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n, "Messaging Query Failed", true);
            }
        }

       
        private void Restart_check_Tick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            TimeSpan ts = DateTime.Now - restart_time;
            int total_minutes = (int) ts.TotalMinutes;
            
            if (total_minutes == 0)
            {

                Random rnd = new Random();
                int miliseconds = rnd.Next(1, 120 * 100 * 60); 
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(miliseconds);
                

                string my_username = "US\\" + Environment.UserName.ToUpper();
                bool other_deals = Database.Common.GetGlobal<bool>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_DEAL_TRANCHES);

                List<string> exempts = new List<string>(Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_BBG_EXEMPT).Split(';'));

                if (!exempts.Contains(my_username))
                    Utils.KeepBatcaveUpdatedInternal(this.server, other_deals);


                BatCave.Utils.RestartApp(server);
            }
        }


        public void TabSearcher(int tab_id, Nullable<int> respective_id)
        {
            RefreshActiveTab(true, tab_id, respective_id);
            
        }
        public void TabSwitcherName(string tab_name, Nullable<int> respective_id)
        {
                int i = 0;
                foreach(var v in mainTabControl.Pages)
                {
                    if (v.Name == tab_name)
                        TabSearcher(i,respective_id);
                    i++;
                }

        }

        


        public Nullable<int> GetIndexByTabId(int tab_id)
        {
            string internal_name = BatCaveLib.Tabs.GetInternalTabName(this.server, tab_id);
            int i = 0;
            foreach(var v in mainTabControl.Pages)
            {
                if (v.Name == internal_name)
                    return i;
                i++;
            }
            return null;
        }


        public delegate void RefreshOtherTabDelegate(bool force, Nullable<int> tab_id, Nullable<int> respective_id);
        public void RefreshActiveTab(bool force, Nullable<int> tab_id, Nullable<int> respective_id)
        {
            if(null != tab_id)
            {
                Nullable<int> index = GetIndexByTabId(tab_id.Value);
                
                if (null != index)
                    mainTabControl.SelectedPageIndex = index.Value;
            }
            if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabBWICs)
                ctrlBWICs.RefreshTab(force, respective_id);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabCalendar)
                ctrlCalendar.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabScratchPad)
                ctrlScratchPad.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabMEMarks)
                ctrlMEMarks.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAdmin)
                ctrlAdmin.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabPortfolios)
                ctrlPortfolios.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAccounts)
                ctrlAccounts.RefreshTab(false);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabInventory)
                ctrlInventory.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabOrders)
                ctrlOrders.RefreshTab(respective_id, true);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabReports)
                ctrlAdvancedReports.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAlerts)
                ctrlEvents1.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAlertStreamer)
                ctrlAxeStreamer.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabPnL)
                ctrlPnL.RefreshTab();
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabNewIssue)
                ctrlNewIssue.RefreshTab();
        }


        private void mainTabControl_SelectedPageChanged(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.SelectedPageChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            RefreshActiveTab(false,null,null);
        }

        private void mainForm_KeyUp(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.F5)
            {
                RefreshActiveTab(true, null, null);
            }
            if(e.KeyCode == Keys.Q && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                Utils.RestartApp(this.server);
            }
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.D && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
                BloombergLib.Bloomberg.GetInstance().ClearInMemoryCache();

                XtraMessageBox.Show("Database & BBG Cache Cleared");
            }
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.B && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                BloombergLib.Bloomberg.ClearSession();
            }
        }

        private void mainTabControl_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void mainForm_FormClosing(object sender, FormClosingEventArgs e)
        {
            try
            {
                if (e.CloseReason.Equals(CloseReason.WindowsShutDown))
                {
                    System.Diagnostics.Process p = System.Diagnostics.Process.Start("shutdown", "-a");
                    Database.DBUtils.RecordUsage(this.server, 4,null, null, null,null,true);
                    
                    e.Cancel = true;
                }

            }catch (Exception n)
            {
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);

            }

            if (e.Cancel == false)
            {
                if (null != _bat_signal)
                    _bat_signal.Disconnect();
            }
        }

        private void mainForm_PreviewKeyDown(object sender, PreviewKeyDownEventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void mainAlertControl_AlertClick(object sender, AlertClickEventArgs e)
        {
            AlertHelper ah = e.Info.Tag as AlertHelper;
            if(null != ah)
            {
                Nullable<int> tab_id = ah.tab_id;
                Nullable<int> respective_id = ah.respective_id;
                if(null != tab_id)
                {
                    this.TabSearcher(tab_id.Value, respective_id);
                }
            }

            e.AlertForm.Close();
        }

        private void mainAlertControl_BeforeFormShow(object sender, AlertFormEventArgs e)
        {
            e.AlertForm.Size = new System.Drawing.Size(600, 60);
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\Program.cs ---
namespace BatCave
{
    static class Program
    {
        [STAThread]
        
        static void Main()
        {

            



            NGEN();

            Application.EnableVisualStyles();
            Application.SetCompatibleTextRenderingDefault(false);
            
            if (!Environment.UserName.ToLower().Contains("dfoster"))
            {
                AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += new UnhandledExceptionEventHandler(CurrentDomain_UnhandledException);
            }
            
            BonusSkins.Register();
            SkinManager.EnableFormSkins();
            WindowsFormsSettings.UseDXDialogs = DevExpress.Utils.DefaultBoolean.True;
            
            
            
            
            Application.Run(new mainForm());
        }

        public static void NGEN()
        {
            if (ApplicationDeployment.IsNetworkDeployed && ApplicationDeployment.CurrentDeployment.IsFirstRun)
            {

                string appPath = Application.StartupPath;
                string winPath = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("WINDIR");

                Process proc = new Process();
                System.IO.Directory.SetCurrentDirectory(appPath);

                proc.EnableRaisingEvents = false;
                proc.StartInfo.CreateNoWindow = false;
                proc.StartInfo.WindowStyle = ProcessWindowStyle.Hidden;

                proc.StartInfo.FileName = winPath + @"\Microsoft.NET\Framework\v2.0.50727\ngen.exe";
                proc.StartInfo.Arguments = "uninstall " + Application.ProductName + " /nologo /silent";

                proc.Start();
                proc.WaitForExit();

                proc.StartInfo.FileName = winPath + @"\Microsoft.NET\Framework\v2.0.50727\ngen.exe";
                proc.StartInfo.Arguments = "install " + Application.ProductName + " /nologo /silent";

                proc.Start();
                proc.WaitForExit();

            }
        }
        private static void CurrentDomain_UnhandledException(Object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)
        {
            try
            {
                Exception n = (Exception)e.ExceptionObject;
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Error Report Has Been Sent", "BatCave had an error...", MessageBoxButtons.OK,MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                UtilsLib.Error.SendDefaultError(n);
            }
            catch (Exception n)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Really bad error - Tell Dan", "Oops...");
            }
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\BDHolders.sql ---
select h.ticker,a.bond_label_1,position_date,par_held,par_change,aggregate_position_date
  from 
    HolderAccounts ha
    join Holders h on ha.id = h.holderaccount_id
    left join Assets a on a.ticker = h.ticker
  where
    ha.account_id = @account_id
    order by h.ticker


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\CLOAssets.sql ---
select
top 5  max(ticker) [ticker]
  , deal_name 
  from 
    assets 
    where 
      bond_label_1  = 'CDO/CLO' 
      and collat_type LIKE '%CLO%'
      and deal_name is not null 
	  and oc_unavailable is null
	  and factor > 0
    group by deal_name


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\CoverageSummary.sql ---
select account_id,name,product,CONVERT(BIT,0) [BD_Mapping] into #tmp from vAccountCoverageLong acl where child = 0 and [override] = 0 order by [name],[product]

update t set bd_mapping = 1 from #tmp t join HolderAccounts ha on t.account_id = ha.account_id
select * from #tmp
drop table #tmp


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\FindAssets.sql ---
create table #tickers
(
  ticker varchar(35)
)

select distinct bwd.ticker
  from
    vBWICs b
    join vBWICDetail bwd ON bwd.bwic_id = b.[bwic_id]
    left join vAssets a on a.ticker = bwd.ticker
  where
    b.bid_time > DATEADD(D, -7, GetDate())
    and a.ticker is null
  
drop table #tickers


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\GetBulkAssets.sql ---
SELect 
     a.bond_label_1
  , a.oface/1e6 [oface]
  , a.cface/1E6 [cface]
  , a.ticker
  , a.cusip
  , a.bond_label_2
  
  , n.naic_1
  , a.cce
  , a.detachment [detatch]
  , a.dlq_60p
  , a.rating [m/s/f]
  , a.bval [bval]
  , a.wrap [wrap]
  , a.coupon [cpn]
  , a.wac [wac]
  , a.loan_count [ln_cnt]
  , vPR_3M [3M_CRR]
  , vPR_12M [1Y_CRR]
  , cdr_3m 
  , cdr_12m
  , sev_3m
  , sev_12m
  , shelf
  , convert(bit,case when n.naic_1 is not null then 1 else 0 end) has_naic_1
  , rating_ig
  , vintage

from
  Assets a
  left join NAIC n on a.cusip = n.cusip and n.avr_designation = 'AVR'
where
  market_sector = 'Mtge'

  order by a.ticker


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\GetBWICDetail.sql ---
select item,convert(bit,count(*)) [cover] into #cover from @bwic_ids bi join vBWICs b on b.bwic_id = bi.item join vBWICDetail bwd on bwd.bwic_id = b.bwic_id join Assets a on a.ticker = bwd.ticker join vAccountCoverageLong acl on acl.account_id = b.account_id and a.product_id = acl.product_id and [cover] = 1 group by item


SELect 
  bwd.ID [bwicdetail_id]
  , b.bid_time
  
  , a.bond_label_1
  , bwd.oface/1e6 [oface]
  , (bwd.factor*bwd.oface)/1E6 [cface]
  , a.ticker_nice [ticker]
  , a.cusip
  , bwd.px_talk
  , bwd.results
  , bids.note [bid]
  , bids.account_id [bid_acct]
  , c.color [private_color]
  , bwd.public_color
  , a.bond_label_2
  
  
  , case when n.naic_1 is null then '-' else format(n.naic_1,'0.00') end [naic_1]
  , a.cce
  , a.detachment
  , a.dlq_60p
  , a.rating
  , a.bval
  , a.wrap
  , a.coupon [cpn]
  , a.wac
  , a.loan_count [ln_cnt]
  , vPR_3M [3M_CRR]
  , vPR_12M [1Y_CRR]
  , cdr_3m 
  , cdr_12m
  , sev_3m
  , sev_12m
  , c.color_id [privatecolor_id]
  , bids.bwicdetail_id
  , a.ticker [ticker_bbg]
  , bids.bid_id
  
  , format(b.bid_time,'M/d h:mm tt') + ' - [' + format(b.oface,'0.0') + '/' + format(b.cface,'0.0') + '] - ' + b.list_type + ' - ' + case when b.list_name is null then '' else b.list_name + ' - ' end + case when cvg.cover is null then b.[account_type] else accts.name end [BWIC]
  ,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY b.bid_time,bwd.id asc) [row_sort]
  , a.product_id
  , a.reinvest_end
	, a.mv_oc
	, a.par_oc
	, a.wavg_price
	, a.oc_asOf
	, a.mv_oc
    , a.par_oc
    , a.wavg_price
    , a.oc_asOf
	  , a.wal
    , a.deal_type
    , a.wal
    , a.dlq_90p
    , a.coupon_type
    , a.last_trade_date
    , a.prop_type_1
    , a.prop_type_2
    , a.prop_type_3
    , a.top_10_ln_conc
	, a.collat_type
	, a.cmbs_type
  

from
  vBWICs b
  join vBWICDetail bwd on b.bwic_id = bwd.bwic_id
  left join Assets a on bwd.ticker = a.ticker
  left join NAIC n on a.cusip = n.cusip and n.avr_designation = 'AVR'
  left join vColor c on bwd.id = c.bwicdetail_id and c.[public] = 0 and c.default_colorgroup = 1
  left join vBids bids on bwd.bwicdetail_id = bids.bwicdetail_id
  join @bwic_ids bw on b.bwic_id = bw.item
  left join #cover cvg on cvg.item = b.bwic_id
  join vAccountsUnsafe accts on accts.account_id = b.account_id


  

  
  
  
  
  order by b.bid_time,bwd.id asc
  
  drop table #cover

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\GetMEMarkDetail_DELETE.sql ---
create table #dates
(
  due_date date
)

create table #tickers
(
  ticker varchar(35)
  , [order_id] int identity
)

create table #result
(
  ticker varchar(35)
  , asOf date
  , mark_dbl float
  , mark_raw VARCHAR(35)
)


insert into #dates (due_date) select m2.due_date from MEMarks m1 join MEMarks m2 on m2.account_id = m1.account_id where m1.id = @memark_id and m2.due_date <= m1.due_date

insert into #tickers (ticker) select ticker from MEMarks m join MEMarkDetail mmd on m.id = mmd.memark_id where m.id = @memark_id 

insert into #result select t.ticker,m.asOf,m.mark_dbl,m.mark_raw from #tickers t join Marks m on t.ticker = m.ticker join #dates d on d.due_date = m.asOf







select * from #dates order by due_date desc
select * from #result

drop table #dates
drop table #tickers
drop table #result

--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\TEMP-GetBWICColor.sql ---
select b.id,account_id,bid_time,oface,cface,list_name,indirect,bwd.ticker,a.name
into #bwics
  from BWICs b
  left join BWICDetail bwd on b.id = bwd.bwic_id
  left join vAccounts a on a.id = b.account_id
  where 
    b.bid_time > GetDate()
  order by b.bid_time
  
  
 create table #color
 (
  ticker varchar(35)
  , bid_time datetime
  , oface float
  , cface float
  , color varchar(500)
  , account varchar(40)
  , color_type varchar(40)
 )
 
insert into #color (color_type, oface, cface, account, ticker,bid_time,color) select 'TRADE', b.oface, b.cface, b.name, b.ticker,b.bid_time,convert(varchar(80),convert(decimal(18,3),t.oface/1e6)) + ' to ' + t.master_account+'/'+isnull(t.firm_short_name,'') + ' on ' + format(t.asOf,'M/d/yy') + ' @ ' + convert(varchar(10),t.price) from Trades t join #bwics b on t.ticker = b.ticker
insert into #color (color_type, oface, cface, account, ticker,bid_time,color) select 'PORTFOLIO', b.oface, b.cface, b.name, b.ticker,b.bid_time,a.name + ' as of ' + format(p.asOf,'M/d/yy')  from PortfolioDetail pd join Portfolios p on p.id = pd.portfolio_id join Accounts a on a.id = p.account_id join #bwics b on b.ticker = pd.ticker


select ticker,oface,cface,bid_time [list_time],account [bwic_account],COLOR_TYPE,color from #color
 
drop table #color
drop table #bwics


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\UpcomingCLOs.sql ---
select max(bwd.ticker) [ticker],deal_name,max(bid_time) [bid_time]
  from 
    vBWICS b
    join vBWICDetail bwd on b.bwic_id = bwd.bwic_id
    join Assets a on a.ticker = bWD.ticker
    where
    b.bid_time >= dateadd(wk,-1,GetDate())
    and a.collat_type like '%CLO%'
	and oc_unavailable is null
    group by deal_name
    order by bid_time desc


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\UpcomingCoveredHolders.sql ---
select item,convert(bit,count(*)) [cover],b.account_id,convert(varchar(500),null) [acct] into #cover from @bwic_id bi join vBWICs b on b.bwic_id = bi.item join vBWICDetail bwd on bwd.bwic_id = b.bwic_id join Assets a on a.ticker = bwd.ticker join vAccountCoverageLong acl on acl.account_id = b.account_id and a.product_id = acl.product_id and [cover] = 1 group by item,b.account_id 
update c set acct = case when c.cover = 1 then a.name else at.[type] end from #cover c join vAccounts a on a.account_id = c.account_id join AccountTypes at on at.id = a.accounttype_id


select
     b.bwic_id
    , ass.bond_label_1
    , b.bid_time
    , case when c.acct is null then b.account_type else c.[acct] end [bwic_account]
    , h.ticker
    , h.par_held/1e6 [par_held]
    , h.par_change/1e6 [par_change]
    , h.position_date
    , case when acl.name is not null then acl.[name] else ap.[type] end [holder_account]
    , ha.id
    , ha.account_id
	  , ha.[name] [raw_big_dough]
    , convert(bit,case when acl.[name] is not null then 1 else 0 end) [i_cover]
	into #tmp
    from vBWICs b
    join vBWICDetail bwd on b.bwic_id = bwd.bwic_id
    join Holders h on bwd.ticker = h.ticker
    join HolderAccounts ha ON h.holderaccount_id = ha.id
    join Assets ass on bwd.ticker = ass.ticker
    
   
    left join #cover c on c.item = b.bwic_id and c.cover = 1
    left join vAccountsPublic ap on ha.account_id = ap.account_id
    left join vAccountCoverageLong acl on acl.account_id = ha.account_id and acl.product_id = ass.product_id and c.cover = 1
  
	  join @bwic_id bwid on bwid.item = b.bwic_id

    order by [i_cover] desc,b.bid_time

  select * from #tmp order by [i_cover] desc, bid_time asc
  
drop table #tmp
drop table #cover


--- FILE: BatCave\BatCave\SQL\UpcomingCoveredMatchers.sql ---
select item,convert(bit,count(*)) [cover],b.account_id,convert(varchar(500),null) [acct] into #cover from @bwic_id bi join vBWICs b on b.bwic_id = bi.item join vBWICDetail bwd on bwd.bwic_id = b.bwic_id join Assets a on a.ticker = bwd.ticker join vAccountCoverageLong acl on acl.account_id = b.account_id and a.product_id = acl.product_id and [cover] = 1 group by item,b.account_id 
update c set acct = case when c.cover = 1 then a.name else at.[type] end from #cover c join vAccounts a on a.account_id = c.account_id join AccountTypes at on at.id = a.accounttype_id


SELECT 
  b.bwic_id
  , a.bond_label_1
  , b.bid_time
  , case when c.item is null then b.account_type else c.acct end [bwic_account]
  , bwd.ticker
  , case when acl.account_id is null then ap.[name] else acl.[name] end [matcher_account]
  , convert(bit,case when acl.account_id is null then 0 else 1 end) [i_cover]
  FROM 
    vBWICS b     
      join vBWICDetail bwd on b.bwic_id = bwd.bwic_id
      join vMatchers m on m.ticker = bwd.ticker
      join Assets a on a.ticker = bwd.ticker
      join vAccountsPublic ap on ap.account_id = m.account_id
      join @bwic_id bwid on bwid.item = b.bwic_id
      left join vAccountCoverageLong acl on acl.account_id = m.account_id and acl.product_id = a.product_id
      left join #cover c on c.item = b.bwic_id
    
    order by [i_cover] desc,b.bid_time

drop table #cover

            cusips.Add("31738PBG2");
            cusips.Add("BCC20W6T6");
            cusips.Add("00764MAD9");
            cusips.Add("00764MAK3");
            cusips.Add("00764MAH0");
            cusips.Add("00764MAY3");

            return String.Join(Environment.NewLine, cusips.ToArray());
        }



        public static void RestartApp(string server)
        {
            string location = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_LOCATION);
            
            UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.ERROR_EMAIL, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, null, null);
            m.SendSMTPMail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.ERROR_EMAIL, null, null, "RESTARTED CAVE", null, null, false, true, null);
            System.Diagnostics.Process p = new System.Diagnostics.Process();
            p.StartInfo.FileName = location;

            p.Start();
            p.WaitForExit();
            System.Windows.Forms.Application.Exit();
        }

      


        public static void KeepBatcaveUpdatedInternal(string server, bool include_deal)
        {

            int how_many = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_BBG_UPDATE);

            List<string> assets = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetNeededUpdatedAssets(server, how_many);
            
            
            
            
            
            
            

            string error = "";
            int i = 0;
            List<string> success = new List<string>();
            List<string> fails = new List<string>();
            foreach (string cusip in assets)
            {
                try

                {
                    
                    if (i < how_many)
                    {
                        bool great_success = false;
                        var v = Assets.MT.InsertUpdateIfNeeded(server, cusip, false, true, null, false);
                        great_success = v.updated;
                        if (include_deal)
                        {
                            MT.LoadHelper lh = Assets.MT.EnsureAllTranchesLoaded(server, cusip);
                            i += lh.inserted_bonds;
                        }
                        i++;
                        if (great_success)
                            success.Add(cusip);
                        else
                            fails.Add(cusip);
                    }
                    else
                        break;

                }
                catch (Exception n)
                {
                    error = n.Message;
                    BatCaveLib.Utils.WriteBBGUpdateError(server, cusip, error);
                    if(!fails.Contains(cusip))
                        fails.Add(cusip);
                }
            }
            UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.ERROR_EMAIL, CommonInterfaces.Constants.SMTP_SERVER, null, null);
            

            m.SendSMTPMail(CommonInterfaces.Constants.ERROR_EMAIL, null, null, "Assets Updated: " + success.Count + "/" + how_many, "ERROR: " + error + "\n\nSuccess:\n\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, success) + "\n\nFails:\n\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, fails) + "\n\nTOTAL:\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, assets), null, false, true, null);
        }
    }
}

        {

            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();

        }

        public static DataTable GetAccountsForColor(string server)
        {
            DataTable accounts = null;
            bool special_accounts = BatCaveLib.Permissions.HasCustomPermission(server, BatCaveLib.Permissions.PermissionNames.Permission.ALL_ACCOUNTS_FOR_COLOR);
            if (special_accounts)
            {
                accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountListUnsafe(server);
            }
            else
                accounts = BatCaveLib.Accounts.GetAccountList(server);
            return accounts;
        }

        public static int InsertUpdateNote(string server, int account_id,string note,bool delete, int colorgroup_id, Nullable<int> id,Nullable<int> product_id)
        {
            if (null == id)
                id = -1;
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateNote @note=@note, @account_id=@account_id, @delete=@delete, @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id, @product_id=@product_id, @note_id=@note_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@note_id|OUT", id);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.AddParameter("@delete", delete);
            q.Execute();
            int note_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@note_id"]);
            return note_id;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> CreateIfNoExistAccount(string server, bool create_if_no_exists, string name,Nullable<int> accounttype_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetAccountId @name=@name, @create_if_no_exists=@create_if_no_exists, @accounttype_id = @accounttype_id, @account_id=@account_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@create_if_no_exists", create_if_no_exists);
            q.AddParameter("@accounttype_id", accounttype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            Nullable<int> acct = null;
            if(DBNull.Value != q.Parameters["@account_id"])
                acct = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@account_id"]);
            return acct;
        }

namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class Alerts
    {
       

        public static void InsertAlert(string db_server, int alerttype_id, string caption, string message, Nullable<int> user_id, Nullable<int> tab_id, Nullable<int> respective_id, Nullable<DateTime> asOf)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertAlert @alerttype_id=@alerttype_id, @caption=@caption, @message=@message, @user_id=@user_id, @tab_id=@tab_id, @respective_id=@respective_id, @asOf=@asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, db_server);
            q.AddParameter("@alerttype_id", alerttype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@message", message);
            q.AddParameter("@caption", caption);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.AddParameter("@tab_id", tab_id);
            q.AddParameter("@respective_id", respective_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetLatest(string server,Nullable<DateTime> start_time)
        {
            
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetAlertSummary @starT=@start";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@start", start_time);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static string EventTypeName(string server, int alerttype_id)
        {
            string sql = "select name from AlertTypes e where id = @alerttype_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@alerttype_id", alerttype_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }
        public static DateTime LastEvent(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select convert(smalldatetime,value) [value] from Globals where [key] = 'LAST_EVENT'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<DateTime>();
        }

        public static void ToggleAlertPref(string server, int colortype_id, Nullable<int> user_id, bool enable)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ToggleAlertPref @colortype_id=@colortype_id, @user_id=@user_id, @enable=@enable";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@colortype_id", colortype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.AddParameter("@enable", enable);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static Dictionary<string,int> GetAllAlertActiveTypes(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select name,id from AlertTypes where active = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.GetMultiRowDict<string, int>("name", "id");
        }

        public static Dictionary<int,bool> GetSummary(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAlertPrefs";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            Dictionary<int, bool> results = new Dictionary<int, bool>();
            foreach(DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                int colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["colortype_id"]);
                bool enabled = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["enable"]);
                results.Add(colorgroup_id, enabled);
            }
            return results;
        }
    }
}

namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class Axe
    {

        public static bool SupportsFilter(int product_id)
        {
            List<int> supports = new List<int>(new int[] { 3 });
            return supports.Contains(product_id);
        }

        public static Query GetQuery(string server, int product_id)
        {
            if (product_id == 3)
            {
                string sql = "select bond_label_1, ticker, cmbs_type, issue_type, tranche, vintage, top_10_conc, anchored_retail_pct, houston_pct, gateway_pct, barclays_agg from assets where bond_LabeL_1 = 'CMBS'";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                return q;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static DataTable GetAxeTypes(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [axetype_id], [type] from AxeTypes";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

    }

--- FILE: BatCaveLib\BlastConfigs\ABS.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public partial class BWICBlastConfigs
    {
        public static void ApplyABSBond(ref BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, double? oface, double? cface, string ticker, string cusip, Nullable<double> cce, Nullable<double> dlq60p, string rating_moody, string rating_sp, string naic, string px_talk, string bid, string results, string large_fmt, string larger_fmt, string largest_fmt, string rating_fitch, Nullable<double> mvoc, Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end, Nullable<double> par_attach, Nullable<double> wal_call, Nullable<double> wal, Nullable<double> mvoc_nav, string coupon_formula, string rating_worst, Nullable<DateTime> reinveset_end_kanerai, string cins, string level, string kanerai_dm_str, string size_str, double? kanerai_wal, double? coupon, string tag, string public_note, string ticker_long)
        {
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Curr", cface, GetFaceFormat(null, cface, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cusip);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("C/E", cce, cce <= -10 ? "0" : null);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("60+", dlq60p);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("MDY", rating_moody);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("S&P", rating_sp);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("WAL", wal);
                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Px Talk", px_talk);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Curr", cface, GetFaceFormat(null, cface, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cusip);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bid", bid);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Curr", cface, GetFaceFormat(null, cface, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cusip);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Results", results);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Curr", cface, GetFaceFormat(null, cface, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cusip);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("C/E", cce, cce <= -10 ? "0" : null);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("60+", dlq60p);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("MDY", rating_moody);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("S&P", rating_sp);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("WAL", wal);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Level", level);
            }
            bmh.AppendLineFinalize();
        }


        public static BBGMSGHelper GetABSBlastConfig(BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format)
        {
            BBGMSGHelper bbgmsg = new UtilsLib.BBGMSGHelper();
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0.000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 5, "0.00", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 18, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("C/E", 4, "0.0", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("60+", 4, "0.0", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("MDY", 4, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("S&P", 4, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("WAL", 4, "0.0", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Px Talk", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0.000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 5, "0.00", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 17, "", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", " | ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bid", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0.000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 5, "0.00", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 17, "", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", " | ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Results", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0.000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 5, "0.00", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 18, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("C/E", 4, "0.0", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("60+", 4, "0.0", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("MDY", 4, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("S&P", 4, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("WAL", 4, "0.0", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Level", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }
            return bbgmsg;
        }

    }

        public static BBGMSGHelper GetACMBSBlastConfig(BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format)
        {
            BBGMSGHelper bbgmsg = new UtilsLib.BBGMSGHelper();
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 18, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 11, "0,000", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));              
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 11, "0,000", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));          

                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("WAL",5 , "0.0", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));

                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("PxTalk", 6, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0,000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 17, "", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", " | ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bid", 15, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Cusip", 9, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Bond", 18, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0,000", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Results", 15-1, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("SIZE", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("BOND", 15, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("CUSIP", 9, "", "|", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("TAG", 6, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("LEVEL", 5, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("NOTE", 32, "", " ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT));
                
                
                
                


                bbgmsg.blast_subject = $"BAIRD ACMBS: AXES & ORDERS {DateTime.Today.ToString("MM/dd/yyyy")}";
            }
            return bbgmsg;
        }

        public static void ApplyACMBSBond(ref BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, double? oface, double? cface, string ticker, string cusip, Nullable<double> cce, Nullable<double> dlq60p, string rating_moody, string rating_sp, string naic, string px_talk, string bid, string results, string large_fmt, string larger_fmt, string largest_fmt, string rating_fitch, Nullable<double> mvoc, Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end, Nullable<double> par_attach, Nullable<double> wal_wall, Nullable<double> wal, Nullable<double> mvoc_nav,string coupon_formula, string rating_worst, Nullable<DateTime> reinveset_end_kanerai,string cins, string level, string kanerai_dm_str, string size_str, double? kanerai_wal,double? coupon,string tag, string public_note, string ticker_long)
        {

            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface*1e6);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Curr", cface*1e6);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("WAL", wal);
                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("PxTalk", px_talk);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface*1e6, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bid", bid);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
      
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface*1e6);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("WAL", wal);

                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Results", results);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("SIZE", size_str);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("BOND", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CUSIP", cusip);
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("TAG", tag);
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("LEVEL", level);
                if (null != public_note && public_note.Length > bmh.FindHeader("NOTE").length)
                    public_note = public_note.Substring(0,bmh.FindHeader("NOTE").length);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("NOTE", public_note);
            }


            bmh.AppendLineFinalize();
        }

    }
}

                bbgmsg.AddHeader(new BBGHeaderConfig("Level", 10, "", "", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.CENTER));
            }

        public static void ApplyCDOSIMPLEBond(ref BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, double? oface, double? cface, string ticker, string cusip, Nullable<double> cce, Nullable<double> dlq60p, string rating_moody, string rating_sp, string naic, string px_talk, string bid, string results, string large_fmt, string larger_fmt, string largest_fmt, string rating_fitch, Nullable<double> mvoc, Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end, Nullable<double> par_attach, Nullable<double> wal_wall, Nullable<double> wal, Nullable<double> mvoc_nav, string coupon_formula,string rating_worst, Nullable<DateTime> reinveset_end_kanerai,string cins, string level, string kanerai_dm_str, string size_str, double? kanerai_wal, double? coupon, string tag, string public_note, string ticker_long)
        {

            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);
                
                
                
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("EORP", reinvest_end);
                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Px Talk", px_talk);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bid", bid);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, oface >= 100 ? large_fmt : null);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);

                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Results", results);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);
                
                
                
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("EORP", reinvest_end);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Level", level);
            }

            bmh.AppendLineFinalize();
        }
    }
}

        public static void ApplyCDOBond(ref BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, double? oface, double? cface, string ticker, string cusip, Nullable<double> cce, Nullable<double> dlq60p, string rating_moody, string rating_sp, string naic, string px_talk, string bid, string results, string large_fmt, string larger_fmt, string largest_fmt, string rating_fitch, Nullable<double> mvoc, Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end, Nullable<double> par_attach, Nullable<double> wal_wall, Nullable<double> wal, Nullable<double> mvoc_nav,string coupon_formula, string rating_worst, Nullable<DateTime> reinveset_end_kanerai,string cins, string level, string kanerai_dm_str, string size_str, double? kanerai_wal, double? coupon, string tag, string public_note, string ticker_long)
        {

            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker_long);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("EORP", reinveset_end_kanerai);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("MVOC/NAV", mvoc_nav);
                
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                
                if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                    bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("PxTalk", px_talk);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
            {
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, GetFaceFormat(oface, null, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt));
                
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker_long);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bid", bid);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
            {
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                
                

                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker_long);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Orig", oface, oface >= 100 ? large_fmt : null);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("EORP",reinveset_end_kanerai);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("MVOC/NAV", mvoc_nav);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Results", results);
            }
            if (format == BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Cusip", cins);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("Bond", ticker_long);
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("CPN", coupon_formula);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("EORP", reinveset_end_kanerai);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("MVOC", mvoc);
                
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("RTG", rating_worst);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("BID/OFF", level);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("DM", kanerai_dm_str);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("SIZE", size_str);
                bmh.AppendNonHeaderTxt("WAL", kanerai_wal);
            }


            bmh.AppendLineFinalize();
        }

    }

        public  static string GetFaceFormat(Nullable<double> oface, Nullable<double> cface,string large_fmt,string larger_fmt,string largest_fmt)
        {
            if(null != oface)
            {
                if (oface.Value >= 1000)
                    return largest_fmt;
                if (oface.Value >= 100)
                    return larger_fmt;
                return null;
            }
            if (null != cface)
            {
                if (cface >= 1000)
                    return largest_fmt;
                if (cface.Value >= 100)
                    return larger_fmt;
                return null;
            }
            return null;
        }
