--- FILE: BatCaveLib\BWICBlastConfigs.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public partial class BWICBlastConfigs
    {

        public enum BLAST_TEMPLATE { DEFAULT, CDO_CLO, CDO_CLO_SIMPLE, CMBS, ABS, ACMBS }

        public static BLAST_TEMPLATE GetBlastTemplate(string name)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(name) || name.ContainsIns("default") || name.ContainsIns("NONAGENCY") || name.ContainsIns("SBC"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.DEFAULT;
            if (name.ContainsIns("CDO/CLO-SIMPLE"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO_SIMPLE;
            if (name.ContainsIns("CDO/CLO"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO;
            if (name.ContainsIns("ACMBS"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.ACMBS;
            if (name.ContainsIns("CMBS"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.CMBS;
            if (name.ContainsIns("ABS"))
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.ABS;

            return BLAST_TEMPLATE.DEFAULT;
        }
        public static BLAST_TEMPLATE GetBlastTemplate(Nullable<int> product_id)
        {
            if (null == product_id)
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.DEFAULT;
            
                
            if (product_id.Value == 2)
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO;
            if (product_id.Value == 3)
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.CMBS;
            if (product_id.Value == 4)
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.ABS;
            if (product_id.Value == 8)
                return BLAST_TEMPLATE.ACMBS;
            return BLAST_TEMPLATE.DEFAULT;
        }


        public static BBGMSGHelper GetBlastConfig(BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, BLAST_TEMPLATE bt)
        {
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO)
            {
                return GetCDOBlastConfig(format);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO_SIMPLE)
            {
                return GetCDOSIMPLEBlastConfig(format);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CMBS)
            {
                return GetCMBSBlastConfig(format);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.ABS)
            {
                return GetABSBlastConfig(format);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.ACMBS)
            {
                return GetACMBSBlastConfig(format);
            }
            return GetDefaultBlastConfig(format);
        }


        public static void SetupMessage(ref BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, BLAST_TEMPLATE bt, double? oface, double? cface,string ticker,string cusip,Nullable<double> cce,Nullable<double> dlq60p,string rating_moody,string rating_sp,string naic,string px_talk, string bid,string results, string large_fmt, string larger_fmt, string largest_fmt, string rating_fitch, Nullable<double> mvoc,Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end,Nullable<double> par_attach, Nullable<double> wal_call, Nullable<double> wal, Nullable<double> mvoc_nav, string coupon_formula, string rating_worst, Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end_kanerai, string cins, string level,string kanerai_dm_str, string size_str, double? kanerai_wal, double? coupon, string tag,string public_note,string ticker_long)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(cins))
                cins = cusip;
            if(bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.DEFAULT)
            {
                ApplyDefaultBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt,  rating_fitch,  mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO)
            {
                ApplyCDOBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CDO_CLO_SIMPLE)
            {
                ApplyCDOSIMPLEBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.CMBS)
            {
                ApplyCMBSBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.ABS)
            {
                ApplyABSBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            if (bt == BLAST_TEMPLATE.ACMBS)
            {
                ApplyACMBSBond(ref bmh, format, oface, cface, ticker, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, results, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
        }

        
       
    }
}


--- FILE: BatCaveLib\BWICBlastHelper.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class BWICBlastHelper
    {
        public enum BBG_BLAST_FORMAT { BWIC, BWIC_WITH_TALK, BID, RESULTS, OFFER, NOT_SUPPORTED }
        public enum BBG_MSG_FORMAT { BLAST, CLIPBOARD, IB}
        public static void BlastSelectedBWICS(string server, List<int> ids, BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, List<string> tickers, BBG_MSG_FORMAT blast, bool include_indirects, DataTable all, UtilsLib.BBGDDE _bbg, BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt)
        {

            
            string s = "(" + String.Join(",", ids.ToArray()) + ")";
            string sql = "bwic_id in " + s;
            if (include_indirects == false)
            {
                sql += " and indirect = False";
            }
            DataTable prods = all.Clone();
            DataRow[] rows = all.Select(sql);

            foreach (DataRow row in rows)
                prods.Rows.Add(row.ItemArray);

            if (rows.Length != ids.Count)
            {
                IEnumerable<int> selected = prods.UniqueValues<int>("bwic_id");
                List<int> to_remove = new List<int>();
                foreach (int i in ids)
                {
                    if (!selected.Contains(i))
                    {
                        to_remove.Add(i);
                    }
                }
                foreach (int i in to_remove)
                {
                    ids.Remove(i);
                }
            }

            if (null == tickers && blast == BBG_MSG_FORMAT.IB)
            {
                tickers = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetUniqueBWICTickers(server, ids);
            }
            List<string> lists = new List<string>();
            string product = null;
            if (all.Columns.Contains("list_type"))
            {
                lists = all.ListBasedOnID<string, int>(ids, "bwic_id", "list_type");
                product = prods.GetMaxBasedOnThresholdNullable("list_type", "cface", .70);
            }
            
            if (lists.Count == 1)
            {
                if (lists[0] == "NONAGENCY")
                    product = "NA";
                else
                    product = lists[0];
            }
            string subject = null;
            if (product == "NONAGENCY")
                product = "NA RMBS";
            if (format == BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC || format == BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BWIC_WITH_TALK)
                subject = String.Format("BAIRD {0} BWIC Summary", product);
            if (format == BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.BID)
                subject = "BAIRD Bids";
            if (format == BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.RESULTS)
                subject = "BAIRD Results";

            if (product == "ACMBS")
                subject = "BAIRD ACMBS: ";



            subject = subject.Replace("  ", " ");
            BlastBBGInternal(server, all, subject, ids, format, tickers, blast, _bbg, bt,BLAST_BOND_SOURCE.BWIC);
        }

        public enum BLAST_BOND_SOURCE { BWIC, ORDER }

        public static DataTable GetAllBlastFormats()
        {
            DataTable formats = new DataTable();
            formats.Columns.Add("name");
            formats.Rows.Add("Default");
            formats.Rows.Add("CDO/CLO");
            formats.Rows.Add("CDO/CLO-SIMPLE");
            formats.Rows.Add("CMBS");
            formats.Rows.Add("ABS");
            formats.Rows.Add("ACMBS");

            return formats;
        }

        public static void BlastBBGInternal(string server, DataTable tbl, string subject, List<int> bwic_ids, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, List<string> tickers, BBG_MSG_FORMAT blast, UtilsLib.BBGDDE _bbg, BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt, BLAST_BOND_SOURCE bbs)
        {


            BBGMSGHelper bbgmsg = BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.GetBlastConfig(format,bt);

            if (null != bbgmsg.blast_subject)
            {
                subject = bbgmsg.blast_subject;
            }

            bbgmsg.AddBreak('*');

            if (bbs == BLAST_BOND_SOURCE.BWIC)
            {
                foreach (int i in bwic_ids)
                {
                    DataRow row = tbl.GetSingleRowAny("bwic_id", i.ToString());
                    DateTime bwic_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["bid_time"]);
                    string f = bwic_time.ToString("M/d/yyyy - h:mm tt");
                    bbgmsg.AddLine(f);

                    int bwic_id = i;
                    
                    bbgmsg.AddHeaderLine();
                    DataTable bwd = GetCleanBWICDataTable(server, bwic_id);
                    HandleBWICDetails(server, bbgmsg, format, tickers, bt, bwd);
                    bbgmsg.AddBreak(' ');
                    bbgmsg.AddBreak('*');
                }
            }
            if(bbs == BLAST_BOND_SOURCE.ORDER)
            {

                bbgmsg.AddHeaderLine();
                HandleBWICDetails(server, bbgmsg, format, tickers, bt, tbl);
                bbgmsg.AddBreak(' ');
                bbgmsg.AddBreak('*');
            }
            if (blast == BBG_MSG_FORMAT.BLAST)
            {
                
                _bbg.SendMSGE("", subject, bbgmsg);
            }
            else
            {
                
                string msg = bbgmsg.Message;
                
                if (blast == BBG_MSG_FORMAT.IB)
                {
                    char pad_char = '\u2007';
                    msg = msg.Insert(0, Convert.ToChar(7) + "\n");
                    msg = msg.Replace(' ', pad_char);
                    
                    msg = msg.Replace("********************************************************************************", "**************************************************");
                    if (null != tickers)
                    {
                        foreach (string ticker in tickers)
                        {
                            msg = msg.Replace(ticker.Replace(' ', pad_char), ticker.Replace(pad_char, ' '));
                        }
                    }
                    
                    msg = msg.Replace('|', pad_char);
                    foreach(string s in bbgmsg.exempt_spaces)
                    {
                        string before = s.Replace(' ', pad_char);
                        msg = msg.Replace(before, s);
                    }
                }
                System.Windows.Forms.Clipboard.SetText(msg);

                
                XtraMessageBox.Show("BBG message copied to your clipboard.","FYI");
            }
        }

        public static void HandleBWICDetails(string server, BBGMSGHelper bmh, BWICBlastHelper.BBG_BLAST_FORMAT format, List<string> tickers,BWICBlastConfigs.BLAST_TEMPLATE bt, DataTable bwd)
        {
            


            BBGHeaderConfig o_Orig = new BBGHeaderConfig("Orig", 6, "0.000", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.LEFT);
            BBGHeaderConfig o_Crig = new BBGHeaderConfig("Curr", 5, "0.00", "  ", BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT, BBGHeaderConfig.ALIGNMENT.RIGHT);

            string large_fmt = "0.00";
            string larger_fmt = "0.0";
            string largest_fmt = "0";

            List<string> bonds_no_oface = new List<string>();
            string bwic_time = "";
            if (format != BBG_BLAST_FORMAT.OFFER)
            {
                foreach (DataRow row in bwd.Rows)
                {

                    if (DBNull.Value == row["oface"] || DBNull.Value == row["cface"])
                    {
                        if (bwd.Columns.Contains("bid_time") && DBNull.Value != row["bid_time"])
                            bwic_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["bid_time"]).ToString("M/d h:mm tt");
                        string ticker_short = row["ticker_short"].ToString();
                        if (DBNull.Value == row["ticker_short"])
                            ticker_short = row["ticker"].ToString();
                        bonds_no_oface.Add(ticker_short);
                    }
                }

            }

            if (bonds_no_oface.Count > 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("(no oface/cface/short ticker):  \n\n" + String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds_no_oface.ToArray()), "Error On Blast: " + bwic_time + " - Ignoring.");
                return;
            }

            foreach (DataRow row in bwd.Rows)
            {
                string ticker_short = row["ticker_short"].ToString();
                string ticker_long = row["ticker"].ToString();
                if (null != tickers)
                {
                    if (!tickers.Contains(ticker_long))
                        continue;
                }
                string ticker_nice = row["ticker_nice"].ToString();

                double? oface = null;
                if(DBNull.Value != row["oface"])
                      oface = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["oface"]);
                {
                    
                    oface = oface / 1e6;
                }
                double? cface = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["cface"])
                {
                    cface = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["cface"]);

                    
                    cface = cface / 1e6;
                }

                string cusip = row["cusip"].ToString();

                Nullable<double> mvoc = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["mvoc"])
                    mvoc = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["mvoc"]);

                Nullable<double> cce = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["cce"])
                    cce = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["cce"]);

                Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["reinvest_end"])
                    reinvest_end = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["reinvest_end"]);

                Nullable<DateTime> reinvest_end_kanerai = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["kanerai_reinvest_end"])
                    reinvest_end_kanerai = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["kanerai_reinvest_end"]);

                Nullable<double> par_attach = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["par_attach"])
                    par_attach = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["par_attach"]);

                Nullable<double> wal_call = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["wal_call"])
                    wal_call = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["wal_call"]);

                Nullable<double> mvoc_nav = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["mvoc_nav"])
                    mvoc_nav = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["mvoc_nav"]);

                Nullable<double> wal = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["wal"])
                    wal = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["wal"]);

                Nullable<double> kanerai_wal = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["kanerai_wal"])
                    kanerai_wal = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["kanerai_wal"]);

                Nullable<double> dlq60p = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["dlq_60p"])
                    dlq60p = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["dlq_60p"]);

                Nullable<double> coupon = null;
                if (DBNull.Value != row["coupon"])
                    coupon = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["coupon"]);

                string rating_moody = row["rating_moody"].ToString();
                string rating_sp = row["rating_sp"].ToString();
                string rating_fitch = row["rating_fitch"].ToString();
                string naic = !bwd.Columns.Contains("naic") ? null : row["naic"].ToString();
                string level = !bwd.Columns.Contains("level") ? null : row["level"].ToString();

                string bid = !bwd.Columns.Contains("bid") ? null : row["bid"].ToString();
                string result = !bwd.Columns.Contains("results") ? null : row["results"].ToString();
                string coupon_formula = row["cpn_formula"].ToString();
                string rating_worst = row["rating_worst"].ToString();
                string cins = row["cins"].ToString();
                string tag = !bwd.Columns.Contains("tag") ? null : row.Field<string>("tag");

                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(coupon_formula) && coupon_formula == "0")
                    coupon_formula = "- ";
                if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(naic))
                    naic = "Y";
                else
                    naic = "-";

                string ticker_answer = ticker_short;
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker_answer))
                    ticker_answer = ticker_nice;
                if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ticker_answer))
                {
                    int ticker_length_max = bmh.GetHeader("Bond").length;
                    if (ticker_long.Length >= ticker_length_max)
                        ticker_answer = "";
                    else
                        ticker_answer = ticker_long;
                }

                
                
                
                string kanerai_dm_str = !bwd.Columns.Contains("kanerai_dm") ? null : row.Field<string>("kanerai_dm");
                string size_str = !bwd.Columns.Contains("size") ? null : row.Field<string>("size");
                string px_talk = !bwd.Columns.Contains("px_talk") ? null : row.Field<string>("px_talk");
                if(!bmh.exempt_spaces.Contains(ticker_answer))
                    bmh.exempt_spaces.Add(ticker_answer);
                string public_note = !bwd.Columns.Contains("public") ? null : row["public"].ToString();
                BatCaveLib.BWICBlastConfigs.SetupMessage(ref bmh, format, bt, oface, cface, ticker_answer, cusip, cce, dlq60p, rating_moody, rating_sp, naic, px_talk, bid, result, large_fmt, larger_fmt, largest_fmt, rating_fitch, mvoc, reinvest_end, par_attach, wal_call, wal, mvoc_nav, coupon_formula, rating_worst, reinvest_end_kanerai, cins, level, kanerai_dm_str, size_str, kanerai_wal, coupon, tag, public_note, ticker_long);
            }
            
            

            

            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public static void ProcessTableForIB(DataTable t)
        {
            foreach(DataColumn col in t.Columns)
            {
                int max_len = 0;
                foreach(DataRow row in t.Rows)
                {
                    if(DBNull.Value != row[col])
                    {
                        int local_len = row[col].ToString().Trim().Length;
                        if (local_len > max_len)
                            max_len = local_len;
                    }
                }
                foreach (DataRow row in t.Rows)
                {
                    char pad_char = Char.ConvertFromUtf32(8195)[0];
                    row[col] = row[col].ToString().Trim().PadRight(max_len+1, pad_char);
                }
                   
            }
        }
        public static DataTable GetCleanBWICDataTable(string server, int bwic_id)
        {
            DataTable tbl = BatCaveLib.BWICs.GetBWICDetailTable(server, bwic_id);
            return tbl;
        }


    }
}

        public static List<string> GetUniqueBWICTickers(string server, List<int> bwic_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select distinct ticker from vBWICs b join vBWICDetail bwd on bwd.bwic_id = b.bwic_id join @bwic_ids bb on bb.item = b.bwic_id ";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bwic_ids", bwic_ids);
            var tickers = q.ExecuteList<string>("ticker");
            return tickers;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> GetBWICId(int account_id, DateTime bid_time,bool day_only)
        {
            string sql = "select id from BWICs where account_id = @account_id and bid_time = @bid_time";
            if(day_only)
            {
                sql = "select id from BWICs where account_id = @account_id and cast(bid_time as date) = cast(@bid_time as date)";
            }
            Query q = new Query(sql, CommonInterfaces.Constants.Database.DATABASE_SERVER);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@bid_time", bid_time);
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
            if (DBNull.Value != o && null != o)
                return System.Convert.ToInt32(o);
            return null;
        }
        public static void AddSingleBond(string server,int bwic_id, string ticker,Nullable<double> oface, string px_talk, string results,Nullable<int> bwicdetail_id,Nullable<int> px_talk_kanerai_load_id, Nullable<int> results_kanerai_load_id )

        public static void AddBWICorder(DataTable bwics,string order_column,string summary_column)
        {
            DataColumn col = bwics.Columns.Add(order_column);
            string last_bwic = "";
            int i = 0;
            foreach (DataRow row in bwics.Rows)
            {
                string bwic = row[summary_column].ToString();
                if (bwic != last_bwic)
                    i++;
                row[order_column] = i;
                last_bwic = bwic;
            }
        }
        public static int InsertUpdateBWIC(string server,Nullable<int> bwic_id, DateTime bid_time,Nullable<int> account_id,bool indirect,string list_name,Nullable<int> product_id_override)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateBWIC @bwic_id=@bwic_id ,@bid_time=@bid_time, @account_id=@account_id, @indirect=@indirect, @list_name=@list_name, @product_id_override=@product_id_override, @returnbwic_id=@returnbwic_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@bid_time", bid_time);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@indirect", indirect);
            q.AddParameter("@bwic_id", bwic_id);
            q.AddParameter("@list_name", list_name);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id_override", product_id_override);
            q.AddParameter("@returnbwic_id|OUT", -1);

            q.Execute();
            int returnbwic_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@returnbwic_id"]);
            return returnbwic_id;
        }

        public static Dictionary<int,string> GetColorGroupsDict(string server,bool include_public)
        {
            DataTable table = GetMyColorGroups(server, include_public);
            Dictionary<int, string> retVal = new Dictionary<int, string>();
            foreach(DataRow row in table.Rows)
            {
                int colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["colorgroup_id"]);
                string name = row["name"].ToString();
                retVal.Add(colorgroup_id, name);
            }
            return retVal;
        }

        public static List<int> GetMyColorGroupsIds(string server, bool include_public)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vColorGroups where ([public] = 0 or @public=1) order by [default_colorgroup] desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@public", include_public);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("colorgroup_id");
        }

        public static int InsertColor(string server, string ticker, Nullable<int> colorgroup_id, string color,Nullable<int> account_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertColor @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id, @ticker=@ticker, @color=@color, @account_id=@account_id,@id=@color_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            q.AddParameter("@color", color);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@color_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            
            return 1;
        }

        public static List<string> GetTickersFromWildCard(string server, List<string> bonds)
        {
            List<string> answers = new List<string>();
            foreach(string bond in bonds)
            {
                List<string> tickers = GetTickersFromSingleWildCard(server, bond);
                answers.AddRange(tickers);
                
                
                
                
                
            }
            return answers.Distinct().ToList();
        }

        public static List<string> GetTickersFromSingleWildCard(string server,string partial_bond)
        {
            string sql = "select distinct ticker from Assets where ticker like '" + partial_bond + "'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteList<string>("ticker");
        }


        public static string GetSingleTickerFromDeal(string server, string deal)
        {
            List<string> tickers = GetTickersFromDeal(server, new List<string>(new string[] { deal }));
            if (tickers.Count == 0)
                return null;
            return tickers[0];
        }
        public static List<string> GetAllTickersFromDealAndEnsureAllLoaded(string server,IEnumerable<string> tickers,Nullable<int> max_to_allow)
        {

            List<string> all_tickers = new List<string>();
            List<Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper> list = new List<Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper>();
            int total_inserted = 0;
            foreach (var s in tickers)
            {
                MT.LoadHelper lh = Assets.MT.EnsureAllTranchesLoaded(server, s);
                total_inserted += lh.inserted_bonds;
                List<string> ts = lh.all_tickers;
                foreach (string newt in ts)
                {
                    if (!all_tickers.Contains(newt))
                    {
                        Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper bph = new Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper();
                        bph.ticker = newt;
                        list.Add(bph);
                        all_tickers.Add(newt);
                    }
                }
                if (null != max_to_allow && total_inserted >= max_to_allow)
                    break;
            }
            
            

            return all_tickers;
        }

        public static List<string> GetTickersFromDeal(string server, string deal_name_or_ticker)
        {
            return GetTickersFromDeal(server, new List<string>(new string[] { deal_name_or_ticker }));
        }
        public static List<string> GetTickersFromDeal(string server,List<string> deal_name)
        {
            return MT.GetTickersFromDeal(server, deal_name);
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
        }

        public static DataSet SearchBase(string server, List<string> tickers, List<int> account_ids, bool include_bids, bool include_bwics, bool include_color, bool include_trace, bool include_portfolios, bool include_matchers, bool include_trades, bool run_color_filter, bool include_todays_bwics, bool include_scratchpad, bool include_memarks, bool include_orders,bool include_news, bool include_malls, IEnumerable<int> products, bool include_color_table, bool process_row_colors, bool include_new_issue_px, bool include_offers, bool include_ooc_bids)
        {
            if (null == tickers)
                tickers = new List<string>();
            if (null == account_ids)
                account_ids = new List<int>();
            if (null == products)
                products = new List<int>();

            List<int> color_filter = new List<int>();
            if (include_bids)
                color_filter.Add(2);
            if (include_bwics)
                color_filter.Add(3);
            if (include_trace)
                color_filter.Add(12);
            if (include_portfolios)
                color_filter.Add(4);
            if (include_matchers)
                color_filter.Add(6);
            if (include_trades)
                color_filter.Add(1);
            if (include_scratchpad)
                color_filter.Add(10);
            if (include_memarks)
                color_filter.Add(9);
            if (include_color)
                color_filter.Add(5);
            if (include_news)
                color_filter.Add(15);
            if (include_malls)
                color_filter.Add(16);
            if (include_new_issue_px)
                color_filter.Add(17);
            if (include_offers)
                color_filter.Add(18);
            if (include_ooc_bids)
                color_filter.Add(21);

            
            string sql = "exec dbo.AssetInfo @tickers=@tickers, @accounts=@accounts, @include_bids=@include_bids, @include_bwics=@include_bwics, @include_color=@include_color, @include_trace=@include_trace, @include_portfolios=@include_portfolios, @include_matchers=@include_matchers, @run_color_filter=@run_color_filter, @include_todays_bwics=@include_todays_bwics, @include_trades=@include_trades, @include_scratchpad=@include_scratchpad, @include_memarks=@include_memarks, @include_orders=@include_orders, @include_news=@include_news, @include_malls=@include_malls, @generic_color_filter=@generic_color_filter, @products=@products, @include_color_table=@include_color_table, @process_row_colors=@process_row_colors,@include_new_issue_px=@include_new_issue_px, @include_offers=@include_offers, @include_ooc_bids=@include_ooc_bids";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@tickers", tickers);
            q.AddParameter("@accounts", account_ids);
            q.AddParameter("@include_bids", include_bids);
            q.AddParameter("@include_bwics", include_bwics);
            q.AddParameter("@include_color", include_color);
            q.AddParameter("@include_trace", include_trace);
            q.AddParameter("@include_portfolios", include_portfolios);
            q.AddParameter("@include_matchers", include_matchers);
            q.AddParameter("@run_color_filter", run_color_filter);
            q.AddParameter("@include_todays_bwics", include_todays_bwics);
            q.AddParameter("@include_trades", include_trades);
            q.AddParameter("@include_scratchpad", include_scratchpad);
            q.AddParameter("@include_memarks", include_memarks);
            
            q.AddParameter("@include_orders", include_orders);
            q.AddParameter("@include_news", include_news);
            q.AddParameter("@include_malls", include_malls);
            q.AddParameter("@generic_color_filter", color_filter);
            q.AddParameter("@products", products);
            q.AddParameter("@include_color_table", include_color_table);
            q.AddParameter("@process_row_colors", process_row_colors);
            q.AddParameter("@include_new_issue_px", include_new_issue_px);
            q.AddParameter("@include_offers", include_offers);
            q.AddParameter("@include_ooc_bids", include_ooc_bids);
            
            DataSet t = q.Execute();
            if (t.Tables.Count > 0)
                t.Tables[0].TableName = "Main";

            if (t.Tables.Count > 1 && include_color_table)
                t.Tables[1].TableName = "Color";
            return t;
        }

        public static int InsertUpdateColor(string server, int color_type, string ticker, Nullable<int> colorgroup_id, string color, Nullable<int> account_id,Nullable<int> privatecolor_id,bool delete,Nullable<double> oface, string internal_comment,Nullable<DateTime> asOf,Nullable<double> bwicdetail_id, Nullable<int> analytics_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateColor @color_type=@color_type, @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id, @ticker=@ticker, @color=@color, @account_id=@account_id,@privatecolor_id=@privatecolor_id, @delete=@delete, @oface=@oface, @internal_comment=@internal_comment, @asOf=@asOf, @bwicdetail_id=@bwicdetail_id, @analytics_id=@analytics_id, @id=@color_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@color_type", color_type);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            q.AddParameter("@color", color);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@privatecolor_id", privatecolor_id);
            q.AddParameter("@delete", delete);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@internal_comment", internal_comment);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@bwicdetail_id", bwicdetail_id);
            q.AddParameter("@analytics_id", analytics_id);
            q.AddParameter("@color_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            int new_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@color_id"]);
            return new_id;
        }

        public class SimpleColor
        {
            public Nullable<int> account_id;
            public int colortype_id;
            public int respective_color_id;
            public Nullable<int> colorgroup_id;
            public string color;
            public Nullable<double> oface;
            public Nullable<double> cface;

            public string account_name_unsafe;
            public string colorgroup_name_unsafe;
            public DateTime asOf;
        }

        public static SimpleColor GetSimpleColor(string server, int colortype_id, int respective_color_id,bool delete)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetSpecificColor @colortype_id=@colortype_id, @respective_color_id=@respective_color_id, @delete=@delete";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@colortype_id", colortype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@respective_color_id", respective_color_id);
            q.AddParameter("@delete", delete);
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (null == t || null != t && t.Rows.Count != 1)
                return null;
            DataRow row = t.Rows[0];
            SimpleColor sc = new SimpleColor();
            if(DBNull.Value != row["account_id"])
                sc.account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]);
            sc.colortype_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["colortype_id"]);
            sc.respective_color_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["respective_color_id"]);
            if(DBNull.Value != row["colorgroup_id"])
                sc.colorgroup_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["colorgroup_id"]);

            string account_name = null;
            if (null != row["account_name"] && DBNull.Value != row["account_name"])
                sc.account_name_unsafe = row["account_name"].ToString();
            string colorgroup_name = null;
            if (null != row["colorgroup_name"] && DBNull.Value != row["colorgroup_name"])
                sc.colorgroup_name_unsafe = row["colorgroup_name"].ToString();
            sc.color = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != row["color"])
                sc.color = row["color"].ToString();
            sc.asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["asOf"]);
           
            return sc;
        }

        public static DataSet GetColorSync(string server, List<string> tickers, bool include_todays_bwics, bool color_table, bool include_holders, bool include_trade_history, List<int> accounts, Database.Query.PostAction pa,bool include_portfolios, bool other_registrations,bool apply_account_filter_to_color, bool process_row_colors,bool include_naic_trades,bool include_ooc_bids, bool include_me_marks)
        {
            Query q = GetColorQuery(server, tickers, include_holders, color_table, include_holders, include_trade_history, accounts, include_portfolios, other_registrations, apply_account_filter_to_color, process_row_colors, include_naic_trades, include_ooc_bids, include_me_marks);

        public static Query GetColorQuery(string server, List<string> tickers, bool include_todays_bwics, bool color_table, bool include_holders,bool include_trade_history,List<int> accounts,bool include_portfolios, bool other_registrations,bool apply_account_filter_to_color,bool process_row_colors, bool include_naic_trades, bool include_ooc_bids, bool include_memarks)
        {
            if (null == accounts)
                accounts = new List<int>();

            int tickers_num = 0;
            if (null != tickers)
                tickers_num = tickers.Count;

            int accounts_num = 0;
            if (null != accounts)
                accounts_num = accounts.Count;

            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine("Color Query Kicked Off: " + tickers_num + "/" + accounts_num);
            if(tickers_num == 0 && accounts_num == 0)
            {

            }
            List<int> colorfilter = new List<int>();



            string sql = "exec dbo.[GetColorOnly] @tickers=@tickers, @include_todays_bwics=@include_todays_bwics,@color_table=@color_table, @include_holders=@include_holders, @accounts=@accounts, @include_trade_history=@include_trade_history, @include_portfolios=@include_portfolios, @other_registrations=@other_registrations, @debug=@debug, @apply_account_filter_to_color=@apply_account_filter_to_color,@process_row_colors=@process_row_colors, @include_naic_trades=@include_naic_trades, @include_ooc_bids=@include_ooc_bids,@include_memarks=@include_memarks";
            
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@include_todays_bwics", include_todays_bwics);
            q.AddParameter("@tickers", tickers);
            q.AddParameter("@color_table", color_table);
            q.AddParameter("@include_holders", include_holders);
            q.AddParameter("@accounts", accounts);
            q.AddParameter("@include_trade_history", include_trade_history);
            q.AddParameter("@include_portfolios", include_portfolios);
            q.AddParameter("@other_registrations", other_registrations);
            q.AddParameter("@apply_account_filter_to_color", apply_account_filter_to_color);
            q.AddParameter("@debug", false);
            q.AddParameter("@process_row_colors", process_row_colors);
            q.AddParameter("@include_naic_trades", include_naic_trades);
            q.AddParameter("@include_ooc_bids", include_ooc_bids);
            
            q.AddParameter("@include_memarks", include_memarks);

            List<string> names = new List<string>();
            names.Add("Color");
            if (color_table)
                names.Add("Color Table");
            if (include_holders)
                names.Add("Holders");
            if (include_trade_history)
                names.Add("Trade History");
            if (include_naic_trades)
                names.Add("NAIC Trades");
            q.SetTableNames(names);
           
            return q;
        }

        public static string GetDefaultColorGroup(string server,int? product_id)
        {
            string group = GetDefaultColorGroup<string>(server,"name",product_id);
            if (null == group)
                group = "<JUST ME>"; ;
            return group;
        }

        public static T GetDefaultColorGroup<T>(string server,string retVal,int? product_id)
        {
            
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetDefaultColorGroupId @product_id=@product_id, @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", -1);

            q.UseCache = true;
            string t = q.ExecuteSingle<string>(retVal);
            return (T) System.Convert.ChangeType(t,typeof(T));
        }


        public static int DefautlColorGroupId(string server,int? product_id)
        {
            return GetDefaultColorGroup<int>(server, "colorgroup_id", product_id);
        }

        public static DataSet SearchRaw(string server, string raw_bonds, Form parent_form, bool splash, List<int> account_ids, bool include_bids, bool include_bwics, bool include_color, bool include_trace, bool include_portfolios, bool include_matchers, bool allow_all_cusips, bool include_trades, bool run_color_filter, bool include_todays_bwics, bool deal_search_mode, bool orig_sort, bool include_scratchpad, bool include_memarks, bool include_orders, bool include_news, bool include_malls, List<int> products, bool include_color_table, bool process_row_colors, bool include_new_issue_px, bool include_offers, bool include_ooc_bids)
        {
            DataSet results = null;
            try
            {

                if (splash)
                    SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(parent_form, false, false, null, null);

                List<string> tickers = new List<string>();

                Assets.Assets.BondMatchHelper bonds = new Assets.Assets.BondMatchHelper();
                if (deal_search_mode || (null != raw_bonds && raw_bonds.Contains("%")))
                {
                    List<string> deals = new List<string>();
                    foreach (string s in raw_bonds.Split('\n'))
                    {
                        string raw = s.ToUpper().Trim();
                        if (!deals.Contains(raw) && !String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(raw))
                            deals.Add(raw);
                    }

                    if (raw_bonds.Contains("%"))
                    {
                        tickers = BatCaveLib.Color.GetTickersFromWildCard(server, deals);

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        
                        foreach (string s in deals)
                        {
                            string ticker = BatCaveLib.Color.GetSingleTickerFromDeal(server, s);
                            if (!tickers.Contains(ticker))
                                tickers.Add(ticker);
                        }
                    }
                    foreach (string s in tickers.Distinct())
                    {
                        Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper bph = new Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper();
                        bph.ticker = s;
                        
                        {
                            bonds.AddMatched(bph);
                        }
                    }
                    
                }
                else
                {
                    bonds = Assets.Assets.CleanUpAndUpdate(server, raw_bonds, '\n', true, true);
                }

                if (deal_search_mode)
                {
                    int max_to_insert = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(server, CommonInterfaces.Globals.BATCAVE_MAX_DEAL_INSERT);
                    List<string> all_tickers_from_deal = BatCaveLib.Color.GetAllTickersFromDealAndEnsureAllLoaded(server, bonds.matched_simple, max_to_insert);
                    foreach (string s in all_tickers_from_deal)
                    {
                        var v = new Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper();
                        v.ticker = s;
                        if (!bonds.matched_simple.Contains(s))
                            bonds.AddMatched(v);
                    }
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                }

                Database.DBUtils.RecordUsage(server, 2, bonds.matched_count, null,null,null,true);

                if (bonds.notmatched.Count > 0)
                {
                    if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                        SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
                    string matched = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.notmatched.ToArray());
                    string errors = String.Join(Environment.NewLine, bonds.errors.ToArray());
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("Couldn't match: " + matched + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + errors, "Oops");
                }
                if (!allow_all_cusips && bonds.matched_count == 0)
                {
                    if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                        SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
                    XtraMessageBox.Show("ERROR: No bonds selected");
                    return null;
                }

                results = BatCaveLib.Color.SearchBase(server, bonds.matched_simple, account_ids, include_bids, include_bwics, include_color, include_trace, include_portfolios, include_matchers, include_trades, run_color_filter, include_todays_bwics, include_scratchpad, include_memarks, include_orders, include_news, include_malls, products, include_color_table, process_row_colors, include_new_issue_px, include_offers, include_ooc_bids);

                string color_table = "Main";
                if (null != results && results.Tables.Contains(color_table) && results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("oface") && results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("cface"))
                {
                    foreach (var v in bonds.matched_list)
                    {
                        if (null != v.oface)
                        {
                            string sql = String.Format("ticker = '{0}'", v.ticker);
                            DataRow[] rows = results.Tables[color_table].Select(sql);
                            foreach (DataRow row in rows)
                            {
                                if (!results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Contains("custom_size"))
                                {
                                    DataColumn c = results.Tables[color_table].Columns.Add("custom_size", typeof(bool));
                                    c.DefaultValue = false;
                                }
                                if (DBNull.Value != row["oface"] && DBNull.Value != row["cface"])
                                {
                                    row["custom_size"] = true;
                                    double factor = System.Convert.ToDouble(row["cface"]) / System.Convert.ToDouble(row["oface"]);
                                    row["oface"] = v.oface / 1e6;
                                    row["cface"] = (v.oface * factor) / 1e6;
                                }

                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (orig_sort)
                {
                    if (results.Tables.Count > 0)
                    {
                        results.Tables[0].Columns.Add("row_order", typeof(int));
                        int i = 0;
                        foreach (Assets.Assets.BondParseHelper s in bonds.matched_list)
                        {
                            string search = "ticker";
                            if (UtilsLib.Validate.IsCusip(s.ticker))
                            {
                                search = "cusip";
                            }
                            string sql = String.Format("[{0}] = '{1}'", search, s.ticker);
                            DataRow[] matches = results.Tables[0].Select(sql);
                            foreach (DataRow row in matches)
                            {
                                row["row_order"] = i;
                            }
                            i++;
                        }
                        
                        
                        results.Tables[0].DefaultView.Sort = "row_order asc";
                    }
                }
                
                
                
                
                
                
            }
            finally
            {
                if (splash && null != SplashScreenManager.Default && SplashScreenManager.Default.IsSplashFormVisible)
                    SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
            }
            return results;
        }


    }
}

namespace BatCaveLib

    public class Coverage
    {
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static List<T> GetCoverageAttribute<T>(string server, int account_id, List<int> products,string return_column)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetCoverageAttribute @account_id=@account_id, @products=@products";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@products", products);
            List<T> l = q.ExecuteList<T>(return_column);
            return new List<T>(l.Distinct());
        }
        public static bool HasCoverage(string server, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Coverage where account_id = @account_id and [override] = 0";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return (tbl.Rows.Count > 0);
        }

        public static bool HasProductCoverage(string server, int account_id,int product_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Coverage where account_id = @account_id and [override] = 0 and product_id = @product_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return (tbl.Rows.Count > 0);
        }


        public static List<int> GetRepCodeUsers(string server,string rep_code)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM RepCodeUserMapping rcum join Users u on u.id = rcum.user_id where repcode = @repcode and u.active=1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@repcode", rep_code);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("user_id");
        }

        public static bool AnyParentCoverages(string server, int user_id, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Coverage where [override] = 0 and child = 0 and user_id = @user_id and account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static List<T> GetRepCodeUsers<T>(string server, string repcode,string return_col)
        {
            string sql = "select * from RepCodeUserMapping rcum join Users u on rcum.user_id = u.id and rcum.repcode = @repcode";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@repcode", repcode);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<T>(return_col);
        }

        public static Nullable<int> GetAccountFromSalesMapping(string server, string sf_name)
        {
            Nullable<int> acct_id = Accounts.CreateIfNoExistAccount(server, false, sf_name, null);
            if (null != acct_id)
                return acct_id.Value;

            string sql = "select account_id from SalesForceMapping sfm where salesforce_name = @sf_name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@sf_name", sf_name);
            q.UseCache = true;
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<object>("account_id");
            if (null == o)
                return null;
            return System.Convert.ToInt32(o);
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public static Nullable<int> InsertUpdateCoverage(string server, int user_id, int account_id, int product_id, Nullable<int> coverage_id, string repcode, bool delete)
        {
            string sql = "exec InsertUpdateCoverage @account_id=@account_id, @user_id=@user_id, @product_id=@product_id, @coverage_id=@coverage_id, @delete=@delete, @repcode=@repcode, @id=@new_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.AddParameter("@coverage_id", coverage_id);
            q.AddParameter("@repcode", repcode);
            q.AddParameter("@delete", delete);
            q.AddParameter("@new_id|OUT", -1);
            DataTable retTable = q.ExecuteTable();
            Nullable<int> retVal = coverage_id;
            if(DBNull.Value != q.Parameters["@new_id"])
                retVal = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@new_id"]);
            if (retVal == -1)
                return null;
            return retVal;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, int> GetAllProducts(string server,string which_field)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Products where salesforce_map is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            Dictionary<string,int> p = new Dictionary<string, int>();
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            foreach (DataRow row in t.Rows)
            {
                int id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["id"].ToString());
                string product = row[which_field].ToString();
                p.Add(product,id);
            }
            return p;
        }
    }

--- FILE: BatCaveLib\Forms\VerifyPassword.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib.Forms
{
    public partial class frmVerifyPassword : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraForm
    {
        public frmVerifyPassword()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            
        }
        public bool valid_password = false;
        private void simpleButton1_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            Validate();
        }
        public void Validate()
        {
            string domain = System.Environment.UserDomainName;
            string username = System.Environment.UserName;
            valid_password = UtilsLib.AD.ValidateUserCredentials(domain, username, txtPassword.Text);
            if (!valid_password)
            {
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Wrong Password");
            }
            else
            {
                this.Close();
            }
        }

        private void frmVerifyPassword_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            this.Activate();
            txtPassword.Focus();
            txtPassword.SelectionStart = 0;
            txtPassword.SelectionLength = 0;
            txtPassword.ScrollToCaret();
        }

        private void txtPassword_KeyDown(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            {
                if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Enter)
                {
                    Validate();
                    e.Handled = true;
                    
                }
                if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Escape)
                {
                    this.Close();
                    e.Handled = true;
                    
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BatCaveLib\KaneraiHelper.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public static class KaneraiHelper
    {
        public static Nullable<int> SubmitKaneraiPricingIfNeeded(string server, string cusip,int product_id,string price_string)
        {
            bool kanerai_enabled = BatCaveLib.Products.GetKaneraiProducts(server).Contains(product_id);
            Nullable<int> result =null;
            if (!String.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(price_string))
            {
                double? px = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.PriceTalkToPrice(price_string);
                if (null != px)
                {
                    result = KaneraiLib.DB.QueueKaneraiLoad(server, cusip, DateTime.Today, px, null, price_string, null);
                }
            }

            return result;
        }
    }
}

        public static MEMark GetDetails(string server, int memark_id)
        {
            DataSet set = MarkDataSetDetail(server, memark_id);

            MEMark m = null;
            foreach (DataRow row in set.Tables[3].Rows)
            {
                DateTime due_time = System.Convert.ToDateTime(row["due_date"]);
                int account_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["account_id"]);
                string email_list = row["email_list"].ToString();
                string note = row["note"].ToString();
                List<string> bonds = new List<string>();
                foreach(DataRow b in set.Tables[0].Rows)
                {
                    bonds.Add(b["ticker"].ToString());
                }
                m = new MEMark(memark_id,due_time, account_id, note, bonds, email_list);
            }
            return m;
        }


        public class MEMark
        {
            public Nullable<DateTime> due_time;
            public Nullable<int> account_id;
            public string note;
            public List<string> bonds;
            public string email_list;
            public Nullable<int> memark_id;
            public MEMark(Nullable<int> memark_id, Nullable<DateTime> due_time, Nullable<int> account_id,string note,List<string> bonds, string email_list)
            {
                this.memark_id = memark_id;
                this.due_time = due_time;
                this.account_id = account_id;
                this.note = note;
                this.bonds = bonds;
                this.email_list = email_list;
            }
        }


        public static string GetLastSentEmails(string server,int account_id,bool literally_last)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetLastMEMarkMails @account_id=@account_id, @literally_last=@literally_last";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@literally_last", literally_last);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }

        public static void InsertUpdateMark(string server, string ticker, DateTime asOf,string raw_input,bool clear_completes)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateMark @ticker=@ticker, @asOf=@asOf, @mark_dbl=@mark_dbl, @mark_raw=@mark_raw, @clear_completes=@clear_completes";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@mark_raw", raw_input);
            Nullable<double> tic_dec = null;
            if(null != raw_input)
                tic_dec = UtilsLib.ConvertHelper.TicDec(raw_input);
            q.AddParameter("@mark_dbl", tic_dec);
            q.AddParameter("@clear_completes", clear_completes);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static T GetLastMarkDetail<T>(string server, string ticker,DateTime asOf, bool only_matching_asOf,string ret_val)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetLastMark @ticker=@ticker, @asOf=@asOf, @only_matching_asOf=@only_matching_asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@only_matching_asOf", only_matching_asOf);
            
            
            
            
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(ret_val);
        }

        public static Nullable<double> GetLastMark(string server, string ticker, DateTime asOf, bool only_matching_asOf)
        {
            return GetLastMarkDetail<double?>(server, ticker, asOf, only_matching_asOf, "mark_dbl");
        }
        public static Nullable<int> GetLastMEMarkMarkedBy(string server, string ticker, DateTime asOf, bool only_matching_asOf)
        {
            return GetLastMarkDetail<int>(server, ticker, asOf, only_matching_asOf, "user_id");
        }


        public static List<T> GetAssociatedMEMarks<T>(string server, string ticker, DateTime asOf,bool only_complete,string return_column)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetAssociatedMEMarks @ticker=@ticker, @asOf=@asOf, @only_complete=@only_complete";

            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@only_complete", only_complete);

--- FILE: BatCaveLib\NewIssue.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class NewIssue
    {

        public static DataTable GetSummary(string server)
        {
            string sql =
                "select distinct a.issue_date,a.deal_name,a.bond_label_2,sum(a.oface/1E6) [oface],A.MANAGER,A.ISSUER FROM NewIssue ni join Assets a on a.deal_name = ni.deal_name GROUP BY a.issue_date,a.bond_label_1,a.bond_label_2 , a.deal_name,A.MANAGER,A.ISSUER order by a.issue_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetDetail(string server,string deal_name)
        {
            string sql =
                "select A.ticker,a.cusip,a.tranche,a.oface/1e6 [oface],a.bond_label_2, a.rating_full, a.pricing_speed_orig, a.pricing_wal, a.issue_px, a.issue_spread, a.spread_benchmark, a.issue_yield, mtg_type_long, a.cce, a.detachment FROM Assets a where a.deal_name = @deal_name order by a.detachment  desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@deal_name", deal_name);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static List<string> InsertRMBSNewIssue(string server,DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertNewIssue @asOf=@asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            return q.ExecuteList<string>("cusip", 0);
        }
    }

        public static int InsertUpdateOrder(string server,Nullable<int> order_id, string ticker,Nullable<double> oface, string public_notes, string private_notes, bool live, int colorgroup_id, Nullable<int> account_id, bool publish, string tag, string level, Nullable<int> rating_id, Nullable<int> publish_to, int product_id, string sql_clause, string filter, Nullable<int> result_id,int? axetype_id,string size)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateOrder @order_id=@order_id, @ticker=@ticker, @oface=@oface, @public=@public, @private=@private, @live=@live, @publish=@publish, @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id, @account_id=@account_id, @tag=@tag, @level=@level, @rating_id=@rating_id, @publish_to=@publish_to, @product_id=@product_id, @result_id=@result_id, @sql_clause=@sql_clause, @filter=@filter, @axetype_id=@axetype_id, @size=@size, @id=@newid|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("@order_id", order_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@public", public_notes);
            q.AddParameter("@private", private_notes);
            q.AddParameter("@live", live);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@publish", publish);
            
            q.AddParameter("@tag", tag);
            q.AddParameter("@level", level);
            q.AddParameter("@rating_id", rating_id);
            q.AddParameter("@publish_to", publish_to);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.AddParameter("@result_id", result_id);
            q.AddParameter("@sql_clause", sql_clause);
            q.AddParameter("@filter", filter);
            q.AddParameter("@axetype_id", axetype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@size", size);
            q.AddParameter("@newid|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();

            int id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@newid"]);
            return id;
        }
    }

        {

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            List<int> t = q.ExecuteList<int>("product_id");
            return t;
        }

        public static List<string> GetTradingProductAlerts(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vMyProductPermissions where see_all_color = 1 and hide_top_secret = 0 and show_hidden_trades = 1 and include_stock_accounts = 1 and do_alerts = 1 and product_is_parent = 0";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            List<string> t = q.ExecuteList<string>("product_name");
            return t;
        }




        public static List<int> GetMyBookPermissions(string server)
        {

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            List<int> t = q.ExecuteList<int>("book_id");
            return t;
        }

        public static List<int> GetAxeOnlyAccessProducts(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vMyAxeAccess";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            List<int> t = q.ExecuteList<int>("product_id");
            return t;
        }

        public static List<int> GetInclusiveAxeccessProducts(string server)
        {
            List<int> prods = GetMyProductPermissions(server);
            List<int> axes = GetAxeOnlyAccessProducts(server);
            prods.AddRange(axes.Except(prods));
            prods = prods.Distinct().ToList();
            return prods;

        }

        public static bool HasProductPermissions(string server)
        {
            return ProductPermissions(server).Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static bool HasCustomPermission(string server,string permission)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vCustomPermissions where permission = @permission";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            q.AddParameter("@permission", permission);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return tbl.Rows.Count > 0;
        }

namespace BatCaveLib

    public class Portfolios
    {
        public static DataTable GetPortfolioSummary(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select portfolio_id,account_id,name, sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'NONAGENCY' then 1 else 0 end) [NONAGENCY], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'CMBS' then 1 else 0 end) [CMBS], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'CDO/CLO' then 1 else 0 end) [CDO/CLO], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'ABS' then 1 else 0 end) [ABS], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'CORP' then 1 else 0 end) [CORP], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'MUNI' then 1 else 0 end) [MUNI], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'AGENCY PT' then 1 else 0 end) [AGENCY PT], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'MBS CMO' then 1 else 0 end) [MBS CMO], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'ACMBS' then 1 else 0 end) [ACMBS], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 're-SEC' then 1 else 0 end) [re-SEC],  sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'SBC' then 1 else 0 end) [SBC], sum(case when bond_label_1 = 'GOVT' then 1 else 0 end) [GOVT], sum(case when bond_label_1 not in ('CDO/CLO','CMBS','CORP','ABS','NONAGENCY','MUNI','AGENCY PT','GOVT','SBC','MBS CMO','ACMBS','re-SEC') then 1 else 0 end) [OTHER], count(*) [TOTAL_BONDS], p.portfolio_type,loaded_by_last_name [loaded_by], asOf  from vPortfolios p  group by portfolio_id,account_id,[name],account_id,portfoliotype_id, [PORTFOLIO_TYPE], loaded_by_last_name, asOf order by asOf desc, name desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@portfolio_id", portfolio_id);

        public static bool PortfolioExists(string server, DateTime asOf, int account_id)
        {

        public static DataSet GetPortfolioDetail(string server,int portfolio_id)
        {
            string sql = "select a.bond_label_1,p.ticker,p.oface/1e6 [oface],p.cface /1e6 [cface] from vPortfolios p left join Assets a on a.ticker=p.ticker where portfolio_id = @portfolio_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@portfolio_id", portfolio_id);
            List<string> tickers = q.ExecuteList<string>("ticker");
            if (tickers.Count == 0)
                tickers.Add("-1");
            DataTable sizes = q.ExecuteTable();

            DataSet s = BatCaveLib.Color.SearchBase(server, tickers, null,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false,null,false,false,false,false,false);
            string str = "oface is not null or cface is not null";
            DataRow[] sizes_rows = sizes.Select(str);
            foreach (DataRow row in sizes_rows)
            {
                string ticker = row["ticker"].ToString();
                object oface = row["oface"];
                object cface = row["cface"];
                string query = String.Format("ticker = '{0}'", ticker);
                foreach (DataRow r in s.Tables[0].Select(query))
                {
                    r["oface"] = oface;
                    r["cface"] = cface;
                }
            }
            return s;

        }

        public static DataSet GetPortfolioCompare(string server, int portfolio_id1, int portfolio_id2)

            q.AddParameter("@p2", portfolio_id2);
            return q.Execute();
        }

        public static bool TickerInPortfolio(string server, int portfolio_id, string ticker)
        {
            
            string sql = "select count(*) [count] from PortfolioDetail where portfolio_id = @portfolio_id and ticker=@ticker";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@portfolio_id", portfolio_id);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            int rows = q.ExecuteSingle<int>("count");
            return !(rows == 0);

--- FILE: BatCaveLib\Preferences.cs ---
namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class Preferences
    {
        public static List<T> GetUserPreference<T>(string server, int preference_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vUserPreferences up where up.preference_id = @preference_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@preference_id", preference_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<T>("value");
        }
        public static Nullable<T> GetUserPreferenceSingle<T>(string server, int preference_id,bool allow_cache) where T : struct
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vUserPreferences up where up.preference_id = @preference_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@preference_id", preference_id);
            q.UseCache = allow_cache;
            Nullable<T> t = null;
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<object>("value");
            if (null != o)
                t = (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
            return t;

        }
        public static T GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<T>(string server, int preference_id, bool allow_cache)
        {
            return GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<T>(server, preference_id, allow_cache, default(T));
        }
        public static T GetUserPreferenceSingleNull<T>(string server, int preference_id,bool allow_cache,T default_value)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vUserPreferences up where up.preference_id = @preference_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@preference_id", preference_id);
            q.UseCache = allow_cache;
            
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<object>("value");
            if (null != o)
                return (T)System.Convert.ChangeType(o, typeof(T));
            return default_value;
        }

        public static void SetUserPreference(string server, Nullable<int> user_id, int preference_id, object value)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.SetUserPreference @user_id=@user_id, @preference_id=@preference_id, @value=@value";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.AddParameter("@preference_id", preference_id);
            q.AddParameter("@value", value);
            q.Execute();
        }

    }
}
