        public static List<int> GetPreferredProducts(string server)
        {
            return BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreference<int>(server, 1);
        }

        public static List<string> GetPreferredProductNames(string _server, bool include_unknown)
        {
            List<int> preferred_products = BatCaveLib.Preferences.GetUserPreference<int>(_server, 1);
            List<string> prod_names = new List<string>();

            if (preferred_products.Count > 0)
            {
                foreach (int i in preferred_products)
                {
                    string name = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductName(_server, i);
                    prod_names.Add(name);
                    
                }
            }
            
            if (prod_names.Count != 0 && include_unknown)
            {
                string unk_product = GetProductName(_server, 12);
                if(!prod_names.Contains(unk_product))
                    prod_names.Add(unk_product);
            }
                

            return prod_names;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> GetProductsFast(string server,string name)
        {
            Dictionary<string, int> prods = GetProductDict(server);
            if (prods.ContainsKey(name))
                return prods[name];
            return null;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string,int> GetProductDict(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Products";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            Dictionary<string, int> prods = new Dictionary<string, int>();
            foreach (DataRow row in t.Rows)
            {
                string s = row["name"].ToString();
                int id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["id"].ToString());
                prods.Add(s, id);
            }
            return prods;
        }


        public static List<int> GetKaneraiProducts(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id from Products where kanerai = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<int>("id");
        }
        public static string GetProductName(string server, int id)
        {
            string sql = "select name from Products where id = @id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@id", id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }

        public static int GetProductId(string server, string name)
        {
            string sql = "select id from Products where name = @name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }

        public static string GetOrdersAxeBCC(string server, int product_id) 
        {
            return GetGeneric<string>(server, product_id,"orders_axe_bcc_emails");
        }

        public static T GetGeneric<T>(string server, int product_id, string return_val)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Products where id = @product_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(return_val);
        }

        public static T? GetGenericNullable<T>(string server,int product_id, string return_val) where T : struct
        {
            string sql = "select * from Products where id = @product_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@id", product_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<T>(return_val);
        }

        public static SortedDictionary<string, string> GetAllProductList(string server,bool include_parents,string field_as_value)
        {
            return GetAllProductList(server, include_parents, field_as_value, false);
        }

        public static SortedDictionary<string, string> GetAllProductList(string server, bool include_parents, string field_as_value,bool hide_hidden)
        {
            DataTable products = GetProductList(server, include_parents, hide_hidden);
            return ProcessProducts(products, field_as_value);
        }
        public static SortedDictionary<string, string> ProcessProducts(DataTable tbl,string field)
        {
            SortedDictionary<string, string> products = new SortedDictionary<string, string>();
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                string product = row[field].ToString();
                foreach (string p in product.Split(','))
                {
                    if (!products.ContainsKey(p.Trim()))
                        products.Add(p.Trim(),field);
                }
            }
            return products;
        }


    }
}

        public static int InsertUpdateScratchPad(string server,string ticker,string notes, bool active, Nullable<int> scratch_id,Nullable<double> oface, Nullable<int> scratchpriority_id, Nullable<int> colorgroup_id, Nullable<int> account_id,string tag,string level)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateScratchPad @ticker=@ticker,@notes=@notes,@active=@active,@scratch_id=@scratch_id, @oface=@oface, @scratchpriority_id=@scratchpriority_id, @colorgroup_id=@colorgroup_id, @account_id=@account_id, @tag=@tag, @level=@level, @id=@newid|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker", ticker);
            q.AddParameter("@notes", notes);
            q.AddParameter("@active", active);
            q.AddParameter("@scratch_id", scratch_id);
            q.AddParameter("@scratchpriority_id", scratchpriority_id);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            q.AddParameter("@colorgroup_id", colorgroup_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@tag", tag);
            q.AddParameter("@level", level);
            q.AddParameter("@newid|OUT", -1);

            q.Execute();
            int id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@newid"]);
            return id;
        }

        public static DataTable GetRepCodeUserList(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select ID [user_id],name [name],convert(varchar(30),null) [repcode] from Users union select -r.id [repcode_id],isnull(r.label,sales_cvg_long) [label],repcode from repcodes r WHERE SALES_CVG_LONG IS NOT NULL --ORDER BY R.LABEL DESC,SALES_CVG_LONG ASC -- where repcode = 'LO10'";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable t = q.ExecuteTable();
            return t;
        }

        public static T GetUserDetail<T>(string server,Nullable<int> user_id,string return_val)
        {
            if (null == user_id)
                return default(T);
            string sql = "select * from Users where id = @user_id order by name asc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", user_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(return_val);
        }


        public static T GetMyUserDetail<T>(string server, string return_val)
        {
            int user_id = GetMyCaveUserId(server);
            return GetUserDetail<T>(server, user_id,return_val);
        }

        {
            string sql = "select id from Users u where u.username = SYSTEM_USER";

            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            
        }

        public static List<T> GetRepCodeUsersIds<T>(string server,int repcode_id,string return_val)
        {
            string sql = "select rcm.user_id,r.repcode from Repcodes r join RepcodeUserMapping rcm on rcm.repcode = r.repcode JOIN Users u on u.id = rcm.user_id where r.id = @repcode_id and u.active = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@repcode_id", repcode_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteList<T>(return_val);
            
        }

namespace BatCaveLib
{
    public class Utils
    {
        public static string DefaultFormats(string server, string key, Nullable<int> product_id, string bond_label_2 = null)
        {
            if (null == product_id)
                product_id = 0;
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetDisplayFormat_NEW @key=@key, @product_id=@product_id, @bond_label_2=@bond_label_2";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@key", key);
            q.AddParameter("@product_id", product_id);
            q.AddParameter("@bond_label_2", bond_label_2);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>();
        }



        public static void WriteBBGUpdateError(string server,string ticker_or_cusip,string error_str)
        {
            string sql = "insert into BBGDataFail (cusip_or_ticker,error_str) values (@ticker_or_cusip,@error_str)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ticker_or_cusip<varchar>", ticker_or_cusip);
            q.AddParameter("@error_str", error_str);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static List<string> GetNeededUpdatedAssets(string server, Nullable<int> how_many)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetNextBBGUpdates";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            List<string> assets = q.ExecuteList<string>();
            assets.Shuffle();
            if (null != how_many)
            {
                if (how_many.Value < assets.Count)
                    assets.RemoveRange(how_many.Value, assets.Count - how_many.Value);
            }
            return assets;
        }
     

        
        public static void Test(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Assets";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.Execute();
        }
        public static string GetFormatBasedOnTickers(string server, string key, DataTable tbl, string product_id_column)
        {
            Nullable<int> product_id = GetProductId(tbl, product_id_column);
            string format = DefaultFormats(server, key, product_id);
            return format;
        }


        public static Nullable<int> GetProductId(DataTable tbl, string product_id_column)
        {
            Dictionary<object, int> counts = new Dictionary<object, int>();
            Nullable<int> product_id = null;

            foreach(DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                object o = row[product_id_column];
                Nullable<int> raw = null;

                if (!counts.ContainsKey(o))
                    counts.Add(o,0);

                counts[o]++;
                
                
                
                
                
            }

            object answer = null;
            int max = 0;
            foreach(KeyValuePair<object,int> kvp in counts)
            {
                if (kvp.Value >= max)
                {
                    max = kvp.Value;
                    answer = kvp.Key;
                }
            }
            if (DBNull.Value == answer)
                return null;
            else
                return System.Convert.ToInt32(answer);
        }

    }
}

        private void filteringUIContext1_QueryLookupData(object sender, QueryLookupDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "bond_label_1")
            {
                List<string> bond_label_1 = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_1");
                e.Result.DataSource = bond_label_1;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "bond_label_2")
            {
                List<string> bond_label_2 = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("bond_label_2");
                e.Result.DataSource = bond_label_2;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "shelf")
            {
                List<string> shelf = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("shelf");
                e.Result.DataSource = shelf;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "wrap")
            {
                List<string> wrap = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("wrap");
                e.Result.DataSource = wrap;
            }
            if (e.PropertyPath == "rating_ig")
            {
                List<string> rating_ig = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<string>("rating_ig");
                e.Result.DataSource = rating_ig;
            }

        }

        private void hideContainerBottom_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void _filter_QueryRangeData(object sender, QueryRangeDataEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.PropertyPath == "ln_cnt")
            {
                List<int> list = gridDetail.MainView().GetUniqueList<int>("ln_cnt");
                int min = list.Min();
                int max = list.Max();
                e.Result.Minimum = min;
                e.Result.Maximum = max;
            }
        }

        private void btnResetFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            _filter.ClearFilterCriteria();
            _grid.ClearAutoFilter();
            rdGrpResults.Enabled = false;
            txtBondFilter.EditValue = null;
            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        private bool ExpandedTickerFilter = false;
        private bool ExpandedColorAccountFilter = false;

        private DataSet _filter_ds = null;

        
        private void btnBondFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            rdGrpResults.EditValue = "tickers";
            string raw_bonds = txtBondFilter.Text;
            _filter.ClearFilterCriteria();
            _grid.ClearAutoFilter();
            
            List<int> account_filters = _gh_accounts.GetSelectedRowList<int>("account_id");
           
            
            
            if (!chkUseAccountFilter.Checked)
                account_filters.Clear();

            bool include_bids = (chkColorTypes.Items["bids"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_bwics = (chkColorTypes.Items["bwics"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_portfolios = (chkColorTypes.Items["portfolios"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_color = (chkColorTypes.Items["color"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_trace = (chkColorTypes.Items["trace"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_matchers = (chkColorTypes.Items["matchers"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_trades = (chkColorTypes.Items["trades"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_scratchpad = (chkColorTypes.Items["scratchpad"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_memarks = (chkColorTypes.Items["memarks"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_orders = (chkColorTypes.Items["orders"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_news = (chkColorTypes.Items["news"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_malls = (chkColorTypes.Items["malls"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_new_issue_px = (chkColorTypes.Items["include_new_issue_px"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_offers = (chkColorTypes.Items["offer"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);
            bool include_ooc_bids = (chkColorTypes.Items["ooc_bids"].CheckState == CheckState.Checked);

            List<int> products = ctrlProductFilter.GetSelectedProducts(_server);
            bool include_color_table = true;

            bool anything_selected = (products.Count > 0 || account_filters.Count > 0 || txtBondFilter.Text.Length > 0); 

            if (!anything_selected)
            {
                DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You don't have any accounts/product types/bonds as criteria\n\nYou sure you want to do this search? Will take ~5 min", "Just making sure....",MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
                if (dr != DialogResult.Yes)
                    return;
            }


            DataSet tickers = BatCaveLib.Color.SearchRaw(_server, raw_bonds, this.ParentForm, true, account_filters, include_bids, include_bwics, include_color, include_trace, include_portfolios, include_matchers,true,include_trades,true,true,false,false,include_scratchpad, include_memarks, include_orders, include_news, include_malls,products, include_color_table, true, include_new_issue_px, include_offers, include_ooc_bids);
            _filter_ds = tickers;
            string column_format = BatCaveLib.Utils.GetFormatBasedOnTickers(_server, "big_search", tickers.Tables[0], "product_id");
            _grid.SetGrid(_filter_ds, column_format);
            _grid.ApplyNewColor(tickers, false, null, column_format, false, true, false);
            

            
            rdGrpResults.Enabled = true;
            btnAddColor.Visible = tickers.Tables[0].Rows.Count > 0;
            
            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        private DialogResult ThrowOutFiltered(DataSet set)
        {

            DialogResult dr = XtraMessageBox.Show("You have filtered rows - Throw those way and only show color on the filtered table?\n\n(Recommend: YES)", "Question...", MessageBoxButtons.YesNoCancel);
            if (dr == DialogResult.Yes)
            {
                List<string> tickers = viewSearch.GetFilteredData<string>("ticker");

                DataSet s = _grid._DataSet.Copy();
                s.RemoveRowsNotIn<string>("ticker", tickers);
                string format = _grid.GetVisibleCSVString();
                _grid.SetGrid(s, format);


 
            }
            if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
            {
                return dr;
            }
            return dr;
        }

        {

        }

        private void simpleButton1_Click_1(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            _filter.UpdateMemberBindings();
        }

        private void checkEdit1_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            grdAccounts.Enabled = chkUseAccountFilter.Checked;
            chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Enabled = chkUseAccountFilter.Checked;
            if (!chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Enabled)
            {
                chkApplyAccountFilterColor.Checked = false;
                grdAccounts.MainView().ClearSelection();
                grdAccounts.MainView().ClearColumnsFilter();
            }

        }


        private void dockManager1_StartDocking(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.Docking.DockPanelCancelEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Cancel = true;
        }

        private void rdGrpResults_EditValueChanging(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ChangingEventArgs e)
        {

            HandleToggle(e.NewValue.ToString());
            
            
        }

        public void HandleToggle(string val)
        {
            
            
            if (_grid.AnyRowsFiltered())
            {
                DialogResult dr = ThrowOutFiltered(_grid._DataSet);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
                    return;
            }
            if (null == val || (null != val && val == "tickers"))
            {
                _grid.TwistOrig(null, null);
            }
            else
            {
                _grid.TwistColor(null, null);
            }
        }

        private void btnClear_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            chkColorTypes.UnCheckAll();
        }

        private void btnClearBondFilter_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            txtBondFilter.EditValue = null;
        }

        private void chkColorTypes_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void rdGrpResults_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        private void btnAddColor_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_grid.AnyRowsFiltered())
            {
                DialogResult dr = ThrowOutFiltered(_grid._DataSet);
                if (dr == DialogResult.Cancel)
                    return;
            }
            string current_format = _grid.CurrentColumnVisible;
            SplashScreenManager.ShowDefaultWaitForm(this.ParentForm, false, false, null, null);
            bool toggle = false;
            if (rdGrpResults.EditValue.ToString() != "tickers")
                toggle = true;
            if(toggle)
                _grid.TwistOrig(null, null);
            _grid.AddColorInternal(true, true, null, current_format, true, false, true, null, true, true, false, false, false, true, true, true);
            if (toggle)
                _grid.TwistColor(null, null);
            SplashScreenManager.CloseDefaultWaitForm();
        }


        
        
        
        
        

        
    }

--- FILE: BatCaveControls\ctrlBWICFilter.cs ---
namespace BatCave.Controls
{
    public partial class ctrlBWICFilter : DevExpress.XtraEditors.XtraUserControl
    {
        public ctrlBWICFilter()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        public delegate void UpdateFilterDelegate(DevExpress.Data.Filtering.CriteriaOperator filter);

        private void BWICFilter_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        UpdateFilterDelegate _ufd;
        public void SetFilterUpdate(UpdateFilterDelegate filter)
        {
            _ufd = filter;
        }

        public void NoBorder()
        {
            chkProducts.BorderStyle = BorderStyles.NoBorder;
        }
        public void SetBorder(BorderStyles b)
        {
            chkProducts.BorderStyle = b;
        }

        SortedDictionary<string, string> _products;
        List<string> _preferred_products;
        public void SetPreferred(List<string> products)
        {
            _preferred_products = products;
        }
        public void PopulateBoxes(SortedDictionary<string,string> products)
        {
            _products = products;
            
            
            
            
            
            
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string,string> kvp in products.ToArray())
            {
                if(!chkProducts.Items.Contains(kvp.Key))
                {
                    bool check_mark = false;
                    if (null != _preferred_products && _preferred_products.Contains(kvp.Key))
                        check_mark = true;
                    chkProducts.Items.Add(kvp.Key, check_mark);
                }
                else
                {
                    List<DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem> to_remove = new List<CheckedListBoxItem>();
                    foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem cl in chkProducts.Items)
                    {
                        if(!_products.ContainsKey(cl.Value.ToString()))
                        {
                            to_remove.Add(cl);
                        }
                    }
                    foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem cl in to_remove)
                    {
                        chkProducts.Items.Remove(cl);
                    }

                    

                }
            }
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        public void ToggleCheckVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            chkOnlyUpcoming.Visible = visible;
            chkOnlyToday.Visible = visible;
            chkMyBWICs.Visible = visible;
            chkTomorrowPlus.Visible = visible;
        }
        private void chkProducts_SelectedIndexChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }

        public void Resize(Nullable<int> width, Nullable<int> height)
        {
            int _width = chkProducts.Width;
            int _height = chkProducts.Height;
            if (null != width)
                _width = width.Value;
            if (null != height)
                _height = height.Value;

            chkProducts.Size = new Size(_width, _height);
        }

        public void ToggleHeaderVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            lblProducts.Visible = visible;
        }
        private void chkProducts_ItemCheck(object sender, DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.ItemCheckEventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }
        public void MultiColumn(bool multi)
        {
            chkProducts.MultiColumn = multi;
        }
        public void ToggleLabelVisibility(bool visible)
        {
            lblProducts.Visible = visible;
        }

        public void UnSelectAll()
        {
            chkProducts.UnSelectAll();
        }
        public void HandleFilterChanged()
        {
            string criteria = BuildFilterString();
            CriteriaOperator o = CriteriaOperator.Parse(criteria);
            if (null != _ufd)
            {
                _ufd(o);
            }
        }

        private string _fitler_col;
        public void SetGridFilterField(string field)
        {
            _fitler_col = field;
        }

        public List<int> GetSelectedProducts(string server)
        {
            List<int> products = new List<int>();
            foreach (DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem v in chkProducts.Items)
            {
                if (v.CheckState == CheckState.Checked)
                {
                    Nullable<int> product_id = BatCaveLib.Products.GetProductsFast(server, v.Value.ToString());
                    if(null != product_id)
                        products.Add(product_id.Value);
                }
            }
            return products;
        }

        private string BuildFilterString()
        {
            List<string> sqls = new List<string>();
            List<string> final = new List<string>();
            
            foreach(DevExpress.XtraEditors.Controls.CheckedListBoxItem v in chkProducts.Items)
            {
                if (v.CheckState == CheckState.Checked)
                {
                    string src_field = _products[v.Value.ToString()];
                    if (null != _fitler_col)
                        src_field = _fitler_col;
                    
                    sqls.Add("Contains ([" + src_field + "], '" + v.Value.ToString() + "')");
                    
                }
            }
            string products_sql = String.Join("','", sqls.ToArray());
            
            if (sqls.Count > 0)
            {
                string product_filter = "(" + String.Join(" OR ", sqls.ToArray()) + ")";
                final.Add(product_filter);
            }
            

            
            if(chkOnlyToday.Checked)
            {
                string today_only = "[today] = True";
                final.Add(today_only);
            }
            if (chkOnlyUpcoming.Checked)
            {
                string  today_only = "[upcoming] = True";
                final.Add(today_only);
            }
            if (chkMyBWICs.Checked)
            {
                string my_bwics = "[my_bwic] = True";
                final.Add(my_bwics);
            }
            if(chkTomorrowPlus.Checked)
            {
                string tomorrow_later = "[future_upcoming] = True";
                final.Add(tomorrow_later);
            }
            string final_final = String.Join(" and ", final.ToArray());
            return final_final;
        }

        private void chkOnlyUpcoming_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void chkOnlyToday_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void chkMyBWICs_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }

        private void ctrlTomorrowPlus_CheckedChanged(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            HandleFilterChanged();
        }
    }
}

                    if ((DateTime.Today.Day >= 23) && (DateTime.Today.Day <= 31))
                        UserLookAndFeel.Default.SkinName = "Summer";
                    break;

                    break;

        public void SetFormText(string text)
        {
            if(this.InvokeRequired)
            {
                this.Invoke(new MethodInvoker(() => { SetFormText(text); }));
            }
            else
                this.Text = text;
        }

        private void BarSearchItem_ShownEditor(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.ItemClickEventArgs e)
        {
            var item = (BarEditItem)sender;
            item.Manager.ActiveEditor.KeyDown -= ActiveEditor_KeyDown;
            item.Manager.ActiveEditor.KeyDown += ActiveEditor_KeyDown;
        }

        private bool IsAssetIDHack(string asset_id)
        {
            if (null != ctrlSearch.lookup && null != asset_id)
                return ctrlSearch.lookup.Contains(asset_id.ToUpper().Trim());
            return false;
        }
        private void ActiveEditor_KeyDown(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            var textEdit = sender as TextEdit;
            if (e.KeyCode == System.Windows.Forms.Keys.Enter)
            {
                string search = textEdit.Text.Trim();
                bool is_max_id = MaxLib.Utils.IsMaxId(search);
                if (!is_max_id)
                    is_max_id = IsAssetIDHack(search);
                if (is_max_id)
                {
                    string asset_id = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, search, "asset_id", true);
                    SetActiveHEI(asset_id);
                    return;
                }
                
                string csv_cols = "max_id,effective_date,address_simple,name_simple,phone_number,email,city,state,investment_payment,investment_pct,exchange_rate,unlock_pct,file_num,asset_id";
                DataTable tbl = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllHEIQuickSearch(this.server, csv_cols);
                
               
                textEdit.EditValue = null;
                DXHelper.QuickSearch qs = new DXHelper.QuickSearch();
                qs.SetExecuteDelegateOnSingleItemFilter(true);
                qs.SetPostOpenEvent(PostOpenEventHelper);
                qs.SpawnQuickSearch(this.server, tbl, csv_cols,search, this.Owner, SetActiveHEI, true);
            }
        }

        public void PostOpenEventHelper(GridHelper gh)
        {
            BadgerControls.CustomPopups.GetInstance(gh).RegisterBadgerPopups(SetActiveHEI);
        }
        
        public void HandleToolbarSearch()
        {
            barSearchItem.ShownEditor += BarSearchItem_ShownEditor;
        }

        public void EnableLockedTabs()
        {
            var p = BadgerLib.Permissions.GetAllPermissions(server);
            foreach (var per in p)
            {
                if (per.Name == "Tab")
                {
                    int i = mainTabControl.Pages.GetTabIndex(per.key);
                    mainTabControl.Pages[i].Enabled = true;
                }
            }
        }
        public void ToggleHEITabs(List<string> disabled_by_default_tabs,bool enable)
        {
            foreach (string s in disabled_by_default_tabs)
            {
                int i = mainTabControl.Pages.GetTabIndex(s);
                if(!locked_tabs.Contains(s) || enable == false)
                    mainTabControl.Pages[i].Enabled = enable;
            }
        }
        private void ctrlUserInfo_Load(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {

        }






        private string title_base = "Badger";
        public void SetActiveHEI(string asset_id)
        {
            
            
            
            
            
            active_hei = asset_id;
            if (!active_hea.LoadAsset(asset_id))
            {
                MessageBox.Show( "Unable to find Asset Details","Badger Asset Loading:");
                return;
            }

            
            string nice_name = active_hea.GetAssetNiceName();
            this.Text = $"{title_base} - {nice_name}";
            ToggleHEITabs(disabled_by_default_tabs, true);
            string default_tab = (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabSearch) ? Constants.TabNames.AssetInfo : null;
            RefreshActiveTab(default_tab, true);
            barButtonItem2.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            barButtonItem3.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            btnOpenFSEA.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            barBtnAddNote.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            btnFileWorksheet.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            btnCopy.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            btnExecutedFolder.Enabled = null != asset_id;
            btnMax.Enabled = null != asset_id;

        }

        public Nullable<int> GetIndexByTabName(string name)
        {

            int i = 0;
            foreach (var v in mainTabControl.Pages)
            {
                if (v.Name == name)
                    return i;
                i++;
            }
            return null;
        }

        private string active_hei = null;
        private HEA active_hea = new HEA();

        public void RefreshActiveTab(string tabName,bool force)
        {
            if (null != tabName)
            {
                int? id = GetIndexByTabName(tabName);
                if (null != id)
                    mainTabControl.SelectedPageIndex = id.Value;
            }

            if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAdmin)
                ctrlAdmin.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabInfo)
                ctrlUserInfo.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabSearch)
                ctrlSearch.RefreshTab(active_hei,force );
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabTasks)
                ctrlTasks.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabDocs)
                ctrlDocs.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabPropertyValues)
                ctrlPropertyValues.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabInsurance)
                ctrlInsurance.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabMortgage)
                ctrlMortgage.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabCredit)
                ctrlCredit.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabSettlement)
                ctrlSettlement.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabSurveillance)
                ctrlSurveillance.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabTrash)
                ctrlTrash.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabDocCustodian)
                ctrlDocCustodian.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabAssetAdmin)
                ctrlAssetAdmin.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabPipeline)
                ctrlPipeline.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabTrades)
                ctrlTrades.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabBanking)
                ctrlBanking.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabUnderwriting)
                ctrlUnderwriting.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabServicing)
                ctrlServicing.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            
            
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabDefaults)
                ctrlDefaults.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabExpenses)
                ctrlExpenses.RefreshTab(active_hei);
            else if (mainTabControl.SelectedPage == tabBadgerTime)
                ctrlBadgerTime.RefreshTab(active_hei);
        }
        private void mainForm_KeyUp(object sender, KeyEventArgs e)
        {
            if (e.KeyCode == Keys.F5)
            {
                RefreshActiveTab(null,true);
            }
            else if (e.KeyCode == Keys.F && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                
                barSearchItem.Links[0].Focus();
                (barSearchItem.Links[0] as DevExpress.XtraBars.BarEditItemLink).EditValue = null;
                (barSearchItem.Links[0] as DevExpress.XtraBars.BarEditItemLink).ShowEditor();
            }
            else if (e.KeyCode == Keys.Q && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                
            }
            else if (e.KeyCode == Keys.D && Control.ModifierKeys == Keys.Control)
            {
                Database.DBCache.GetInstance().Pool.Clear();
                Fields.GetInstance(this.server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal).ClearCache();
                XtraMessageBox.Show("Database Cache Cleared");
            }
}


        private void mainTabControl_SelectedPageChanging(object sender, DevExpress.XtraBars.Navigation.SelectedPageChangingEventArgs e)
        {
            e.Cancel = (!e.Page.Enabled);
        }

        DateTime restart_time;
        public void SetRestart(string server)
        {
            int restart_hours = Database.Common.GetGlobal<int>(this.server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BADGER_RESTART_HOUR,true);

            restart_time = DateTime.Today.AddHours(restart_hours);
            restart_time = DateTime.Today.SetTime(10, 30);
            if (restart_time <= DateTime.Now)
                restart_time = DateTime.Today.AddDays(1).AddHours(restart_hours);


            restart_check.Tick += Restart_check_Tick;
            restart_check.Interval = 60 * 1000;
            restart_check.Start();
        }
        System.Windows.Forms.Timer restart_check = new System.Windows.Forms.Timer();
        private void Restart_check_Tick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            
            TimeSpan ts = DateTime.Now - restart_time;
            int total_minutes = (int)ts.TotalMinutes;
            
            if (total_minutes == 0)
            {

                Random rnd = new Random();
                int miliseconds = rnd.Next(1, 120 * 100 * 60); 
                System.Threading.Thread.Sleep(miliseconds);


                

                
                
            }
        }

    }
